href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　居乡，与程瑀唱和。作品：伯宇知府给事宠和子贱与仆域字韵诗，格力超绝，辄复次韵。<div id='poem_527570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伯宇知府给事宠和子贱与仆域字韵诗格力超绝辄复次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527570")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527570'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527570'>中原困干戈，衣冠沦异域。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527570'>忠臣愤切骨，义士血空滴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527570'>平生忧国心，岂以死生易。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527570'>年来返田庐，门巷无辙迹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527570'>老骥万里心，垂耳卧空枥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527570'>素交今几人，十载劳梦役。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527570'>宣城拥朱轓，潘子缚禅寂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527570'>屹然障颓波，我亦心匪石。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527570'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527570_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='39954e3e6c2e4b998477001178e700aa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("39954e3e6c2e4b998477001178e700aa");'><span id='39954e3e6c2e4b998477001178e700aa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1135')">1132-1135年</a>，55-58岁</div><div id='39954e3e6c2e4b998477001178e700aa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞。冬，与律师通公游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，为陈师锡《闲乐奏议》作序。作品：闲乐先生奏议序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1221162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>閒乐先生奏议序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221162")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221162'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221162'>议官御史，专以犯颜婴鳞、排击奸邪为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221162_comment'></div>若论而不切，则不能起人主之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221162_comment'></div>辨之不早，则不能折祸乱之萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221162_comment'></div>建中靖国初，太上皇新即大位，号召天下名贤，聚之朝廷，自执政大臣下逮台阁之士，皆极一时之选，故殿中侍御史陈公伯修其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221162_comment'></div>是时蔡京方为翰林学士承旨，虽明智之士，未能知其必乱天下也，公独慨然论奏，条其过恶，章凡四五上而不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221162_comment'></div>且曰：「若果用京，则治乱自此分，祖宗基业自此隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221162_comment'></div>臣非自爱而忧之，盖为陛下忧，为社稷忧，为天下贤人君子忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221162_comment'></div>未几京遂为执政，尽逐异己者，固宠市权，荧惑主听，握国柄者几三十年，谏争之路自此塞绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221162_comment'></div>卒之强敌肆虐，生民涂炭，公之言始效，于此可不谓先见之明乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221162_comment'></div>司马温公志吕献可墓，称其论列王安石于海内归重之时，人主信任之际，以谓明达先识，己所不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221162_comment'></div>若伯修可谓无愧于斯人矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221162_comment'></div>某尝恨今世士大夫徒知称诵陈莹中，而知公者尚鲜，岂非造膝之言，秘不敢传乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221162_comment'></div>古人之称「死而不朽」者，如臧文仲既殁，其言立是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221162_comment'></div>韩退之作《谏臣论》曰：「入则谏其君，出不使人知之者，大臣宰相之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221162_comment'></div>若官以谏为名，宜有以奉其职，使四方后代知朝廷有直言骨鲠之臣，顾不美欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221162_comment'></div>公既殁，其子某乃集录平生遗藁，得奏议十有五篇，以书抵武林张子韶，求予序冠其首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221162_comment'></div>子韶曰：「伯修立志如此，一陷党籍，至老且死，终不用，凡有志于斯道者，孰不恻然」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221162_comment'></div>某虽生晚，幸及识公于三衢，引接诲诱，待以国士，今二十一年矣，追惟平昔，因泫然而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221162_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221162_comment'></div>君子小人不两进，邪谄得君则正士危，理势自然，无足深慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221162_comment'></div>公虽流离窜斥，终身抱不遇之叹，于今望之，凛凛尚有生气，而彼纷纷者果安在哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221162_comment'></div>览是书者亦可为持禄养交、择利畏祸者之戒云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221162_comment'></div>绍兴三年八月二十日，上虞李某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1221162_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，李纲与李光书论君子小人进退之理。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，向黄与善借黄庭坚集，感而成诗。作品：与善借示鲁直集，雕刻虽精而非老眼所便，戏成小诗还之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_527950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与善借示鲁直集雕刻虽精而非老眼所便戏成小诗还之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527950")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527950'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527950'>墙角年来弃短檠，捐书默坐眼方明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527950'>知君欲嗣江西派，净几明窗付后生<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527950'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527950'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527950_0'>⑴ 自注：近日吕居仁舍人作《江西宗派序》，以鲁直为宗主也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527950_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，仲秋，水盛涨，有诗与诸兄弟交游唱和。作品：甲寅仲秋水涨，独民先兄、元发弟徙居招提，日有登览棋酒之胜，连日雨复大作，水且洊至，举室几于湿浸，仰二公之旷逹，叹辎重之为累。辄成鄙句以寄，并呈志尹、宣教表兄洎往来诸友兄一笑。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span>和孚先兄久雨。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_527709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲寅仲秋水涨独民先兄元发弟徙居招提日有登览棋酒之胜连日雨复大作水且荐至举室几于湿浸仰二公之旷达叹辎重之为累辄成鄙句以寄并呈志尹宣教表兄洎往来诸友兄一笑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527709")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527709'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527709'>活计从来祗旋营，急难方悟此生轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527709'>资身但有书盈腹，润屋不将金满籯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527709'>尘榻晓寒资酒力，空阶夜雨杂棋声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527709'>茗瓯时赴汤休约，肯念人间雨与晴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527709'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527709_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和孚先兄久雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527708")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527708'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527708'>未容春色到园林，寂寞莺花困久阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527708'>积潦坏墙低易补，晓寒侵被破难禁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527708'>门闲剩欲偿诗债，裘敝犹堪当酒金。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527708'>昨夜东风扫群翳，放回天地发生心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527708'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，喜晴，有诗。作品：喜晴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_527710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜晴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527710")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527710'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527710'>西风一夜卷层波，并落人声喜气多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527710'>巨浸涨天吞梦泽，空庭积水湛星河。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527710'>光摇万瓦疑浮动，翠飐群山巧琢磨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527710'>从此江湖更清旷，肯将轩冕换渔蓑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527710'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，有诗次韵孚先兄，时韩世忠败金人于淮北承州。作品：孚先兄以连雨形于咏歌，是时适闻韩侯淮北之捷因次韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_527706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孚先兄以连雨形于咏歌是时适闻韩侯淮北之捷因次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527706")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527706'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527706'>颓垣败屋未须悲，淮北于今暗铁衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527706'>背水汉营朝气锐，青冈敌骑夜声微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527706'>萧条里巷徵符急，浩渺江湖羽檄稀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527706'>不及戎行亲矢石，独将诗礼继庭闱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527706'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，闻韩世忠败金人于承州，李光喜作诗。作品：伏睹亲征榜，又闻韩侯过江北，是皆可喜，然小臣区区，亦有不胜忧者。辄次韵成鄙句，呈子骏侍郎。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_527707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伏睹亲征榜又闻韩侯过江北是皆可喜然小臣区区亦有不胜忧者辄次韵成鄙句呈子骏侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527707")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527707'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527707'>亲征一纸诏书颁，顿觉中原气象还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527707'>漫说风沙临瀚海，遥怜草木旧淮山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527707'>百年社稷倾危后，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_527707", 527707, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>一掷乾坤</span>胜负间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527707'>北望銮舆心共折，小臣无路得追攀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527707'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，李纲有诗寄李光。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　宫祀居乡上虞，期间，有诗。作品：予自入夏多徜徉逃暑，中秋后乍凉，杜门却扫，求古圣贤于残编断简中，渐觉有味，喜而成诗（小窗秋半日晖晖）<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_527722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>不出示邻士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527722")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527722'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527722'>小窗秋半日晖晖，蠹简陈编渐可窥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527722'>晨起已空摩诘室，晚凉深下董生帷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527722'>参差红影蕉临水，散漫寒香菊绕篱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527722'>从此杖藜休引步，习池花草任离披。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527722'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527722_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月2日</a>　在上虞。复宝文阁待制，知湖州。作品：辞免知湖州状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1221006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免知湖州状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221006")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221006'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221006'>降授左奉议郎、新除宝文阁待制、知湖州臣李某奏：准尚书省劄子，「三省、枢密院同奉圣旨，李某复宝文阁待制、知湖州，不候受告，不许辞免，限指挥到，日下起发前去之任」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221006_comment'></div>臣闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221006_comment'></div>伏念臣本以庸愚，久叨任使，夤缘奖拔，浸至超踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221006_comment'></div>罪衅横生，谤讟荐至，衔冤唶舌，不敢自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221006_comment'></div>伏自投閒以来，已踰两稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221006_comment'></div>方强敌凭陵，陛下亲御戎衣之际，而臣名在丹书，屏伏田里，既不能吐一奇策，仰裨庙算，又不获身当矢石，以备戎行，无路请缨，徒深忧愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221006_comment'></div>今敌既退遁，朝廷清明，固宜搜访草莱，延登英杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221006_comment'></div>如臣志气凋落，已试罔功，华阁清资，既难轻受，名邦辅郡，岂敢冒居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221006_comment'></div>伏望圣慈俯察忱辞，特收涣汗，再除臣宫观一次，以养衰残，庶息多言，少安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221006_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1221006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月</a>　在上虞，通公律师至上虞为李光饯行，请李光书《舍黄蘖裴公真像》作品：舍黄蘖裴公真像并偈。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1221178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舍黄蘖裴公真像<span class='inlineComment2'>（并偈）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221178")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221178'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221178'>宣州广教禅寺，实唐裴公故宅、黄蘖道场，二公像设存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221178_comment'></div>气韵森严，笔法简古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221178_comment'></div>予守郡日，命工摹得之，顾私家不能严净，适通公律师访予五松山，一见若有宿契，因请留寘铁磬堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221178_comment'></div>或曰：「静凝学徒皆宗律教，以南山为祖师，得无异议乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221178_comment'></div>予曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221178_comment'></div>禅、律二宗，本相因依，后学末师，妄自分别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221178_comment'></div>昔宽禅师谓白乐天曰：『无上菩提者，被于身为律，说于口为法，得于心为禅，应用者三，其致一也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221178_comment'></div>故如来所说大乘诸经，以文殊为问答之首者，皆明法身妙慧之门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221178_comment'></div>以普贤为问荅之首者，皆明妙智之万行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221178_comment'></div>诸佛菩萨皆依此二尊者以为师范，然后成菩萨之极果，处如来之上乘，岂有二哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221178_comment'></div>通公志行苦卓，识趣超然，禅、律并行，不相留碍，其必有得于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221178_comment'></div>恐诸衲子尚有疑情，对大众前复说偈曰：君看铁磬堂前像，恰似文殊对普贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221178_comment'></div>更着白须裴老子，夜深同听祖师禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221178_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1221178'>予作此文，通公盖尝刻之石矣，字画既不工，又镌刻失真，师意每怅然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221178_comment'></div>予以绍兴乙卯仲春赴官霅川，师追饯至上虞，临别犹眷眷要予书，且砻石以俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221178_comment'></div>仲秋几望，其徒仲珣法嗣遣净人持书至平江，言师以七月五日示寂坐逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221178_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221178_comment'></div>师虽学律，而于少林宗风尤所通解，盖已超然神游八极之外矣，无足深悲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221178_comment'></div>适予友人邹德久相过，因道师行业之美，相与感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221178_comment'></div>德久书实当今第一，篆、真、行各臻其妙，庶几师之名，托此以不朽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221178_comment'></div>五松居士李某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1221178_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='22d97304f746404b9057cf6689fe6ffd_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>，60岁</div><div id='22d97304f746404b9057cf6689fe6ffd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年12月26日</a>　经婺州至衢州，过家乡，有诗。作品：丁已十二月二十六日过吾村，早饭宿后溪。永嘉，气温图经谓四时皆温，因以得名。予守郡二年，未尝见积雪，自行衢、婺，连见三白（梅蕊凌寒雪未消）<div id='poem_527906' class='_poem'><div href='/Writing/1220923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞开言路劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年闰3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220923")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220923'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220923'>臣闻帝王之美，莫大于询谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220923_comment'></div>治安之时，尤先于警戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220923_comment'></div>历观前代有为之君，虽聪明有馀，而切直之言不绝于耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220923_comment'></div>虽天下大治，而几微之慎不忘于怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220923_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下以睿知宽仁之资，膺祖宗积累隆平之业，劳心求治，几三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220923_comment'></div>华夏乂安，天地交泰，符瑞之应，史不绝书，所谓太平盈成之期，实在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220923_comment'></div>陛下所当忧勤宵旰，虚己以听纳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220923_comment'></div>群臣所宜精白勉励，夙夜以进戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220923_comment'></div>而近岁以来，士大夫狃于因循，宴安宠禄，谄佞成风，至妄引荀卿有听从无谏争之说，以杜塞言路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220923_comment'></div>多士盈庭，莫敢开说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220923_comment'></div>是陛下有容纳之德，而群臣进拒绝之计，朝政之阙失，臣下之奸邪，生民之利病，海内之休戚，何由尽闻乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220923_comment'></div>古人有言曰：「堂上远于百里，堂下远于千里，门庭远于万里」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220923_comment'></div>盖言壅隔之祸深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220923_comment'></div>臣愚伏望陛下博延群臣，明诏天下，广众正之路，开不讳之门，使忠良謇谔之士有所规益而谠言进，倾邪谗巧之徒不得壅蔽而下情通，实天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220923_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220923_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　闻李光以论事贬阳朔县，刘安世贻书伟之。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='97a578b9260f4bc5ac87772c609bf217_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("97a578b9260f4bc5ac87772c609bf217");'><span id='97a578b9260f4bc5ac87772c609bf217_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1127')">1125-1127年</a>，48-50岁</div><div id='97a578b9260f4bc5ac87772c609bf217' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　在京任司勋员外郎，迁符宝郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　在京任司勋员外郎期间，李纲有诗寄李光。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年8月17日</a>　在京任司勋员外郎期间，李光为张元干祖父手泽题跋。作品：题跋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（张元干《芦川归来集》卷十附录有李光题芦川祖父手泽。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年12月</a>　在京任司勋员外郎，劝徽宗内禅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年12月</a>　在开封。三子孟醇生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年1月12日</a>　在京任右司谏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年2月</a>　在京任右司谏。二月，太上皇东巡。李光有札子多篇。作品：论行宫冒赏札子。乞奉迎上皇札子。论制国用札子。论三镇亲王札子。<div id='poem_1220945' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220945?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论行宫冒赏劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220945")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220945'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220945'>臣闻唐德宗狩奉天，自发洋州以来，百姓进献瓜果，欲各与散官，陆贽以为不可，且曰：「爵禄天下之公器，而国之大柄也，惟功勋才德所宜处之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220945_comment'></div>夫散官，虚名也，贽犹力争至数千百言而不已，诚以所系者重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220945_comment'></div>臣伏闻上皇东巡，州县供馈无阙，此乃臣子之常分，何足为功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220945_comment'></div>兼供馈之物，自一毫以上皆行人及坊郭乡村有物力之人，非出供馈者之家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220945_comment'></div>供馈愈办，则剥民愈深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220945_comment'></div>臣访闻其间巧于谋身者，多是交结近习，纵其请求，需索无艺，往往缘此得其欢心，揄扬赞美，达之上皇，遂致增秩赐金，行宫如市，有再任者，有进三官者，有召赴都堂审察者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220945_comment'></div>恩赏僭滥，非散官之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220945_comment'></div>陆下修明百度，抑绝奔竞如此，而士大夫冒犯廉隅，侥倖苟得如彼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220945_comment'></div>况上皇銮舆还阙，将士冒行阵、突铦锋以卫护社稷者，或横尸原野，或暴露边陲，未闻少加恩典，而首及州县猾邪之徒，非所以示天下之公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220945_comment'></div>所有已降迁官进职等指挥，伏望圣慈特赐寝罢，以安人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220945_comment'></div>臣无任激切待命之至，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1220945'><span class='label'>按：</span>五月二日奉圣旨，上皇经由道路宣力之人，可依下项。宁陵知县赵子游等，各转官有差。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1220945_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1220935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞奉迎上皇劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220935")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220935'>臣闻唐明皇避寇幸蜀，肃宗即位灵武，及二京平，李泌为群臣通奏，具言天子思恋晨昏，请促还以就孝养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220935_comment'></div>若泌者，可谓善处人父子之间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220935_comment'></div>恭惟陛下天性仁孝，伏自上皇东幸暴露，日夜忧思，至避殿减膳，不遑宁处，群臣士庶莫不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220935_comment'></div>而军兴之际，朝廷多事，道路隔绝，臣恐陛下至意未能感通，而奸邪之人易成间隙，以上贻宗庙之忧，下为群臣之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220935_comment'></div>治乱之原，安危之机，尽在于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220935_comment'></div>臣愚伏望陛下亲降诏旨，令三省枢密院集两省台谏官合议奉迎上皇典礼，使陛下大孝之美纯粹光显，过于未登大位之时，实天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220935_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220935_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220939?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论制国用劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220939")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220939_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220939'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220939'>臣伏睹祖宗之制，天下财谷悉总于三司，非条例有定数，不敢擅支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220939_comment'></div>朝廷知其大数，量入为出，故能仓廪充溢，用度有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220939_comment'></div>近年以来，政出多门，法度<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1220939", 1220939, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>寖弛</span>，户部既不得总天下财赋，朝廷亦无缘尽知钱谷大数，侵支互用，不可几察，名为应奉御前，其实般入私室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220939_comment'></div>东南财赋尽于朱勔，西北财赋困于李彦，天下根本之财竭于蔡京、王黼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220939_comment'></div>自徐铸、蒋彝为常平司官，何渐为茶马司官，张琬、徐惕、燕瑛为市舶官，应安道、朱彦美、王子献、王复为转运司官，胡直孺、卢宗原为发运使，王仲闳、胡邃为提点刑狱，宋诲为香盐官，刘寄、吕岯、毛孝立为盐司属官，天下财赋尽归权倖之家，小人乘时无复忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220939_comment'></div>今所至匮竭，公家无半年之储，百姓无旬日之积，加之兵兴，府库金帛，散用将尽，此乃国用危急之时，所谓理财经久之术，不可不虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220939_comment'></div>伏望遵依祖宗故事，使三省、枢密院通知兵民财利大计，与户部量一岁出入，以制国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220939_comment'></div>仍乞精择健吏通知财计者，置司驱磨诸路应干钱物往来移用过及见在之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220939_comment'></div>其官吏各量添俸给，课以功限，为之赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220939_comment'></div>或专遣使命，就所至勾集诸司人吏驱磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220939_comment'></div>庶几利源归一，而天下财用可得而理矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220939_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220939_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论三镇亲王劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220940")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220940'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220940'>臣闻《春秋》之义，许外国者不一而足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220940_comment'></div>颜师古曰：「节制之，不皆称其所求也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220940_comment'></div>臣伏睹金人恃众凌犯，邀求无艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220940_comment'></div>陛下天度包荒，不爱重宝，不惜土地，又遣亲王大臣为质，卑辞厚礼，惟恐少失其意，待之可谓尽矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220940_comment'></div>而贪婪无厌，诡诈难测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220940_comment'></div>近者载遣使人，复以亲王大臣都尉为请，无礼亦甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220940_comment'></div>臣职在谏垣，连日伺候班次，未蒙引对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220940_comment'></div>退伏维念上皇在东南，陛下阙晨昏之养，未有以慰其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220940_comment'></div>今连遣二子入不测之敌，无乃伤父子之情乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220940_comment'></div>况肃王孱弱，置之军中，万一暴露感疾，陛下有杀弟之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220940_comment'></div>又三镇者皆天下劲兵处，太祖、太宗百战乃得之，一旦举以予人，陛下为人子孙，嗣守大业，使两路生灵无故陷没，尚何以为国乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220940_comment'></div>此又不可之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220940_comment'></div>夫城下之盟，诸侯之所深耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220940_comment'></div>以国家全盛之势、四海九州之广，勤王之师不绝于道，伏望陛下明诏将相大臣，别议攻守之策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220940_comment'></div>仍乞间道遣使，檄河东、河北两路，尽发强壮策应，首尾掩击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220940_comment'></div>天地助顺，必成大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220940_comment'></div>臣无任忠愤激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1220940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年2月</a>　在京任右司谏。二月，太上皇东巡。李光有札子奏论太上皇随行内侍颇有邓珙等谗邪之人。作品：论内臣邓珙状。<div id='poem_1220936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论内臣邓珙等状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220936")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220936'>臣恭惟道君太上皇帝仓卒南征，暴露野次，陛下忧惧，不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220936_comment'></div>金人退师之翌日，遣使问安，又择见任执政为奉迎使，陛下东向，临遣于庭，令所至赏犒随行将士，抚谕行宫使已下，令扈从，以必上皇之归，孝思至矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220936_comment'></div>且命宗室父老迎谒近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220936_comment'></div>亦既越旬，未闻属车之音，群臣士庶不能无私忧者，以群小人在侧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220936_comment'></div>臣访问随行内侍，其间颇有谗邪之人，造饰奸言，欲以离间陛下父子，以龙德为隘，而进西幸之策，使陛下以天下之大而不能安其亲，挟此为奸，何所不至！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220936_comment'></div>此诚社稷之深忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220936_comment'></div>臣愿陛下择其尤甚者，行遣一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220936_comment'></div>其往来京城、踪迹诡秘如邓珙者，传播诏书以惑众听如刘奭者，妄议朝政、不循分守如徐霁者，朋附道流、凶恶稔著如董舜贤者，李琮、梁师彦之阴怀反侧，任钧、冯彦、石如冈之素著凶豪，凡此数人，皆工谗善佞，小人之桀黠者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220936_comment'></div>自知过失既多，畏陛下之严，恐一旦有所不容，是以日夜窥觇，搆间百端，不可不虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220936_comment'></div>臣愚伏望陛下遣使躬禀上皇，将此数人重行窜斥，别选老成端愿之人，以充上皇扫除之役，庶几小人不敢牵制行宫，既复二圣重欢，实天下庆幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1220936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年2月</a>　在京任右司谏。奏论王云、宇文虚中朋附童贯，宜早赐罢黜。作品：论王云等札子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年2月</a>　在京任右司谏。金人入寇，王蕃避敌远遁，不知所在。李光奏论王蕃。作品：乞追究王蕃召姚古札子。<div id='poem_1220932' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220932' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220932?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞追究王蕃召姚古劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220932")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220932_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220932'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220932'>臣等伏见朝廷自闻金人入境，即差王蕃、姚古充京畿四面制置使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220932_comment'></div>今姚古未闻来期，王蕃统领禁兵，避敌远遁，不知所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220932_comment'></div>京畿诸邑及近京州县，例被劫掠，道路不通，都城闭关多日，民间百物窘乏，人情忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220932_comment'></div>欲乞先次选差将兵分屯城外，以御他寇，仍开南城一面门，多差将兵讥察守御，以通往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220932_comment'></div>仍乞差官趣召姚古，追究王蕃所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220932_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220932_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年2月</a>　在京任右司谏。金人退师，李光奏论究治在京擅离官守之士大夫之罪。作品：论在京擅离官守人一等科罪札子。<div id='poem_1220949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论在京擅离官守人一等科罪劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220949")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220949'>臣窃惟圣主制世御俗之方，莫大于赏罚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220949_comment'></div>所以行赏罚者，莫先于至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220949_comment'></div>古者爵人于朝，与众共之，刑人于市，与众共之，明不敢以己之私恩，废天下之公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220949_comment'></div>臣伏见金人内侵，都城危逼，士大夫委职而去者五十二员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220949_comment'></div>近缘臣寮论列，有旨令吏部具职位、姓名送大理寺根勘，约法断罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220949_comment'></div>陛下示天下大公之道，可谓尽矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220949_comment'></div>命下之日，士论纷然，或谓罪同罚异，致陛下有失刑之讥，大臣负党奸之谤，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220949_comment'></div>如卫仲达、张劝、冯温舒、蔡行兄弟，皆从官也，林虞、刘焘、袁植，皆致仕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220949_comment'></div>在仲达、劝则除名勒停，虞则追五官除名勒停，行兄弟及温舒、焘、植则置而不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220949_comment'></div>或旋求名目如蔡绩、蔡续者，或妄托假故如许行、宋时者，种种奸欺，莫究虚实，其为擅去官守一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220949_comment'></div>今诈冒者反得轻典，孤拙者多陷深文，陛下既已付之有司，法者天子所与天下公共也，原情定罪，不容有所轻重，况得而私之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220949_comment'></div>伏望圣慈将大理寺定断到应干逃避臣僚，系在去年十二月十七日已后，不问有无事故，尽作擅去官守，一等坐罪，庶几公道昭明，人言弭息，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220949_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1220949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月4日</a>　在京除侍御史，李光上辞免状。作品：辞免除侍御史札子。<div id='poem_1220942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除侍御史劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220942")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220942'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220942'>臣闻命震惊，莫知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220942_comment'></div>伏念臣承学浅陋，赋性迂愚，比者伏蒙陛下擢寘谏垣，日月未几，曾无古人正色献替之效，莫副陛下虚怀听纳之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220942_comment'></div>腼颜尸禄，日俟罪谴，敢图误奖，更践台端？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220942_comment'></div>况今多事之际，士论未一，民论未孚，非智识议论足以裨益政体，刚方谅直足以纠正官邪，曷可仰副陛下责任之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220942_comment'></div>如臣妄庸，猥被简拔，恩私过厚，职任难胜，退自省循，安敢冒处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220942_comment'></div>伏望陛下察臣诚悃，追寝成命，别除一閒慢差遣，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220942_comment'></div>臣无任激切屏营之至，谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220942_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在京除侍御史，李光再上辞免状。作品：再辞免除侍御史札子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月</a>　在京任侍御史。三月累月檄奏不已。论太上皇后不应入居禁中事。作品：议太上皇后还宫之仪状。<div id='poem_1220948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议太上皇后还宫之仪状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220948")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220948'>臣近睹礼部关报，太上皇后先次还宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220948_comment'></div>陛下屡降德音，戒敕有司，缮治撷景园，易名宁德宫，务极闳丽，以称崇奉之意，使命往来，不绝于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220948_comment'></div>陛下每于艰危扰攘之时，延见群臣，忧形于色，未尝不以暴露为念，此于太上皇后可谓无负矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220948_comment'></div>臣闻近日外议籍籍，咸谓太上皇后轻信小人之言，遣使切责陛下，臣在外庭，不知何事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220948_comment'></div>妄传欲开宣德门入居大内，群臣士庶，莫不惶骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220948_comment'></div>以臣料之，万无此理，设或有之，此岂太上皇后保全郑氏之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220948_comment'></div>恭惟道君太上皇帝，上畏天戒，下顺民心，以宗庙社稷之重，躬行尧舜之事，退居潜藩，以神器付陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220948_comment'></div>大内者，天子之居，神器所在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220948_comment'></div>使无纤芥之嫌，陛下欲便温凊之养，迎奉入内，亦当躬禀上皇，下有司讨论典礼，如汉唐故事，缮营宫室，嫔嫱𥊍御，严为限隔，以防意外之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220948_comment'></div>纵陛下母子慈孝，万无他嫌，其如左右近习之人，怀奸结怨，摇动两宫，则萧墙之忧，不可不虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220948_comment'></div>伏望陛下明诏三省、枢密院大臣，速议太上皇后还宫之仪，以全陛下母子之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220948_comment'></div>臣不胜激切待命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月</a>　在京任侍御史。李光奏乞贬逐台谏不施行日下出门事。作品：论贬逐台谏乞不施行日下出门指挥状。<div id='poem_1220965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论贬逐台谏乞不施行日下出门指挥状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220965")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220965'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220965'>臣伏睹前谏议大夫唐重等五人与郡，日下出门，流传四方，士论惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220965_comment'></div>陛下新即大位，开怀听纳之初，宜优容直言，礼遇臣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220965_comment'></div>今重等备员台谏，不知所论何事，既令日下出门，议者遂致纷然，造饰语言，称师骥论十事，孙觌、李擢等攻击宰执，缘此被逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220965_comment'></div>盖朝廷未尝降出得罪之因，宜其纷然有以议陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220965_comment'></div>重等既各与便郡，如同、棣、和，皆天下膏腴处，正使自择，不过此耳，何至迫逐使之仓皇若此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220965_comment'></div>臣伏见祖宗朝斥逐言官，虽远在岭外，未有日下出门者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220965_comment'></div>熙宁中王安石为相，急于行法，恶人之议己，始有此行遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220965_comment'></div>后来蔡京、王黼用事，欲行己私，循用此例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220965_comment'></div>缘此言路塞绝，岂可施于今日艰难之时哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220965_comment'></div>伏望特降睿旨，将日下出门指挥更不施行，庶令般挈家属，收拾行李，以示陛下优纳之意。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1220965'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1220965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月</a>　在京任侍御史。奏论胡直孺、燕瑛等吞食东南财用、交结近幸事。作品：论胡直孺札子。论胡直孺第二札子。论燕瑛胡直孺札子。再论燕瑛胡直孺札子。论燕瑛胡直孺第三札子。<div id='poem_1220954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论胡直孺第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220954")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220954'>臣近再上章论列工部尚书胡直孺罪恶，已蒙陛下开纳，许以必行，亦既累日，不见降黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220954_comment'></div>此必大臣以直孺为贤，曲加覆护，以臣言为妄，未肯施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220954_comment'></div>夫大臣以进退人材为职，所进忠贤则国家享其利，所进<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1220954", 1220954, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>憸佞</span>则人主受其欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220954_comment'></div>陛下不以臣不肖，使得待罪言路，若大臣用人失当，臣得而论之，朝廷行之，则陛下威权立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220954_comment'></div>今臣力言之，陛下虚己而听之，大臣沮抑之，则是陛下威福之柄，反制于大臣，而臣区区不能但已者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220954_comment'></div>况直孺佞邪，天下所闻，与应安道、卢宗原相继为转运使及发运使，欺罔朝廷，如循一轨，将上供物料及粮纲船尽充花石之供，号为应奉，州县帑藏为一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220954_comment'></div>起发封桩，妄称均籴，岁计不足，犹进羡馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220954_comment'></div>缘此进职，滥厕从班，遂知平江府，纵朱氏请求，益肆掊敛，不复知有朝廷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220954_comment'></div>直孺素畜声妓，每携就朱氏园亭，与倡优杂处，啖其子侄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220954_comment'></div>吴民怨愤，目为朱家奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220954_comment'></div>勔入京师，凶焰益炽，至与宰执争权，窃弄国柄，首引直孺为户部侍郎，搢绅侧目，莫不骇叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220954_comment'></div>伏自陛下即位，灼见奸凶，以次流放，党类屏息，独直孺反被褒擢，联八座之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220954_comment'></div>命下之日，士论沸腾，前后臣寮，论列不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220954_comment'></div>伏望陛下断自渊衷，速赐窜黜，以为多士之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220954_comment'></div>如臣所奏失实，欺罔聪听，亦望解臣言职，重置典宪，臣与直孺理难两存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220954_comment'></div>臣不胜激切待命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220954_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1220954_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论燕瑛胡直孺劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220956")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220956'>臣窃谓监司郡守，号为近民之官，势力气焰，足以制百姓死生之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220956_comment'></div>顷者奸倖当权，奢淫无度，竭生灵之膏血，不足以供溪壑之欲，于是分遣亲信之人，忍为残贼敢为奸赃者，布满州县，夤缘假借，上下相蒙，其剥民愈甚，则获赏愈多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220956_comment'></div>如应安道、徐铸之流，死亡略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220956_comment'></div>今其在者踪迹显露，莫如燕瑛、胡直孺二人，皆自郡守监司以赃污致身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220956_comment'></div>臣累具弹奏，必蒙陛下委曲开纳，臣亦委曲为陛下言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220956_comment'></div>若以朝廷多事之际，以为有材，亦当置在三边财谷之地，不当佚以宫祠，优以便郡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220956_comment'></div>今乃反得辅郡，地望愈隆，沮天下至公之论，成憸人怙宠之私，成命既颁，物议沸腾，此必大臣有阴为之地者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220956_comment'></div>二人平昔止能以珍奇货贿交结权倖，饮馔声伎媚说要人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220956_comment'></div>身虽去国，各留子弟见在京师，日造大臣之门，对众附耳，营求百端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220956_comment'></div>稔恶弗悛，无复忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220956_comment'></div>伏望陛下奋发威断，直批付三省褫夺职名，重行窜殛，以解四方之疑，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220956_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220956_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论燕瑛胡直孺第三劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220957")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220957'>臣累论列燕瑛、胡直孺，不当宠以峻职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220957_comment'></div>蒙陛下开纳，许以必行，至今累月，未见褫夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220957_comment'></div>瑛关通交结，皆出宦官，直孺拔擢，悉由朱勔，此陛下所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220957_comment'></div>夫人主之于臣下，患在不知其奸，苟或知之，而复赦之，则小人放纵无所忌惮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220957_comment'></div>故知善而不能用，与知恶而不能去，诚人主之深戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220957_comment'></div>今此二人，非独臣知之，天下之人莫不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220957_comment'></div>臣若不言，则负陛下，言之则触大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220957_comment'></div>傥大臣以直孺等为才，当多事之际，欲湔洗而用之，则当置在三边兵刑财赋有用之地，尚为有名，不当佚以宫祠，优以便郡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220957_comment'></div>臣诚愚瞽，官小言轻，非仰恃陛下优容，势必不敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220957_comment'></div>伏乞检会臣先后所上文字，降付三省，早赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220957_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年4月</a>　在京任侍御史。奏论蔡攸欲以扈卫上皇行宫因缘入都。作品：论蔡攸欲潜入都城札子。<div id='poem_1220947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蔡攸欲潜入都城劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220947")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220947'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220947'>臣伏见蔡京父子当国日久，窃弄威柄，败坏纪纲，使朝廷失信于四方，至上皇负谤于天下，军民怨愤，士论沸腾，前后臣寮，论列非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220947_comment'></div>其它元恶巨奸，悉已窜逐，独京父子尚迟回近甸，未正典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220947_comment'></div>访闻攸不自引避，欲以扈卫行宫为名，侥倖入都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220947_comment'></div>窃听民言，深可忧虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220947_comment'></div>若攸果入都城，则百姓必致生变，万一惊犯上皇属车之尘，则臣坐不预言之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220947_comment'></div>伏望陛下特降睿旨，早赐黜责施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220947_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年5月</a>　在京任侍御史。上书论王安石及元祐之学。作品：论王氏及元祐之学。<div id='poem_1220946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论王氏及元祐之学</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220946")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220946'>臣愚昧朴拙，当陛下初政，偶承乏擢寘言路，每因进对，备闻德言，未尝不以绍复祖宗法度为说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220946_comment'></div>忠臣义士，莫不欢欣鼓舞，日须德化之成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220946_comment'></div>臣今月十七日入台，伏睹三省降到黄榜一道，臣寮上言，以王安石为名世之学，发明要妙，著为新经，天下学者，翕然宗师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220946_comment'></div>又言熙宁、元丰间，内外安平，公私充实，法令备具，赋役均平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220946_comment'></div>其意专以王氏之说为是，公肆诞谩，无复忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220946_comment'></div>以陛下圣明，未可遽欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220946_comment'></div>既以司马光与安石俱为天下之大贤，又云优劣等第，自有公论，觐言者之意，必不肯以光为优，以安石为劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220946_comment'></div>夫光与安石，行事之是非，议论之邪正，皎若白黑，虽儿童走卒，粗有知识者莫不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220946_comment'></div>当熙宁、元丰间，如韩琦、富弼、欧阳修之属，尚皆无恙，安石恶其议己，皆指为因循之人，摈斥不用，卒以愤死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220946_comment'></div>恭惟太祖、太宗创业之艰难，真宗、仁宗守成之不易，规模宏远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220946_comment'></div>安石欲尽废祖宗法度，则为说曰「陛下当制法而不当制于法」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220946_comment'></div>欲尽逐元老大臣，则为说曰「陛下当化俗而不当化于俗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220946_comment'></div>蔡京兄弟祖述其说，五十年间搢绅受祸，生灵被害，海内流毒，而祖宗法度、元老大臣扫荡禁锢，几无馀蕴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220946_comment'></div>幸赖宗庙社稷之灵，上皇悔悟，以祖宗不拔之基全付陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220946_comment'></div>今言者又创为熙、丰之说，以安石为大贤，臣恐此论一出，流闻四方，鼓惑民听，人心一失，不可复收，非朝廷之福也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年6月</a>　在京任侍御史。论奏李会、李擢不当复用事。作品：论李会李擢札子。<div id='poem_1220969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论李会李擢劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220969")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220969_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220969'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220969'>臣伏睹除目，以李会、李擢为左右司谏，训词褒谕，以首论蔡京有功，特被召用，外庭之议，无不骇愕，臣之区区，亦所未喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220969_comment'></div>夫首论蔡京者，陈瓘也，其次则有石公弼、张克公、毛注之流，相继弹击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220969_comment'></div>上皇觉悟，既罢而复用者数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220969_comment'></div>京与王黼前后用事，权倾天下，言路塞绝，多士盈庭，莫敢开说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220969_comment'></div>方是时也，忠义奋发，不避死亡之诛，慷慨言事，不过曹辅等三五人尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220969_comment'></div>下逮韦布之士，廷对大问，进药石之言，则有若范宗尹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220969_comment'></div>投匦献计，箴时政之失，则有若朱梦说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220969_comment'></div>而会、擢在当时迭为台官，身任言责，保宠固位，被阿谀之讥，目睹时事，曾无一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220969_comment'></div>逮陛下龙飞，灼见奸慝，太学诸生伏阙上书，首论六贼之害，蔡京之恶，夫人而能言之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220969_comment'></div>谏官、御史能于此时明目张胆击奸指佞，实恃陛下圣明，不啻摧枯拉朽之易，何足为功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220969_comment'></div>况会、擢当金兵围逼都城，力附白时中、李邦彦，专主避敌割地之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220969_comment'></div>方肃王之北渡也，不罪金人之渝盟，乃敢奋笔横议，以上皇还宫，问肃王所在，劫持上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220969_comment'></div>必欲以祖宗基业委之敌国，至有三镇与王室孰重之语，章疏具存，可以考按。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220969_comment'></div>今时中、邦彦坐是落职，议者犹谓轻典，而会、擢反被召用，复预谏争之列，不知谁为陛下荐此二人者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220969_comment'></div>陛下好恶取舍如此，庙堂之论何时而定，百官有司之众何所适从乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220969_comment'></div>臣愚伏望陛下深思熟察，辨邪正之归，无为诡辞偏说之所倾夺，庶以仰称陛下艰难求助之意，副四方跂竦之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220969_comment'></div>所有会、擢等召命，伏乞特赐寝罢，以安众情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220969_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220969_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在京任侍御史。金人围太原，李光上半年奏请修京城守御之备。作品：乞用河东土豪援太原札子、再乞起河东民兵状。<div id='poem_1220951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞用河东土豪援太原劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220951")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220951'>臣近因进对，伏见陛下以太原围闭日久，援兵无功，深轸宸衷，忧形于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220951_comment'></div>臣退与寮属具言，今日之患，诚无急于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220951_comment'></div>臣东南书生，岂知为兵，因辄询求，博采众议，及河东士大夫有访臣者，皆言方今事势危急，忻、代二州，已为敌境，泽、潞、汾、晋，又遭刘嗣初残破，富家大姓，往往奔走四出，独力田之民，恋著乡土，多自团成保甲，守护乡闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220951_comment'></div>朝廷若起而用之，可得土民十馀万，人人自肯为战，盖子弟之卫父兄，手足之捍头目，其势然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220951_comment'></div>今朝廷兵力单弱，四方兵未有至者，万一太原不守，则河东决非朝廷之有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220951_comment'></div>若恤小害，则大患不除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220951_comment'></div>欲望圣慈逐急就委折彦质，尽起晋、绛、慈、隰、泽、潞、威胜、汾州八处民兵，自二十已上、五十已下，及本路诸县弓手，令见任州知通、县令佐，据所统属，各自部辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220951_comment'></div>其间亦有土豪及士人愿为头首者甚众，若假以初等官及应副器甲，使与官军协力赴援，比之他路起兵，无逃窜剽掠之患，减飞刍挽粟之劳，人自为战，家自为守，功必倍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220951_comment'></div>仍乞先遣信使赍诏书谕以祸福，人必乐从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220951_comment'></div>出夫之家给复三年，州县敢逗挠者，并以军法从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220951_comment'></div>愚计如此，傥粗合圣意，乞诏三省、枢密院大臣详议施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220951_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220951_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞起河东民兵状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220952")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220952'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220952'>臣近尝具奏，乞尽起河东民兵，赴援太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220952_comment'></div>乃是臣呼召平阳府进士刁处仁等商议，为臣言：「力田之民颇恋著乡土，各自团成保甲，咸有斗志，若起而为兵，比之他路，无逃窜剽劫之患，减飞刍挽粟之劳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220952_comment'></div>其言似可采用，未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220952_comment'></div>今河东士大夫避地至都下者甚众，其刁处仁等亦各愿随逐使人前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220952_comment'></div>乞下臣章枢密院，令出榜召募，询访谋策，庶有裨益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220952_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220952_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在京任侍御史。奏论彗出寅、艮间事星。作品：论彗札子。<div id='poem_1220974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论彗劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220974")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220974_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220974'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220974'>臣闻《易》曰：「天垂象，见吉凶，圣人象之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220974_comment'></div>盖观乎天文以验得失者，诚圣王之先务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220974_comment'></div>臣伏见近者彗出寅艮间，躔度甚速，此变易之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220974_comment'></div>或传朝廷用阴阳家说，以分野言之，为敌人灭亡之證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220974_comment'></div>此恐导谀之人，以甘言谄辞媚悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220974_comment'></div>陛下轻信其说，无复答谢天谴之意，则亏损盛德，非宗庙生灵之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220974_comment'></div>臣闻孔子作《春秋》，不书祥瑞而书灾异者，盖欲警戒人君而知恐惧修省，以应天变，不闻以灾异归敌人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220974_comment'></div>二百四十二年之间，彗星三见，祸乱辄应，周室微弱，上下交怨，此皆人事之所感动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220974_comment'></div>天心仁爱人君，故出灾异以谴告之，不闻天心仁爱遐荒，欲其修省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220974_comment'></div>陛下万一惑于邪说，凡天地变动，各以分野言之，则陛下之失，自今以往，谁复敢言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220974_comment'></div>盖天变之发，或发于未然之前，或发于已然之后，皆所以觉悟人君也，所谓应天变之术，岂有他哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220974_comment'></div>在于修人事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220974_comment'></div>臣伏见陛下自即位以来，凡所施为，无非仰合天心，下当人意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220974_comment'></div>勤俭忧劳，不闻有过，然举措之间，安得每事皆当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220974_comment'></div>亦当穷究致彗之由，推至诚，行直道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220974_comment'></div>政事之不中不平者，或未加治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220974_comment'></div>万民之失业穷困者，或未加恤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220974_comment'></div>奸邪之徒荧惑主听者，或未加察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220974_comment'></div>言路骎骎复有壅隔之患，则阴阳之和，何时而致，天地之变，何时而息乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220974_comment'></div>臣所以居言责之地而不能默默也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220974_comment'></div>冒犯天威，臣无任激切恐惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1220974_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在开封，贬汀州酒税，未赴任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在开封，为朝奉郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在开封，为朝奉郎，奏论明节皇后不当立忌。作品：论明节皇后不当立忌状。<div id='poem_1220938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论明节皇后不当立忌状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220938")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220938'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220938'>臣准西上閤门关：「准太常寺关：今年迎奉道君太上皇帝，若在四月二日到京，缘当日系明节皇后忌辰，合分定奉迎及行香官」者，臣尝考求典礼，明节皇后不当立忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220938_comment'></div>昨缘太常少卿林震率意迎合，妄援温成故事为明节皇后立忌，因以为例，不复讨论，遂使圣朝著非礼之举，贻讥后世，不可不革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220938_comment'></div>窃详忌日之制，罢乐废务，修斋行香，皆子孙致其追慕之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220938_comment'></div>五季之乱，可谓无礼法矣，周世宗宣懿皇后入庙，议者犹以太后在上，疑祔庙之后，立忌非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220938_comment'></div>嘉祐中言者以久雨阴沴，宗庙之礼恐有未顺，且谓城南立温成庙，四时祭享，并同太庙之礼，盖当时有司失于讲求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220938_comment'></div>商宗遭变，饬己思咎，祖己训以典祀无丰于昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220938_comment'></div>况以嬖宠列于秩祀，非所以享天心、奉宗庙之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220938_comment'></div>熙宁中有司议改温成庙为祠殿，岁时遣宫臣行事，忌日斋祭，并合废罢，识者是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220938_comment'></div>今陛下初嗣历服，宜大正始之时，宗庙国之大事，伏望圣慈下有司讨论典礼，务合中制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220938_comment'></div>所有明节忌辰，乞且依温成故事罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220938_comment'></div>百官奉慰行香，止令内臣就祠殿行事，荐以常馔，庶合典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220938_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220938_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年6月6日</a>　在开封，擢秘书少监，未赴。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
古县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c9c990adadae491cb80b55fd7fdf217f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c9c990adadae491cb80b55fd7fdf217f");'><span id='c9c990adadae491cb80b55fd7fdf217f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1111')">1106-1111年</a>，29-34岁</div><div id='c9c990adadae491cb80b55fd7fdf217f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1109')">1106-1109年</a>　任岳阳县尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在岳阳。妹夫莫叔达卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　任岳阳县尉。作品：莫叔达墓记。<div id='poem_1221200' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221200' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221200?labeling=true' target='_blank'>莫叔达墓记</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221200")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221200_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221200'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221200'>建中靖国元年辛巳，予妹适馀姚莫叔达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221200_comment'></div>越崇宁三年甲申十月二十二日，以疾卒，即其年十二月二十一日葬于县之双雁乡乾溪之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221200_comment'></div>是时予在国学，每以不及见为终身恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221200_comment'></div>大观四年庚寅，遽闻叔达以六月二十八日卒，予又窃禄河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221200_comment'></div>自甲申距今七年，而君夫妇相继不幸，吁，可伤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221200_comment'></div>况予与君为姻契，盖有不可解于心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221200_comment'></div>其生也既不得数与君游，其死也又不得临尸而一祭，此重为可伤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221200_comment'></div>叔达家世儒者，少孤而立，天性和易，居家遇人与待交游，初终一心，不为疏昵厚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221200_comment'></div>故其死也，亲故无有怨议，既无愧于生死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221200_comment'></div>方吾妹之凶，君始过冠，遂无复有继室意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221200_comment'></div>平居蕴藉，有萧洒出尘之趣，故其死也，脱然如有所之，复何愧于夭寿邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221200_comment'></div>享年二十八，讳彦逵，叔达其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221200_comment'></div>曾祖政，祖偕，父易，皆隐德弗耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221200_comment'></div>以明年政和改元三月三十日，合葬于吾妹之域，从先卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221200_comment'></div>生一子，岁周而殇，先瘗其母之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221200_comment'></div>予闻君讣，得其死之详，故其葬也，述此以见其伤君之情，且以纪其岁月云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221200_comment'></div>将仕郎、晋州岳阳县尉兼主簿、专切教阅保甲、管勾学事李某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221200_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
嘉兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4a1f949985cd48a0a6c1dde79e768593_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a1f949985cd48a0a6c1dde79e768593");'><span id='4a1f949985cd48a0a6c1dde79e768593_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>，50岁</div><div id='4a1f949985cd48a0a6c1dde79e768593' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年9月7日</a>　在开封任秘书少监，被杭寇劫至秀州。作品：与翟公巽书。<div id='poem_1221079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与翟公巽书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221079")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221079'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221079'>某咨目顿首再拜，知府安抚内翰台座，即日伏惟台候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221079_comment'></div>某自越赴召至杭，八月一夜值军变，逃避民居凡五日，稍与人接，乃闻众军独不剽薛昂家，意欲请昂领府事以求招安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221079_comment'></div>昂畏避不出，贼势日炽，至硬刺平民，掳劫妇女，衣冠之族，尤被其辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221079_comment'></div>某两贻书昂，乞援福州金陵例权领府事，昂第皆贼兵环守，不能达至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221079_comment'></div>十九日，昂犹迟疑，又得寄居官列状同请，方肯就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221079_comment'></div>已而宪漕两司遣承议郎赵子璘入招安，贼须黄榜乃受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221079_comment'></div>又得左右提兵叩城，亲与士卒同甘苦，贼既素闻左右恩威，始大恟惧，直至月末，始受高士曈补官文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221079_comment'></div>昂谋遣某与方秘监等四员押第四头项陈青诣秀，请士曈入城抚定之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221079_comment'></div>九月三日见士曈于秀，士曈虽善遇青，而迟疑不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221079_comment'></div>某尝以大义责之，且言左右涉大江、入不测，而阁下号节制，乃远在数百里外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221079_comment'></div>适得黄榜赦令到，士曈乃行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221079_comment'></div>未至杭三十里间，群贼遣迎状相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221079_comment'></div>城门已开，某等先士曈之闾里，人情已帖然，贼兵皆免胄解甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221079_comment'></div>贼首陈通、其三沈安、其六叶轩以素队郊迎士曈于新桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221079_comment'></div>士曈不约束从者，稍捽辱之，以刀拍其背，搜解其刀环，仍夺其系巾金环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221079_comment'></div>群贼忿怒，疑陈青卖己，尽掠其家赀，杀其妻而囚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221079_comment'></div>新宪周格至，犹望其径入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221079_comment'></div>初八、初九，连遣父老僧道往城外，妓乐城内，俟其入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221079_comment'></div>已而闻格暴戾，怒骂其弟杞，群贼大愤，城内人情惴恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221079_comment'></div>贼首来昂第，凶悖殊甚，使群刀手拥某及赵子璘及赍黄榜使臣于庭下，欲杀，久之乃免，但使某与子璘及方元若皆处薛昂第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221079_comment'></div>昼夜贼兵七十馀人，白旗子十七人防守巡逻，仍钉其后门，事势危甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221079_comment'></div>十日大耀兵，十一日贼出兵劫鲍贻逊，为鎗仗手所败，几擒其二杨贵者，杀伤甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221079_comment'></div>是日闻外兵攻涌金门，贼众并力往救，使人叫呼百姓，诈言外兵屠城劫使，挈水救火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221079_comment'></div>续传火息兵退，又传湖上小舟载兵不可胜数，仓皇尽召诸贼往救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221079_comment'></div>至未时，又传兵退，然贼众大惧，达旦奔救叫呼，巡警不敢息，而其徒纷纷出怨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221079_comment'></div>百姓强刺者亦望官军破城，立降旗下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221079_comment'></div>某等不胜欣跃，意谓翌日外兵必大集，连日继攻，则贼破必矣，已而寂然无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221079_comment'></div>十四早，闻贼出馀杭门，欲劫两宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221079_comment'></div>某等意谓两宪既不肯入城，且已交锋，必引中军据要害，且檄鲍所统鎗仗手为声援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221079_comment'></div>而士曈皆不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221079_comment'></div>至午间，忽传擒士曈、杀格，城中士大夫惊骇之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221079_comment'></div>其日贼众凶焰尤炽，阖城生灵不保性命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221079_comment'></div>至十七日，闻群贼出临平，昏夜不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221079_comment'></div>次日乃知临平大掠罢，饮于酒坊，炊未及熟，闻鲍兵在长河欲来讨击，遽引归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221079_comment'></div>是日微雨道滑，自相惊恐，弃甲而遁，三鼓乃入城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221079_comment'></div>次日大恐，却有就招安之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221079_comment'></div>适会秀守赵叔近遣使臣以檄书来招，遂欣然从之，数以文书往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221079_comment'></div>至十月二十日，昂复召某等往秀，请叔近速入抚定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221079_comment'></div>四日至秀，五日叔近行事必可济，某等不复往矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221079_comment'></div>自去月初士曈懦怯，格暴戾无术，遂致平民二万人为贼所刺，南厅十九万缗为贼所费，妄散仓米十数万石，拆烧民居数千间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221079_comment'></div>涂炭一月，不可形状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221079_comment'></div>招安遂成于叔近，所以就招安者，初畏越兵，终畏鲍卒十七日追袭之威也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221079_comment'></div>窃惟执事以名臣守郡，控制东南，威名远著，二浙倚为长城，群贼情状，所宜尽知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221079_comment'></div>是用粗述己事，布于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221079_comment'></div>某崎岖避难，凡六十人，仅存单孑一身，自告敕料历等，皆未知所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221079_comment'></div>方避难时相为命者，独左右所遣虞候孙昌一名耳，至今相随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221079_comment'></div>其他皆为所虏，亦已甘心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221079_comment'></div>冬候顿寒，伏惟保重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221079_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1221079_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='314181a9577a431fb01cbd0a06879b4c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("314181a9577a431fb01cbd0a06879b4c");'><span id='314181a9577a431fb01cbd0a06879b4c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>，51岁</div><div id='314181a9577a431fb01cbd0a06879b4c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　过桐江，经严濑，慨然有感。予方力丐宫祠，有终焉之志，因和致道《水调歌头》，呈子我、行简。作品：水调歌头（兵气暗吴楚）<span class='inlineComment2'>（宣和三年（1121），改睦州为严州。）</span><div id='poem_117769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_117769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/117769?labeling=true' 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_117769")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_117769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_117769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_117769'>兵气暗吴楚，江汉久凄凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_117769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_117769'>当年俊杰安在，酌酒酹严光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_117769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_117769'>南顾豺狼吞噬，北望中原板荡，矫首讯穹苍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_117769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_117769'>归去谢宾友，客路饱风霜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_117769_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_117769'>闭柴扉，窥千载，考三皇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_117769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_117769'>兰亭胜处，依旧流水绕修篁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_117769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_117769'>傍有湖光千顷，时泛扁舟一叶，啸傲水云乡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_117769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_117769'>寄语骑鲸客，何事返南荒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_117769_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
