-----title
宣州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4e473e1519af4b10a209a5407494d189_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4e473e1519af4b10a209a5407494d189");'><span id='4e473e1519af4b10a209a5407494d189_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1130')">1129-1130年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='4e473e1519af4b10a209a5407494d189' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年5月</a>　在宣州，除知宣州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在宣州，进直龙图阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月</a>　在宣州，击退繁昌叛军，进右文殿修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在宣州，上札奏乞并力进兵攻讨金人。作品：乞进兵状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道二年(1166)宣州改为宁国府。）</span><div id='poem_1220979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220979?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞进兵状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220979")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220979'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220979'>昨自建康失守，右仆射杜充退守仪真，陈邦光、李棁率吏民迎降金人，大队由境上入浙，游骑昼夜侵逼，及防江溃兵四散剽掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220979_comment'></div>幸赖朝廷威德，将士协力，防守至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220979_comment'></div>臣探得建康所留敌骑，不过数千人，金萧、张二大帅与陈邦光、李棁同治府事，时复遣兵及黄旂招诱州县，如溧水等处县官，皆已投拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220979_comment'></div>本州实与接境，人情反侧，不住分遣将士，前后杀获首级，招安到溃兵佥军班直、契丹、渤海等处人兵，多方存养讥察外，臣近据于潜知县通直郎陈近仁、昌化县尉保义郎平协申：去年十二月二十日，金经略使称四太子郎君，金知临安府李俦差修武郎乐宏赍文字黄旂前来临安、于潜、昌化等县招抚官吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220979_comment'></div>本县官吏各奋忠义，遂将乐宏等四人斩首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220979_comment'></div>其临安、馀杭知县将带老父入城投拜，邀请敌兵，就县敷买金银疋帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220979_comment'></div>又于今年正月初十日，再遣凌秀才、王秀才二人，金补承信郎，令赍文字前来，本县亦将此二人处斩，枭首号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220979_comment'></div>及两县弓手土豪章开、王仙、毕康等纠率诸乡保甲，义不从降，委是防托有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220979_comment'></div>缘本州管下宁国县，与两邑接境，其知临安府康允之未知去处，吏民无所申诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220979_comment'></div>臣已逐急依已得圣旨，便宜措置，将立功四人先次借补承信郎，及专遣使臣赍去年十二月二十日蜡弹手诏，晓谕官吏兵民，各用命守御去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220979_comment'></div>臣窃观金人敢深入江浙，于天时地利皆非所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220979_comment'></div>臣已率励将士及将已团结到六县保甲，并招安到杜充防江统制官马吉、李进，并班直京军等邀其归路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220979_comment'></div>臣已移文刘光世，乞带领大兵前来同卫王室，及申本路转运使李尚行、朱异前来权建康府安抚司职事，庶几列郡有所禀承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220979_comment'></div>并未蒙回报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220979_comment'></div>今敌马既屯驻临安府，行在信息隔绝难通，小人遂无忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220979_comment'></div>臣累具奏闻，欲乞速降睿旨，差委重臣前来建康，或令宣抚使周望传檄四方，约日进兵，水陆分布，可使只轮不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220979_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1220979_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　在宣州视事，金人不敢入宣州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月</a>　金兵逼境，李光率众坚守，宣州城赖以全。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月14日</a>　戚方围宣州，李光奋力拒敌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月13日</a>　戚方攻宣州不克，退去，宣州解围。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在宣州，贼退后登楼抒发高兴之情。作品：贼退双溪楼遣兴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道二年(1166)宣州改为宁国府。）</span><div id='poem_527694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贼退双溪楼遣兴<span class='inlineComment2'>（是时方力辞召命）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527694")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527694'>朝来喜见妖氛静，坐觉山川胜气还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527694'>关塞罢征车马健，郊原得雨老龙闲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527694'>黄绵惯拥茅檐日，白发羞陪玉笋班。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527694'>好在故园兵火后，那无破屋两三间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　守宣州期间，李光与惠通律师游。作品：舍黄蘖裴公真像并偈。<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道二年(1166)宣州改为宁国府。）</span><div id='poem_1221178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舍黄蘖裴公真像<span class='inlineComment2'>（并偈）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221178")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221178'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221178'>宣州广教禅寺，实唐裴公故宅、黄蘖道场，二公像设存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221178_comment'></div>气韵森严，笔法简古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221178_comment'></div>予守郡日，命工摹得之，顾私家不能严净，适通公律师访予五松山，一见若有宿契，因请留寘铁磬堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221178_comment'></div>或曰：「静凝学徒皆宗律教，以南山为祖师，得无异议乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221178_comment'></div>予曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221178_comment'></div>禅、律二宗，本相因依，后学末师，妄自分别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221178_comment'></div>昔宽禅师谓白乐天曰：『无上菩提者，被于身为律，说于口为法，得于心为禅，应用者三，其致一也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221178_comment'></div>故如来所说大乘诸经，以文殊为问答之首者，皆明法身妙慧之门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221178_comment'></div>以普贤为问荅之首者，皆明妙智之万行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221178_comment'></div>诸佛菩萨皆依此二尊者以为师范，然后成菩萨之极果，处如来之上乘，岂有二哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221178_comment'></div>通公志行苦卓，识趣超然，禅、律并行，不相留碍，其必有得于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221178_comment'></div>恐诸衲子尚有疑情，对大众前复说偈曰：君看铁磬堂前像，恰似文殊对普贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221178_comment'></div>更着白须裴老子，夜深同听祖师禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221178_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1221178'>予作此文，通公盖尝刻之石矣，字画既不工，又镌刻失真，师意每怅然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221178_comment'></div>予以绍兴乙卯仲春赴官霅川，师追饯至上虞，临别犹眷眷要予书，且砻石以俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221178_comment'></div>仲秋几望，其徒仲珣法嗣遣净人持书至平江，言师以七月五日示寂坐逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221178_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221178_comment'></div>师虽学律，而于少林宗风尤所通解，盖已超然神游八极之外矣，无足深悲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221178_comment'></div>适予友人邹德久相过，因道师行业之美，相与感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221178_comment'></div>德久书实当今第一，篆、真、行各臻其妙，庶几师之名，托此以不朽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221178_comment'></div>五松居士李某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1221178_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='620d5f2e9d8946338735af58daf7b18a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("620d5f2e9d8946338735af58daf7b18a");'><span id='620d5f2e9d8946338735af58daf7b18a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，55岁</div><div id='620d5f2e9d8946338735af58daf7b18a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月29日</a>　任淮西招抚使，抵达宣州城下。是夜，与王燮共议讨伐韩世清事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月1日</a>　执韩世清于宣州，押赴行在。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　还自淮西，重至宣城，与德渊寺丞诸友游，有诗抒怀。作品：绍兴二年三月还自淮西，重至宣城，与德渊寺丞诸友散步后圃，登双溪楼。<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道二年(1166)宣州改为宁国府。）</span><div id='poem_527878' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527878' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527878?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绍兴二年三月还自淮西重至宣城与德渊寺丞诸友散步后圃登双溪楼二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527878")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527878_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527878'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527878'>翛然危观出风尘，千里溪山照映人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527878'>飞盖追随宾客旧，满园桃李不胜春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527878'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527878_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527879?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527879'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527879'>夙衔王命出行朝，军士无哗罢击刁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527879'>一笑聊空狐鼠穴<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作关头发三箭，据院本改）</span>，却驱貔虎取天骄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527879'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527879_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月7日</a>　充端明殿学士江东安抚大使，知建康府、兼寿春府，滁濠庐州无为军宣抚使，有谢表。作品：赐对衣金带鞍马谢表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道二年(1166)宣州改为宁国府。）</span><div id='poem_1221061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐对衣金带鞍马谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221061")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221061'>臣某言：伏奉诰命，除臣端明殿学士，仍赐对衣、金带、鞍马者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221061_comment'></div>图书秘殿，既假借于隆名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221061_comment'></div>车服徽章，复叨尘于异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221061_comment'></div>抗辞莫避，抚己难胜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221061_comment'></div>伏念臣患难馀生，离奇朽质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221061_comment'></div>荜门圭窦，敢希清切之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221061_comment'></div>布褐柴车，岂有轻肥之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221061_comment'></div>敢谓圣神之眷，不忘孤远之踪，赉与所加，官师知劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221061_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下天地况施，日月照临，智先成务之几，仁得亲贤之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221061_comment'></div>过形褒诏，深察厚诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221061_comment'></div>既隶职于禁庭，复宣威于巨屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221061_comment'></div>举兹宠渥，并及罔功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221061_comment'></div>臣敢不仰体眷私，益思策厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221061_comment'></div>考惟德其物之义，弥谨临深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221061_comment'></div>遵循名责实之方，稍图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221061_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1221061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月</a>　充端明殿学士江东安抚大使，知建康府、兼寿春府，滁濠庐州无为军宣抚使，有谢宰相表。作品：知建康府谢宰相启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（乾道二年(1166)宣州改为宁国府。）</span><div id='poem_1221147' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221147' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221147?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知建康府谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221147")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221147_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221147'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221147'>入陪从列，谬参八座之联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221147_comment'></div>出领藩条，连委十城之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221147_comment'></div>顾惭疏拙，积冒宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221147_comment'></div>窃以江左名区，金陵会府，兼河山表里之势，号股肱藩辅之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221147_comment'></div>虎踞龙蟠，徒仰帝王之宅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221147_comment'></div>蜂旗虎幄，既为战伐之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221147_comment'></div>群偷屯结而未闻荡定之方，百姓流离而曾乏招怀之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221147_comment'></div>非得迈伦之士，曷收经世之勋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221147_comment'></div>如某者，质本驽骀，学惟糟粕，奋身一介，受任三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221147_comment'></div>第知直道以事君，所愧矫情而镇物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221147_comment'></div>夤缘遭遇，寖冒使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221147_comment'></div>此盖伏遇仆射相公功业冠乎古今，忠信行乎蛮貊，既隆宽而博爱，亦公听而并观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221147_comment'></div>舟楫济川，坐弭风波之险；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221147_comment'></div>盐梅调鼎，曲成品物之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221147_comment'></div>致是迂愚，有兹侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221147_comment'></div>某敢不仰遵庙算，俯究民情，外图疆埸之事几，内访闾阎之疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221147_comment'></div>上酬洪造，次答己知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221147_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月22日</a>　在宣州，朝廷拣张崇军精锐隶属李光，建康屯驻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月24日</a>　在宣州太平州军士陆德军变，李光遣兵捕之。<br /></div>

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f142b4974abf4621b7a7a1637f5c4db0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f142b4974abf4621b7a7a1637f5c4db0");'><span id='f142b4974abf4621b7a7a1637f5c4db0_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月21日</a>　在临安升右文殿修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年9月5日</a>　在临安充徽猷阁待制、知临安府。作品：谢除徽猷阁待制表。<div id='poem_1221057' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221057' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221057?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除徽猷阁待制表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年9月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221057")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221057_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221057'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221057'>臣某言：伏奉告命，除臣徽猷阁待制、知临安军府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221057_comment'></div>寻具辞免，奉圣旨不允，臣已望阙祗受讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221057_comment'></div>南国分符，已窃江乡之守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221057_comment'></div>西清庀职，更参禁掖之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221057_comment'></div>自惭疏贱之踪，有此遭逢之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221057_comment'></div>宠繇上出，感自中深<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221057_comment'></div>窃惟内阁之深严，实宝先朝之谟训，凡预论思之列，必求文学之良，宜得英才，当兹妙简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221057_comment'></div>如臣者，起从寒苦，备历险艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221057_comment'></div>释陇亩锄耰之勤，守简编铅椠之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221057_comment'></div>彯缨入仕，但知移孝以为忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221057_comment'></div>捧檄当官，已分忘家而徇国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221057_comment'></div>惟坚死节，岂暇全身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221057_comment'></div>顷力守于孤城，乃横当于彊寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221057_comment'></div>外乏蚍蜉之援，旁婴貔虎之群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221057_comment'></div>集众苦于一身，脱馀生于九死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221057_comment'></div>岂期末路，更践清涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221057_comment'></div>既升次对之班，复玷藩宣之寄，靡容逊避，第切兢危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221057_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下大度兼容，英谋独断，得驾御群材之术，有奠安四海之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221057_comment'></div>遂使衰迟，有兹侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221057_comment'></div>臣敢不益图后效，期称深恩！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221057_comment'></div>职列从官，献替敢拘于内外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221057_comment'></div>身为屏蔽，糜捐誓矢于死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221057_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1221057_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年9月22日</a>　到临安府任。作品：谢知临安府到任表。<div id='poem_1221058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知临安府到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年9月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221058")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221058'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221058'>臣某言：准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除臣徽猷阁待制、知临安军府事，臣已具辞免职名外，先于九月二十二日到任交割职事讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221058_comment'></div>分符宛水，曾无善最之称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221058_comment'></div>易守武林，叠冒藩宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221058_comment'></div>思欲上宽于忧顾，惟知自竭于糜捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221058_comment'></div>祗拜恩荣，弥深惕厉<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221058_comment'></div>伏念臣受才刚拙，涉世迂愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221058_comment'></div>寡与多仇，久处众嫌之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221058_comment'></div>孤立一意，独持自信之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221058_comment'></div>顷守孤城，数遭巨寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221058_comment'></div>赖朝廷之威令，遣兵将以扫除，一境再生，全家免祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221058_comment'></div>尽出乾坤之造，曾何丝发之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221058_comment'></div>方自愧于罔功，乃并叨于异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221058_comment'></div>进陪从列，移守名邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221058_comment'></div>惟吴会之要冲，望銮舆于咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221058_comment'></div>甲兵刓弊，城邑荒墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221058_comment'></div>当凋残煨烬之馀，继卤莽灭裂之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221058_comment'></div>有民人社稷，既常为退遁之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221058_comment'></div>无甲胄盖藏，何以称拊绥之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221058_comment'></div>倘非健吏，曷整颓纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221058_comment'></div>夫岂懦庸，可胜委任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221058_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下斡旋鸿化，总揽乾纲，举法度而赏罚明，判忠邪而真伪核。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221058_comment'></div>遂使至愚之品，每膺过分之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221058_comment'></div>臣敢不肃整营屯，抚循流寓，使屏翰之防稍备，庶警跸之卫加严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221058_comment'></div>少期岁月之淹，获展涓埃之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221058_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1221058_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月3日</a>　在临安，除知洪州，固辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月8日</a>　在临安，提举临安府洞霄宫。作品：除宫祠谢表。<div id='poem_1221059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除宫祠谢表<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年1月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221059")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221059_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1221059_0'>① 绍兴元年正月八日被旨，移守豫章，以疾乞宫祠，蒙恩差提举临安府洞霄宫。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221059'>抱疾呼天，敢避再三之渎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221059_comment'></div>施仁及物，迄蒙宽大之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221059_comment'></div>绎藩方捍御之劳，遂祠馆便安之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221059_comment'></div>退循侥倖，深切凌兢<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221059_comment'></div>伏念臣涉世迂愚，禀生艰苦，勇忘量力，智昧周身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221059_comment'></div>蚤日涖官，粗励羔羊之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221059_comment'></div>频年出守，横当画鹖之群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221059_comment'></div>积是惊忧，几成委顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221059_comment'></div>念平时徇难，虽肝脑之可捐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221059_comment'></div>今兹祈閒，实筋骸之难强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221059_comment'></div>力陈愚悃，仰叩至慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221059_comment'></div>幸洪造之矜从，抚危衷而感慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221059_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下乾坤博施，日月照临，于人何所不容，无物不得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221059_comment'></div>遂令衰惫，稍获安全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221059_comment'></div>小智易殚，况有负薪之疾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221059_comment'></div>大恩莫报，徒存结草之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221059_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221059_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='165b5003e6b342129e21f098a12a54e7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("165b5003e6b342129e21f098a12a54e7");'><span id='165b5003e6b342129e21f098a12a54e7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1132')">1131-1132年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='165b5003e6b342129e21f098a12a54e7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月28日</a>　在临安，擢吏部侍郎，上辞免状。作品：辞免吏部侍郎状。<div id='poem_1220985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免吏部侍郎状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年9月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220985")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220985'>臣十月二日准尚书省劄子，九月二十八日三省同奉圣旨，除臣吏部侍郎，令乘递马疾速前来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220985_comment'></div>臣闻命震恐，罔知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220985_comment'></div>伏念臣禀性拙艰，承学固陋，幸遭旦暮之遇，得效驰驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220985_comment'></div>比自宫祠，更守近郡，携孥到任，曾未浃旬，敢谓误恩，有此除授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220985_comment'></div>退循谫薄，弥切兢凌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220985_comment'></div>况天官剧曹，素号雄选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220985_comment'></div>吏奸而莫究其弊，官冗而未知所澄，非得刚明之才，曷振颓靡之习？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220985_comment'></div>如臣庸懦，岂敢冒居！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220985_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐追寝成命，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220985_comment'></div>臣已于当日交割职事与以次官，一面起发迤逦至前路听候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220985_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220985_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎，上疏极论朋党之害。作品：乞车驾亲征札子。<div id='poem_1220986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞车驾亲征劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220986")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220986'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220986'>臣闻能扶天下之危，则据天下之安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220986_comment'></div>能除天下之忧，则享天下之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220986_comment'></div>能救天下之祸，则获天下之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220986_comment'></div>故圣人不畏多难，而畏无难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220986_comment'></div>盖多难之世，怀戒惧怵惕之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220986_comment'></div>无难之世，有宴安鸩毒之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220986_comment'></div>自昔有为之君，或开创基业，或拨乱中兴，身遭艰阨，而能奋然特起者，未易概举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220986_comment'></div>以汉高之英雄，身居项王掌握中数矣，然城破复收、兵散复合，彭城之败，至推堕二子而不顾，窘亦甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220986_comment'></div>卒能灭楚以有天下者，忍小耻以成大功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220986_comment'></div>光武北徇燕蓟，困于王郎，蒙犯霜露，面背破裂，惶惑不知所之，然卒能破郎以兴汉祚者，因危难以恢帝业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220986_comment'></div>恭惟陛下以慈俭之德，当艰阨之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220986_comment'></div>维扬之变起于仓卒，人心缘此而震恐，将士因是而骄惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220986_comment'></div>近年以来，议论之臣各怀顾避，上下一律，莫肯慨然以持危扶颠为己任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220986_comment'></div>今翠华驻跸会稽，首尾三载，自去秋迄今，见敌人无复南渡之意，淮甸咫尺，了不经营，长江千里，不为限隔，惴惴然日为乘桴航海之计，谓之万全，臣所未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220986_comment'></div>以区区晋元，草创建国于基绪既绝之际，犹能立宗社，修宫阙，兴学校农桑，保有江浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220986_comment'></div>刘琨、祖逖与聪、勒拒战于并、冀、兖、豫、梁、雍诸州，未尝陷没也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220986_comment'></div>以石季龙之彊大，兵叩历阳，命王导都督中外诸军事以御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220986_comment'></div>周世宗当五代之末，取淮南，攻陇右，下三关，皆御军亲行，威震远近，未闻专主避敌之谋如今日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220986_comment'></div>况陛下英武命世，以真主之势而临金邦，以中国之尊而抗外国，天人助顺，军人士庶孰肯甘心委质，俯首帖耳，终身为污辱降敌之人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220986_comment'></div>今将非不武，兵非不众，陛下傥整兵顺动，则箪食壶浆以迎王师者，袂相属也，患在陛下无其志耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220986_comment'></div>臣愚欲望陛下明诏三省、密院大臣，分令将士守御江津，力为保境之谋，徐决亲征之策，庶几经略中原，渐谋兴复，以副海内生灵颙颙之望，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220986_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1220986_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。奏论朝廷追罢“金人入境，各州府或守或避，令得自便”诏书。作品：乞追罢守臣迁避诏书札子。<div id='poem_1220987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞追罢守臣迁避诏书劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220987")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220987'>臣顷守宣城，准枢密院劄子，建炎三年六月十二日奉圣旨：「金人入境，多是因敌就粮，深入内地，致使吾民重遭涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220987_comment'></div>令逐州府守臣与当职官共议，或守或避，各得自便」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220987_comment'></div>臣仰见陛下忧悯元元、开示宽大之意可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220987_comment'></div>臣窃谓守土之臣，朝廷委以人民社稷之重，固当存亡以之，若预开迁避之门，则人心携贰，亦无肯固守者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220987_comment'></div>臣观百姓安土重迁，非谓其愚无知也，亦其势不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220987_comment'></div>盖富者少而贫者多，所资以生养者，不过日求衣食之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220987_comment'></div>居于山者则有樵采之利，居于泽者则有网罟之利，都邑之民则尽智于交易，田野之民则竭力于垄亩，皆相资以为生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220987_comment'></div>今使转而之他，则是数者皆失其本业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220987_comment'></div>将坐而资于官乎，数万之众，力固不足以给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220987_comment'></div>如此，非独老弱转乎沟壑，虽强且壮者固不免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220987_comment'></div>朝廷设官分职，凡以为民，若使列郡各得择地迁避，大者不过全其帑藏，小者不过保其妻孥而已，此于百姓何所利哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220987_comment'></div>臣之区区，诚愿陛下申敕诸郡，修城池，备器械，积刍粟，聚人民，力为固守之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220987_comment'></div>有望风逆降弃城者，皆严立法禁，责以必死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220987_comment'></div>大者保境，小者守城，敌人虽复长驱，岂能遽窥行在如前日乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220987_comment'></div>臣愚伏望陛下速降指挥，追罢三年六月诏书，慨然责以大义，命将帅遣戍役力，为保境之谋，庶几列郡闻风有所畏惮，实天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220987_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1220987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。高宗欲移跸临安，李光被旨节制临安府见屯诸军，兼户部侍郎、督营缮事。李光上奏移跸事务。作品：乞戒约苛敛状。<div id='poem_1220988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞戒约苛敛状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220988")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220988'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220988'>臣契勘移跸事务，不免科扰临安府及傍近诸郡，如竹木等物，盖有不获已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220988_comment'></div>今来不住体访得诸邑及严州等处，更有转运司科派下供应班直木炭藁荐万数浩瀚，初不曾被受朝廷指挥，以此道路传播，颇属骚扰，深为未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220988_comment'></div>缘臣使事止是总领本府，其傍近诸郡，难以会问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220988_comment'></div>伏望圣慈作访闻行下，严赐约束，庶几少革苛敛之风，仰副陛下仁俭之意，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220988_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1220988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。上奏蠲减二浙赋税。作品：乞蠲二浙积欠札子。<div id='poem_1220993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞蠲二浙积欠劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220993")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220993'>臣伏见近年以来，国运艰难，中原板荡，陛下驻跸东南，乘舆、服御悉务减省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220993_comment'></div>而百司兵众，皆仰给于二浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220993_comment'></div>加以今日营缮所须，一毫以上，皆出民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220993_comment'></div>师旅饥馑之后，斗米千钱，民虽凋弊，罔有怨词，深可怜悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220993_comment'></div>臣愚伏望圣慈因今移跸之后，稍留宽大之泽，以慰人心，应二浙积负一切蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220993_comment'></div>臣契勘临安九邑，科配比它郡最为烦并，其折变小麦，为害尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220993_comment'></div>及去年残零税赋，见今转运司责限催纳，其数至微，欲望特与释放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220993_comment'></div>昨缘前知府孙觌将义仓米于正税外，更有折糙米二斗五升，仓场受纳，复增至一石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220993_comment'></div>又有钞旁公吏，乞觅不下一二千，及每岁和买，州县既不曾支与价钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220993_comment'></div>今闻本府每匹更令纳见钱四百文足，谓之縻费钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220993_comment'></div>窃虑行之既久，遂为永例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220993_comment'></div>诸县因军马经由，支过系省钱斛，多不肯豁除，坊场亏欠课利，委非侵欺，无缘补发，而官吏欲假此骚扰，时一举行，追呼捕逮，谓之干照钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220993_comment'></div>县官无所从出，止是剥民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220993_comment'></div>如斯苛细，望悉蠲除，庶几小民蒙被实惠，仰副陛下勤恤民隐之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220993_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220993_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月3日</a>　在临安，兼权侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。论勿以多杀为功而以招纳为本。作品：论招降盗贼札子。<div id='poem_1220996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论招降盗贼劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220996")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220996'>臣闻之《书》曰：「火炎昆冈，玉石俱焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220996_comment'></div>天吏逸德，烈于猛火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220996_comment'></div>歼厥渠魁，胁从罔治」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220996_comment'></div>太祖皇帝创业之初，盖用此道，故能混一区宇，平定天下，其本在乎得民心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220996_comment'></div>国家自靖康以来，因金人内逼，百姓失业，无所得食，弱者转徙乎沟壑，强者结集为寇盗，固非有雠主嫉上之心，特出于不得已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220996_comment'></div>若抚循有道，驾驭得术，因其讴吟思叹之心，广开招怀抚纳之路，民皆吾民，土皆吾土，则陛下建立中兴之功，不啻若反掌之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220996_comment'></div>今曹成、张用、李宏、马友、刘忠、孔彦舟之徒，各拥众数万，跨州连邑，荆土骚然，比之敌人，尚可以游说动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220996_comment'></div>况祖宗德泽在人，陛下宽仁得众，倘能降咫尺之诏，遣一介之使，布宣王灵，开示德意，又以实利及之，彼不为我用，尚何为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220996_comment'></div>臣观自古创业中兴之君，未有不藉此属而能得天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220996_comment'></div>汉与楚大战彭城不利，隋何说黥布发兵背楚，卒灭项王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220996_comment'></div>关西号光武为铜马帝，正以受降群贼耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220996_comment'></div>魏武得黄巾三十万众，遂定中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220996_comment'></div>今朝廷兵力寡弱，议者乃谓盗贼不可保恃，持必杀之说，臣所未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220996_comment'></div>自李成破败北走，刘豫群盗稍稍革心，倘因斯时显用一二酋豪，以风厉党类，必递相歆艳，以次归降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220996_comment'></div>伏望陛下断自圣心，因孟庾、韩世忠出使，谕以此意，勿以多杀为功，而以招纳为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220996_comment'></div>仍乞别选漕臣一二员，下荆湖之粟，专切应副粮食，汰其老弱以散处淮甸，收其精勇以防守江津，蔽遮金人，兴复中土，是谓一举而两得也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1220996_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月26日</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。令节制临安府内外诸军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。奏论行宫营缮。作品：乞裁减营缮行宫状。乞免住罢行宫营缮状。乞罢营缮添支状。<div id='poem_1220990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞裁减营缮行宫状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220990")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220990'>臣昨准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨遣臣先至临安府节制本府人兵，及总领移跸事务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220990_comment'></div>臣到本府踰旬，与漕臣宋辉、徐康国及知临安府席益以次僚属协力干办，稍见次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220990_comment'></div>臣契勘行宫殿宇，元奉指挥，合依徐康国所上图策，以一百间为率，士大夫传诵，皆仰服陛下深自贬损、爱惜民力之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220990_comment'></div>臣今体访不住承准内降御宝营造去处，非元图所载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220990_comment'></div>窃虑两漕臣及临安应办过当，辇致木植，追呼夫匠，无有已时，前日所降敕榜戒约，殆为虚文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220990_comment'></div>臣今欲望陛下应合增修起造去处，令臣预知，或有过当，许臣执奏，庶几上体陛下恭俭之德，下宽九邑凋瘵之民，实天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220990_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220990_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免住罢行宫营缮状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220991")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220991'>臣近准省劄：「奉圣旨，今防秋戒期，建康府修内可罢封桩，所降钱别听指挥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220991_comment'></div>臣除已恭依即日住罢外，窃缘臣所造正殿、寝殿、两廊、殿门等处，各已毕工，独别殿壅舍双门既已立木，惟结瓦未了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220991_comment'></div>工役已多，若便住罢，窃虑暴露风雨，枉坏材植，他日之费必倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220991_comment'></div>未审合与不合逐旋搭盖结瓦，更合取自圣裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220991_comment'></div>况今农事将隙，自有添差通判吴师直专领营缮，与臣防秋职任自不相妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220991_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1220991'><span class='label'>按：</span>九月十一日，三省同奉圣旨：「依已降指挥，日下住罢，其已立木并见在材植，并如法遮盖，不得损坏。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1220991_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1220992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢营缮添支状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220992")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220992_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220992'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220992'>准尚书省劄子：「发运副使宋辉等劄子：『承降下添修擗截行宫所画一，除修内司兵近已奉十一月二十一日圣旨，许每日支破食钱一百文外，所有壕寨监修部役，催促物料、点检医药饭食、监门等官，每日往来监辖工作，分头部役，委是勤劳，即未有许支食钱指挥』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220992_comment'></div>已奉圣旨，自都壕寨官日支一贯，至白身尅择官日支三百文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220992_comment'></div>凡三十一员，以月计之，共支钱五百馀贯，须至奏闻」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220992_comment'></div>右臣契勘，今来诸营造已见次第，不出岁前，可以毕工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220992_comment'></div>今上项监修官已有本身请给，又有券钱，今又添支逐日食钱，委是太优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220992_comment'></div>窃虑缘此妄作名目，多方迁延，未见了日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220992_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈特降睿旨，除军营席屋外，其行宫百司并限绍兴二年正月初五日已前结局，更不添支食钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220992_comment'></div>如此，非独大驾移跸有期，亦足少革妄滥之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220992_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1220992_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年12月4日</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。奏请复东南诸郡湖田。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。奏论前知临安府孙觌在任赃污不法。作品：论孙觌札子。<div id='poem_1220999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论孙觌劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220999")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220999'>臣伏睹绍兴元年十二月十四日三省同奉圣旨，备坐祖宗旧制，应赃吏决杖配诸州牢城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220999_comment'></div>盖谓军兴之际，不免时有科率，若更容纵赃吏并缘为奸，则民力愈弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220999_comment'></div>此有以见陛下意在生灵，深疾贪污，命下之日，孰不相庆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220999_comment'></div>今已累月，而诸司按察官循习既久，恬不为怪，遂使朝廷美意委为空文，臣窃痛愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220999_comment'></div>伏自艰难以来，朝廷一切姑务涵贷，凶贪之徒割剥生灵，无所忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220999_comment'></div>况朝廷行法当自贵近始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220999_comment'></div>臣伏见前知临安府孙觌在任赃污不法，远近播传，诸司惧其一旦复用，则为己害，不敢按发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220999_comment'></div>觌之为人，朝廷所知，前后臣僚论列，罪大恶稔，至辱詈君父，甚于仇雠，有臣子所不忍闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220999_comment'></div>陛下贷而不诛，又使复典郡寄，于觌恩高厚矣，乃不悛革，益肆无赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220999_comment'></div>到任之初，以军期为名，拘九邑县令在府，勒令出钱共四万伍千馀缗，名曰助军，不附文历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220999_comment'></div>又将亲信使臣毛汝能辟为都监，文林郎毛圭权钱塘县令，令二人提领本府应干仓场库务，偷盗转易，不可稽考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220999_comment'></div>郡中官僚相顾侧目，至有「人生五马贵，莫受二毛侵」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220999_comment'></div>临安府捉获酤卖私酒百姓，其家富厚，觌令圭受钱一千贯，更不解送所司，至帖下本县，直行放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220999_comment'></div>又遣所亲姓董人，乞觅过新城县百姓唐邦臣等钱一千伍百贯，皆有迹状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220999_comment'></div>除代之后，将犒赏金银钱物与都吏专知官等分受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220999_comment'></div>比至得替，其公库供帐之物，并不发还，及将空名度牒官告等移易妄用，收附不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220999_comment'></div>监司往来，厚加结纳，每到发送馈，谓之合食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220999_comment'></div>日事燕游，每会不下百馀千，以此上下相蒙，无缘显露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220999_comment'></div>伏望圣慈奋发乾刚，出自睿断，送大理寺，或差台官一员就府置司体究，候赃證分明，捕逮送狱，依法断遣，以警具僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220999_comment'></div>其属邑县令及人吏等迫于威势者，赃非入己，或许其自首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220999_comment'></div>庶几远近闻风，咸知畏戢，实天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220999_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1220999_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在临安任吏部侍郎。李纲有书信与李光。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月5日</a>　在临安，擢吏部尚书。作品：除吏部尚书谢表。<div id='poem_1221060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除吏部尚书谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年2月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221060")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221060'>职列贰卿，方惧黜幽之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221060_comment'></div>位联八座，亟蒙图旧之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221060_comment'></div>趣就列以惟恭，愧循墙而莫避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221060_comment'></div>宠由上锡，感自中深<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221060_comment'></div>伏念臣赋性迂愚，受才疏拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221060_comment'></div>孤立一意，独持自信之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221060_comment'></div>寡偶少徒，久处众嫌之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221060_comment'></div>虽殚千虑，无补万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221060_comment'></div>仅遵唱注之规，蔑著品题之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221060_comment'></div>乏山涛之识量，讵能激浊以扬清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221060_comment'></div>匪毛玠之公方，何以正身而励俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221060_comment'></div>仰荷非常之遇，终怀不称之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221060_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下盛德日跻，至仁天覆，能知人有尧之哲，不求备得汤之宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221060_comment'></div>知臣有忠于所事之诚，察臣无善自为谋之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221060_comment'></div>老更世故，粗饬官箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221060_comment'></div>未忍弃捐，俾膺奖擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221060_comment'></div>臣敢不益思砥砺，谨守纲条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221060_comment'></div>方圣君尝胆之时，敢怀持禄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221060_comment'></div>惟臣子致身之义，期在捐躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221060_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1221060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月12日</a>　在临安，为淮西招抚使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月21日</a>　在临安，任淮西招抚使，自行在出发。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5f7ca6bf80784668ba3dd754a7b5ab17_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5f7ca6bf80784668ba3dd754a7b5ab17");'><span id='5f7ca6bf80784668ba3dd754a7b5ab17_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>，59岁</div><div id='5f7ca6bf80784668ba3dd754a7b5ab17' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月</a>　在临安任礼部尚书，有诗送廖刚知漳州。作品：送廖用中侍郎知漳州。<div id='poem_527733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送廖用中侍郎知漳州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527733")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527733_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527733'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527733'>羡君忠孝两无亏，出处雍容自造微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527733'>供帐都门疏受去，怀章郡邸买臣归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527733'>君恩已荷全家饱，治绩行看百姓肥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527733'>回首文昌旧游地，相从渐觉故人稀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527733'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527733_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年3月1日</a>　兼权刑部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　在临安府任礼部尚书兼权刑部尚书，临安府多火灾，李光奏论处置事宜。作品：论火灾状。<div id='poem_1221004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论火灾状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221004")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221004'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221004'>臣近权刑部职事，今月二日准尚书省劄子，备坐臣僚章疏论临安府回禄之警，一月之内，火凡数作，焚艺之家，通及千馀，乞申严昨降指挥，以凌迟处死治放火者，仍乞下密院劄付沿流州军密行捕捉等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221004_comment'></div>三月十四日，三省同奉圣旨依奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221004_comment'></div>臣之区区，窃有可疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221004_comment'></div>臣闻尧以水为儆予，汤以大旱而罪己，未闻尽归之于他人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221004_comment'></div>自昔火灾之变，上应天道，盖荧惑徘回斗牛之间久矣，牛斗，吴分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221004_comment'></div>又南方之性察，陛下宜思所以致火之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221004_comment'></div>朝政之阙失，臣下之奸邪，赋役之重，民不聊生，流亡者多，百姓失业，州县之吏或倚法而恣赃贪，囹圄之间或受赇而多枉滥，有一于此，皆足致灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221004_comment'></div>今议者曾不恤此，方峻刑以治失火之家，缘及官司舍屋，皆付之极典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221004_comment'></div>夫奸细固所当治也，而失火之家盖有不幸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221004_comment'></div>臣恐淫刑滥罪，横及无辜，非陛下遇灾恐惧脩省之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221004_comment'></div>兼沿流州军讥察细奸，自有约束，今乃使之各察放火之家，则是硫黄发烛千里而随身矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221004_comment'></div>臣愚伏望圣慈止行下临安府，令督责在城兵官，各认地分，如有违犯，重寘典宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221004_comment'></div>所有今来已得圣旨指挥，臣未行出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221004_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1221004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221004'><span class='label'>御笔：</span>前降指挥更不施行。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221004_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　在临安府任礼部尚书兼权刑部尚书，言检会祖宗故事进呈事。作品：乞委官节录封事札子。<div id='poem_1221005' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221005' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221005?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞委官节录封事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221005")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221005_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221005'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221005'>臣恭闻陛下因城内火灾，惕然恐惧，延问近臣，忧形于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221005_comment'></div>乃发德音、下明诏，以求直言，此甚盛之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221005_comment'></div>陛下自即位以来，数遭变故，仓卒之际，即下求言之诏，勤勤恳恳，发于至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221005_comment'></div>然玩岁阅月，国势日削，邻敌日强，盗贼益炽，百姓益穷，天地之变，水旱为灾，星辰失度，寒暑反时，此岂盛德之报也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221005_comment'></div>臣意陛下有求言之名，而无听言之实故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221005_comment'></div>今艰难之时，愤激献忠者当累及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221005_comment'></div>臣窃虑封事之多，未易省览，不免壅积，是徒为文具而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221005_comment'></div>臣伏见仁祖时尝委张方平、司马光详定中外所上封事，尽心料简，合于义理可施行者，虽文采不足，一一奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221005_comment'></div>光与方平亦尝奏乞，其间识虑稍出于众，开陈政体，文理详明者，乞赐召对，面加询访，果有可采，藉其姓名，随才擢用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221005_comment'></div>今中原士大夫辐辏东南，所献封事，岂无公论？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221005_comment'></div>臣愚伏望圣慈检会祖宗故事，专委侍从官二员，择其公忠端亮者，俾之遴选，据所可取者节录成册，每季或逐月进呈，以备乙夜之览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221005_comment'></div>忠言嘉谟，庶有裨益，以仰副陛下恐惧修省艰难求助之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1221005_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年3月</a>　在临安府任礼部尚书兼权刑部尚书，有诗送张致远。作品：送张子猷给事帅福唐。<div id='poem_527730' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527730' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527730?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张子猷给事帅福唐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527730")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527730_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527730'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527730'>五马东来隘里闾，旌旗照海奉安舆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527730'>时危未暇宽徭役，岁歉无劳进羡馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527730'>赤子弄兵先解散，乌衣侮法费驱除。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527730'>兵戈满眼瞻王室，邮传时时附谏书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527730'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527730_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　在临安府任礼部尚书兼权刑部尚书，为张元干伯父励作墓志铭。作品：宋中奉大夫集英殿修撰张公墓志铭。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e3cb46cd25034b18bc427a929fb9fa01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e3cb46cd25034b18bc427a929fb9fa01");'><span id='e3cb46cd25034b18bc427a929fb9fa01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1139')">1138-1139年</a>，61-62岁</div><div id='e3cb46cd25034b18bc427a929fb9fa01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月7日</a>　在临安，除参知政事，上谢表。作品：辞免参知政事札子。<div id='poem_1221022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221022?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免参知政事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221022")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221022'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221022'>臣骤闻宠命，惊惧交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221022_comment'></div>伏念臣学术孤陋，智识浅短，汩没州县簿领之间，消铄风波危辱之地，年龄衰晚，志气凋落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221022_comment'></div>比蒙召自遐方，还寘近列，曾无古人正色献替之效，莫副陛下虚怀延伫之勤，昼夜以思，未知称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221022_comment'></div>况今朝廷艰难之际，敌使在疆，国论恟恟，上欲慰陛下怀念父母罔极之思，下欲不沮海内忠臣义士之气，则夫今日处庙堂之上，从容求济，顾不难哉，岂臣愚憃所能克堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221022_comment'></div>今旧德老成、俊乂之士布列内外，其间望实出臣之右者甚众，舍而不求，乃此虚授，倘或冒处，必致颠危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221022_comment'></div>伏望圣慈悯怜孤踪，特赐追寝成命，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221022_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1221022_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月7日</a>　在临安，除参知政事，再上谢表。作品：辞免除参知政事表。<div id='poem_1221067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除参知政事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221067")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221067'>臣某言：准尚书劄子，奉圣旨除臣参知政事，寻具辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221067_comment'></div>伏蒙圣恩，特降诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221067_comment'></div>需章沥恳，冀安分义之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221067_comment'></div>诏旨屡颁，仍示延登之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221067_comment'></div>愚衷既竭，渊听未回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221067_comment'></div>重干咫尺之威，敢避再三之渎<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221067_comment'></div>伏念臣以凡庸之品，遭特达之知，虽久冒于使令，无可称之绩效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221067_comment'></div>周旋八郡，荏苒十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221067_comment'></div>帅阃总戎，已叨重寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221067_comment'></div>天官率属，复拜异恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221067_comment'></div>阅岁月之浸深，乏涓尘之可补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221067_comment'></div>顾兹忝窃，方惧谴呵，不图骤玷于圣知，更使参陪于政路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221067_comment'></div>负且乘足以致寇，名与器岂以假人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221067_comment'></div>敢自爱于捐躯，实深虞于误国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221067_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下思用人之贤否，实为国之重轻，特寝误恩，追还成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221067_comment'></div>誓坚犬马之志，仰酬天地之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221067_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月7日</a>　在临安，除参知政事，三上谢表。作品：除参知政事谢表。<div id='poem_1221068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除参知政事谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221068")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221068'>臣某言：伏奉告命，除授臣左中大夫、参知政事、封赐如故，寻具辞免，伏蒙圣恩，特降中使赐臣不允批答，仍断来章者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221068_comment'></div>天听甚高，虽牢辞而莫获；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221068_comment'></div>令行弗反，趣就列以惟恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221068_comment'></div>祗服宠灵，不胜感惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221068_comment'></div>伏念臣性资愚蠢，问学空疏，立朝惟信于朴忠，涉世几成于强聒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221068_comment'></div>更州县簿书之职，遍台省清切之司，誉不足偿谤讟之言，功岂能掩罪累之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221068_comment'></div>方俟瘝官之谴，敢期共政之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221068_comment'></div>幸出非常，分诚匪据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221068_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下德参化育，明极照临，人无同异而并包，材有短长而并用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221068_comment'></div>察臣粗知于体国，念臣素拙于谋身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221068_comment'></div>忘其凡庸，超至严近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221068_comment'></div>臣敢不义之与比，知无不为，感千载之遭逢，戒一时之侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221068_comment'></div>居其位、食其禄，固当尽大臣事君之谊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221068_comment'></div>视所以、观所由，庶无负明主知人之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221068_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1221068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月19日</a>　在临安府任参知政事，言月桩钱之害、常平之利，奏罢常平主管官。作品：论诸路月桩之弊札子。小帖子。<div id='poem_1221016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221016?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论诸路月桩之弊劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221016")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221016'>臣契勘诸路月桩，最为民间重害，而江东西为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221016_comment'></div>元降指挥取拨应干上供封桩，诸司并州县等不以有无拘碍，上供经制酒税课利及漕司移用等钱桩办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221016_comment'></div>如此，州县尚自应办不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221016_comment'></div>今江南路漕司，往往将移用等钱于逐州主管司专委通判拘收，不许取拨，遂致民不堪命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221016_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿者，行下诸路，应有月桩钱，并许将诸色钱桩办，如有馀，方许漕司拘收，庶几垄亩之民，不至失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221016_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221016_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1221016'>〔小贴子〕契勘诸路月桩钱，当时守臣不量民力，有承认偏重去处，重为民害，如抚、信二州是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221016_comment'></div>欲望圣慈行下诸路漕司，将逐州每岁所敷，不得辄有轻重，以伤民力。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1221016_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月23日</a>　在临安府任参知政事，因李光弹劾，贾和仲罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月25日</a>　在临安府任参知政事，秦桧等议国书事，对和议之策，李光默然。绍兴和议遂成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月25日</a>　在临安府任参知政事，有诗悼傅崧卿。作品：十二月二十五日诗悼傅子骏给事。<div id='poem_527731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十二月二十五日诗悼傅子骏给事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527731")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527731'>归寻北海桥边路，恸哭斯人但故庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527731'>三径空存陶令菊，万签难见邺侯书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527731'>丹青写照空留影，慷慨论文孰起予。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527731'>叹息平生英妙气，只今寂寞契真如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月</a>　在临安府任参知政事，以金人来和大赦天下，赦文布告天下。张浚移书泰发、孙近痛陈议和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月14日</a>　在临安府任参知政事，杨炜上书于泰发，论和议事，责李光附时相，隳大节。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月</a>　在临安府任参知政事，向子諲致仕归隐芗林，筑企疏堂。李光题诗。作品：为向伯恭题。<div id='poem_527576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为向伯恭题</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527576")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527576'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527576'>向公天下士，慷慨有祖风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527576'>亦复对行殿，密议裨天聪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527576'>君臣意气合，每进尝从容。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527576'>飘飘青云志，顾肯贪天功。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527576'>荣涂拂衣归，安坐芗林中。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527576'>作堂榜企疏，进退聊比踪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527576'>父老非故乡，何必囊金空。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527576'>俗轨竞奔驰，世路方尚同。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527576'>善为子孙谋，但务田园丰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527576'>伟哉此二子，遐举希冥鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527576'>富贵如浮云，声名压岱嵩。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527576'>千载继者谁，我友向伯恭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527576'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_527576_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年9月5日</a>　在临安府任参知政事，秦桧请以郑亿年为显谟阁直学士，李光于榻前面折而止。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安，罢参知政事，上乞罢奏疏。作品：乞罢政札子。乞罢政第二札子。辞免除职事与郡札子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（罢职后，诏除资政殿学士，知绍兴府。李光不受。）</span>《小帖子》两篇。<div id='poem_1221026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢政第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年12月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221026")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221026'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221026'>臣昨者辄露恳诚，乞罢机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221026_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈特遣中使押赴随班奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221026_comment'></div>进退跼蹐，心神靡宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221026_comment'></div>臣窃谓大臣以道事君，不可则止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221026_comment'></div>所谓大臣，必能振举朝纲，肃清中外，生杀利害、赏庆刑威之权归之人主，礼乐征伐必自天子出，然后为称其职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221026_comment'></div>今臣猥以凡庸，久窃重任，拱手循默，一无所为，可谓失其职甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221026_comment'></div>臣于此时若不自引去，是知其不可而不止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221026_comment'></div>重念臣顷遭陛下，更历中外，十稔于兹，怨仇满路，孤踪易摇，患难风波，何所不有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221026_comment'></div>独蒙陛下保全，以至今日，擢参大政，日享厚禄，恩荣上及于父祖，饱煖下逮于妻孥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221026_comment'></div>臣殒首碎胸，何以论报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221026_comment'></div>若复党蔽雷同，不为陛下振举职守，陛下一旦觉悟，则欺君罔上之罪，尚何所逃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221026_comment'></div>故臣欲及陛下未至厌薄，同列未至倾挤，乞臣残骸，退伏田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221026_comment'></div>伏望陛下哀悯孤踪，诚出迫切，特许臣解罢职任，除臣宫祠差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221026_comment'></div>臣倘未死亡，尚期图报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221026_comment'></div>冒渎天威，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1221026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年12月23日</a>　在临安，李光属官刘一止、周葵并罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。宫祀，作吴升墓志铭。作品：左承议郎吴君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1221202' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221202' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221202?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左承议郎吴君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221202")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221202_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221202'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221202'>君姓吴氏，讳升，字潜道，明之鄞人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221202_comment'></div>曾祖德，祖泽，皆隐德不耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221202_comment'></div>父渭，以君登朝，累赠宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221202_comment'></div>君九岁而孤，母守志鞠养，稍长，告以汝父长者，尝拊汝，当为儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221202_comment'></div>君因发愤读书，昼夜不息，遂博通经史，下笔为文，简而有法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221202_comment'></div>元丰间朝廷以经术取士，君两预乡荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221202_comment'></div>大观己丑遂中进士第，释褐授迪功郎，主宣之泾县簿，摄水阳镇，郡太守累称其贤而未荐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221202_comment'></div>或曰：「盍求之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221202_comment'></div>君曰：「彼知我而不能荐，我为下寮，不求为可知，二者胥失也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221202_comment'></div>考满，丞温之乐清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221202_comment'></div>裨赞县政而弥缝其失，政有大不便者，君力争不能得，则叹曰：「予不负丞，令长其可负百姓乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221202_comment'></div>水阳濒大江，素有水患，君去才旬日，水辄大至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221202_comment'></div>去乐清未几，巨盗窃发，焚掠殆尽，官吏多遇害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221202_comment'></div>君慨然顾谓妻子曰：「造物于我厚矣，始吾读书，姑成先志尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221202_comment'></div>今年踰六十，二子相继登科，吾尚何求哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221202_comment'></div>困挂其冠，得左宣教郎致仕以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221202_comment'></div>遇渊圣皇帝及今天子登宝位，转左承议郎，赐五品服，叙封妻史氏为孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221202_comment'></div>孺人有淑德，孝顺勤俭，能以礼法自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221202_comment'></div>夫妇白首，相待如宾，子孙侍侧，雍雍如也，人皆荣之，先君十年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221202_comment'></div>诸子卜明年庚申正月丁酉，奉君之柩合葬于四明之梅㠗，从治命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221202_comment'></div>君任真自得，遇人无贵贱贫富，一以诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221202_comment'></div>当官任职，未尝择所向，盖无入而不自得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221202_comment'></div>予与秉彝实太学同舍生，尝至其家，见君颀然而长，发鬓垂白，貌温而气清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221202_comment'></div>方精力强壮，内怀止足之计，不待及期而浩浩然勇退，虽古高人胜事，何以加之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221202_comment'></div>所居环堵，竹树萧然，家事有无，一不以介意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221202_comment'></div>晚益萧散，诸子卜居择胜，得小溪之芝山，君欣然从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221202_comment'></div>浮沈里巷间，芒鞋野服，间从方外之士，遇兴辄往，一枰之上，忘怀得失，不知岁月之老也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221202_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐，祸福利害之端，了无足以动其心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221202_comment'></div>享年八十有五，未尝有疾，一夕奄然而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221202_comment'></div>庄周所谓不刻意而高，不导引而寿者，君几是欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221202_comment'></div>生五男：长曰秉仁，四上礼部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221202_comment'></div>次秉彝，左迪功郎、枢密院计议官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221202_comment'></div>次秉礼，先君卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221202_comment'></div>次秉智，举进士未第；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221202_comment'></div>次秉信，左宣教郎、诸王宫大小教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221202_comment'></div>二女，皆嫁为士人妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221202_comment'></div>始君少时，方力学，有道士叩门，自言斋醮之夕，奏章帝所，见金字榜曰：「龟龄显裕，天锡吴升」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221202_comment'></div>其说虽幻怪不经，然退考君平生简易真率，而得数之多，子孙之盛，若非偶然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221202_comment'></div>秉彝一日与其弟秉信累然衰绖，踵门泣而言曰：「先君潜德退节，仕不究其禄，举世无知者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221202_comment'></div>且持左奉议郎、主管台州崇道观高所为行状，请铭于予，因附以所闻，而为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1221202'>芝山峨峨水泠泠，中有隐者逃其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221202_comment'></div>少时力学通群经，老不释卷博且精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221202_comment'></div>平生所修胸中诚，持身接物心和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221202_comment'></div>忘怀得失寄一枰，遗弃轩冕浮云轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221202_comment'></div>自然寿考身康宁，何必辛苦栖岩扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221202_comment'></div>叩门道士心通灵，飞神杳眇游青冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221202_comment'></div>羽衣翩仙朝帝庭，琅函金字标龟龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221202_comment'></div>临行一念超凡情，脱然视身如邮亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221202_comment'></div>子孙蕃衍天可凭，积善衮衮生公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221202_comment'></div>刻诗同藏播芳馨，深固葱郁真佳城。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1221202_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

铜陵

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月15日</a>　元夕，过五松山。有诗呈陈志尹等诸兄。作品：归五松有作，呈陈志尹诸兄。<div id='poem_527701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>归五松有作呈陈志尹诸兄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527701")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527701'>几年辛苦厌兵间，多谢君恩肯放还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527701'>故里萧骚松竹在，流年荏苒鬓毛斑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527701'>愁多不分青春过，睡足聊欣白昼闲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527701'>况有弟兄同保社，年年携酒共浇山<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：北人以上坟为浇山。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527701'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527701_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　元夕，过池州五松山。有诗呈陈志尹等诸兄。作品：复用前韵简志尹。<div id='poem_527702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复用前韵简志尹</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527702")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527702'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527702'>已谋湖上屋三间，身退聊同倦鸟还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527702'>老去最便青箬笠，梦回空想紫宸班<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527702'>招邀山月当轩醉，结约江鸥作伴闲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527702'>赖有渊明能赋咏，悠然把酒对南山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527702'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527702'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527702_0'>⑴ 自注：斑、班字，诗人多通押，东坡《和程正辅诗》云“助我金鼎光斓斑”，再和云“他年许缀蓬莱班”。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527702_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　元夕，过池州五松山。大雪，有诗和李孚先兄。作品：今岁遇元夕于五松，连日大雪，巷陌萧然。孚先兄有诗诧灯火之盛，因成四韵。<div id='poem_527705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>今岁遇元夕于五松连日大雪巷陌萧然孚先兄有诗诧灯火之盛因成四韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527705")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527705'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527705'>里巷萧条户半扃，更无冷月挂山城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527705'>荧荧小市唯渔火，耿耿幽窗但雪声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527705'>海国此时瞻气象，端门何日睹升平。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527705'>会须一扫阴霾尽，尽放冰轮彻夜明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527705'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527705_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年2月</a>　在铜陵。二月，归乡途中有诗。作品：辛亥中春遂宫祠之请，自渔浦转山入离渚，宿化城以归，道中成鄙句。<div id='poem_527697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛亥中春遂宫祠之请自渔浦转山入离渚宿化城以归道中成鄙句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527697'>谁倩冰霜一扫空，旋烘和气转春风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
