-----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8f2e976f578c4007839f2d6455e40436_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8f2e976f578c4007839f2d6455e40436");'><span id='8f2e976f578c4007839f2d6455e40436_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>，54岁</div><div id='8f2e976f578c4007839f2d6455e40436' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月3日</a>　移知婺州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c074d3de58054828b379e171183bf33c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c074d3de58054828b379e171183bf33c");'><span id='c074d3de58054828b379e171183bf33c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>，60岁</div><div id='c074d3de58054828b379e171183bf33c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过婺州，上辞免江西安抚大使状。<div id='poem_1221017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免江西安抚大使状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221017")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221017'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221017'>臣闻命震惊，莫知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221017_comment'></div>窃以朝廷设诸路大帅，内则欲其卫王室，外则欲其御大寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221017_comment'></div>有推毂分阃之专，膺一道兵民之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221017_comment'></div>责任既重，事权匪轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221017_comment'></div>自非一时元老大臣，不以妄授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221017_comment'></div>伏念臣才力不强，智识浅暗，徒缘遭遇，躐寘近班，虽中外之备，更无事功之可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221017_comment'></div>海邦出守，亦既逾年，最绩罔闻，日虞罪衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221017_comment'></div>臣已两贡忱辞，力祈閒退，圣恩宽大，未即矜从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221017_comment'></div>念方朝廷艰危，陛下亲御戎辂之时，忠义之士，孰不思自奋励，勉效涓埃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221017_comment'></div>如臣素受异恩，安敢择地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221017_comment'></div>实缘年龄迟暮，齿发顿衰，兼素有风眩之疾，发作无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221017_comment'></div>故虽东瓯乐易之乡，心知难强；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221017_comment'></div>而当西道连率之职，力岂胜任！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221017_comment'></div>深惧仰负陛下艰难谋帅之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221017_comment'></div>臣若贪冒宠禄，不自引避，则臣前者丐閒之章，实为矫妄，舍小图大，人言谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221017_comment'></div>伏望圣慈悯臣诚恳，检会前奏，除臣在外宫祠差遣一次，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221017_comment'></div>臣已将郡事交割与以次官，迤逦至婺州以来，听候指挥外，谨录状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221017_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作杜慎墓志铭。作品：杜府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1221201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221201")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221201'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221201'>杜氏故京兆人，五世祖辇，唐末习《开元礼》，以本科出身，仕至太子少保，赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221201_comment'></div>五季之乱，南渡至会稽，乐其风土，因居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221201_comment'></div>正献祁国公以直道相昭陵，清节照映一世，于君为伯祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221201_comment'></div>曾大父薳，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221201_comment'></div>祖父式，右朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221201_comment'></div>父调，宣德郎，娶莫氏，遂为馀姚人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221201_comment'></div>生七男子，悉使从师友，皆崭然有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221201_comment'></div>君即第五子，讳缜，字伯玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221201_comment'></div>宣德君既捐馆舍，生理益落，君方少年，能自刻厉读书，昼夜不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221201_comment'></div>应乡举，又试于开封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221201_comment'></div>崇宁中朝廷以舍选取士，君亦入乡校，虽累占优等，卒皆不售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221201_comment'></div>及既有子，则慨然曰：「吾平生苦志而不偶者，命也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221201_comment'></div>则尽以其所学授其子师旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221201_comment'></div>师旦又能克成其志，力学有闻，负笈游上庠，一时名士多馆致之，遂中绍兴二年进士第，盖将大君之门，使君姓名益显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221201_comment'></div>虽师旦之贤，亦君善教之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221201_comment'></div>结庐近郊，得江山之胜，浮沉闾井间，有以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221201_comment'></div>客至，未尝不饮，一枰之上，不知日之既夕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221201_comment'></div>乡邻有缓急叩，能随力赈贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221201_comment'></div>师旦荣归，君喜甚，为文戒之，略皆忠信孝友、立身行己之大节，当以祁公为法，可谓知所训矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221201_comment'></div>绍兴七年四月二十三日卒于家，享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221201_comment'></div>以其年十一月甲辰葬于山阴县迎恩乡苦竹小坞之原，从先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221201_comment'></div>娶莫氏，生三子：长即师旦，今为从政郎，新授饶之馀干令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221201_comment'></div>次师望，举进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221201_comment'></div>次师奭，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221201_comment'></div>女二人：长适韩师尧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221201_comment'></div>次适乡贡进士顾大陆，翰林学士临之孙，气节学问，凛然有祖风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221201_comment'></div>君之将葬，师旦从予求铭数矣，然不止益勤，义不可辞，于是叙次其平生而系之以铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221201_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1221201'>杜自祁公，正直匪躬，其源既深，其流则丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221201_comment'></div>君生孔艰，稽古不逢，教子雪耻，将大厥宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221201_comment'></div>小坞之原，水远山崇，从先人居，永閟幽宫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1221201_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ac8148ed05044e6eb0cf6735d74aaf55_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ac8148ed05044e6eb0cf6735d74aaf55");'><span id='ac8148ed05044e6eb0cf6735d74aaf55_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，55岁</div><div id='ac8148ed05044e6eb0cf6735d74aaf55' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月11日</a>　在江东路界首，交割安抚使司牌印。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月17日</a>　得旨亲往太平州视师进讨陆德，未行而城破。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月21日</a>　到建康府任。作品：谢知建康府到任表。<div id='poem_1221062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知建康府到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年闰4月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221062")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221062'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221062'>臣某言：伏奉诰命，除臣端明殿学士、左朝奉郎、江南东路安抚大使、兼知建康府、充寿春府、滁、濠、庐、和州、无为军宣抚使，寻具辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221062_comment'></div>伏蒙降诏不允，臣已于闰月十一日到江南东路界首交割安抚使司牌印，二十一日到建康府交割本府职事讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221062_comment'></div>总华省之三铨，久惭尸素；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221062_comment'></div>抗戎旃于两路，更冒宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221062_comment'></div>抚己无堪，循涯有愧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221062_comment'></div>伏念臣禀生穷苦，涉世阔疏，剽闻前哲之绪言，粗识人臣之大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221062_comment'></div>备论思之职，蔑闻献替之能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221062_comment'></div>操启拟之权，罔著公方之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221062_comment'></div>丛谤谗而销骨，积忧患以薰心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221062_comment'></div>虽上无投杼之疑，而臣有履冰之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221062_comment'></div>忱辞屡贡，敦谕益勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221062_comment'></div>拜君命于大庭，钦承德意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221062_comment'></div>窥王言于诏绋，祗服恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221062_comment'></div>用勉策其疲驽，庶仰分于忧顾，任隆力小，感激涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221062_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下天度无私，海涵莫测，务广招贤之路，协成恢复之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221062_comment'></div>谓臣朴忠，稍知于勤瘁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221062_comment'></div>察臣孤立，曲被于使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221062_comment'></div>兼抚江淮之封，尽付兵民之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221062_comment'></div>金陵会府，江左奥区，承频年兵火之馀，适千里流亡之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221062_comment'></div>招携怀远，抚循必以宽恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221062_comment'></div>折冲销萌，经画乃其馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221062_comment'></div>臣敢不仰遵睿训，益懋远图，说《礼》敦《诗》，盖尝闻于郤縠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221062_comment'></div>附众威敌，当勉效于穰苴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221062_comment'></div>庶殚犬马之劳，少答乾坤之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221062_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1221062_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月11日</a>　在建康任江东安抚大使，上疏修行宫事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月10日</a>　在建康任江东安抚大使，乞行宫增创后殿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月15日</a>　在建康任江东安抚大使，密奏加措置诸军事宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月</a>　在建康任江东安抚大使，奏翟庆、贺仲堪为宣州兵马监押事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年8月</a>　在建康任江东安抚大使，荐宗颖、胡舜陟为淮西制置使、巡抚使。作品：乞差文臣屯兵庐州状。贴黄。乞差胡舜陟往淮西状。<div id='poem_1221002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞差文臣屯兵庐州状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221002")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221002'>臣契勘淮西路庐、濠二州及六安军，最于伪地接境，近闻王彦充复于寿春府鸠兵聚粮，有窥伺之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221002_comment'></div>窃虑王亨、寇容、谢通辈兵力寡弱，透漏过淮南，则大江之外尽入贼境，深为未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221002_comment'></div>臣自到任，累具申奏，后来又乞五六千人，并乞差近上文臣一员前去庐州屯驻，虽蒙圣慈悯察，降付都督府，至今未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221002_comment'></div>今吕颐浩已到行朝，伏乞速降指挥，庶几防秋之际，不致误事，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221002_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1221002'>〔贴黄〕臣契勘长江千里，守御为难，若止于两淮防托，则力省功倍，臣所乞文臣一员，如傅崧卿难行，则本司参议官宗颖，乃宗泽之子，以其父故为诸将所爱，又其人亦慨然有忠愤之气，或蒙圣慈假以制置或招抚使副之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221002_comment'></div>臣一面措置，乞赐速降指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1221002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221002'><span class='label'>按：</span>八月八日奉圣旨，令李某别选文臣一员充淮西巡抚使，仍差兵二千人付所差官将带前去庐州屯驻。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221002_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1221003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞差胡舜陟往淮西状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221003")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221003'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221003'>臣近准枢密院劄子，奉圣旨，令臣别选文臣一员充淮西巡抚使，仍差兵二千人付所差官将带前去庐州屯驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221003_comment'></div>臣今再踏逐到知江州胡舜陟扬历内外差遣，顷知庐州，为一方军民所爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221003_comment'></div>兼其人忠义奋发，谙晓军政，堪充任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221003_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特与复元职名，速降指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1221003_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　在建康任江东安抚大使，乞降空名迪功郎、承信郎等官告，给付北来效顺归国及投献机密之人。作品：乞降空名官告状。<div id='poem_1220997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞降空名官告状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220997")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220997'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220997'>臣契勘今来防秋，选差材武兵将分守江险，及措置淮西军政事务，所系非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220997_comment'></div>比来不住有北来效顺归国及投献机密之人，未有重赏诱慰其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220997_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨，给降空名迪功郎、承信郎等官告，付臣收管，候接纳到效顺及有奇功显著之人，量其功绩书填给付讫，具名申知朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220997_comment'></div>庶几招怀抚纳，不烦干戈，有以激劝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1220997_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　在建康任江东安抚大使，有诗和胡舜陟。作品：和胡江州丹阳道中二首。<div id='poem_527568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和胡江州丹阳道中二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527568")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527568'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527568'>君才固英奇，志在行天讨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527568'>胡为尚兀兀，疲马踏长道。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527568'>论兵当节制，摧敌如振槁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527568'>不数圯上翁，顾笑渭滨老。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527568'>凛然击搏手，试用岂不早。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527568'>他年梁栋姿，涵养已合抱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527568'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_527568_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527569?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527569'>士卒常有馀，食廪苦不足。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527569'>妻孥惊<span class='inlineComment2'>（院本作竞）</span>笑我，陡换髯鬓绿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527569'>江西鱼稻乡，升平气全复。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527569'>以公封侯相，自可飞食肉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527569'>韬略固辐凑，精神常满腹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e77758c2033a47538d717ee5c18abd67_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e77758c2033a47538d717ee5c18abd67");'><span id='e77758c2033a47538d717ee5c18abd67_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>，58岁</div><div id='e77758c2033a47538d717ee5c18abd67' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月4日</a>　在湖州任，奏请废东南湖田，复田为湖。作品：乞废东南湖田札子。<div id='poem_1220998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞废东南湖田劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年闰2月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220998")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220998'>臣契勘东南地濒江海，水易泄而多旱，历代以来，皆有陂湖蓄水以备旱岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220998_comment'></div>盖湖高于田，田又高于江海，水少则泄田中，水多则放入海，故无水旱之岁、荒芜之田也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220998_comment'></div>祥符、庆历间，民始有盗陂湖为田者，三司转运使下书切责州县，复田为湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220998_comment'></div>当时条约甚严，谨水之畜泄则有闭纵之法，禁民之侵耕则有赏罚之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220998_comment'></div>近年以来，所至尽废为田，涝则水增益不已，旱则无灌溉之利，而湖之田亦旱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220998_comment'></div>民既已承佃，无复脱期，所收租税，悉充御前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220998_comment'></div>而漕司暗亏常赋，数至百万，而民之失业者不可胜计，可谓两失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220998_comment'></div>伏望圣慈速赐指挥，尽罢东南废湖为田者复以为湖，庶几凋瘵之民稍复故业，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220998_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1220998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1220998'><span class='label'>按：</span>三月一日奉圣者，令逐路转运司、常平司同共相度奏闻。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1220998_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年3月</a>　在湖州任，奏请铨量郡守、监司遴选县令及检会。作品：乞荐举武臣状。<div id='poem_1221007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221007?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞荐举武臣状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221007")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221007'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221007'>臣伏准绍兴五年三月六日敕中书门下省，依臣僚奏请，铨量郡守、监司，遴选县令，及检会绍兴元年十一月十九日手诏，令内外侍从官以上，监司、帅臣各举所知，限半月具奏，有以见陛下虚心求助之意，可谓切矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221007_comment'></div>然臣顷任行朝职事官，已尝应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221007_comment'></div>今陛下所求益广，中外荐者纷纷，而文学之士，峨冠博带，布列中外者，固已足用，初无乏材之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221007_comment'></div>昔叔孙通之归汉，从弟子百馀人，乃专言诸壮士进之，或以为言，通曰：「汉王方蒙矢石争天下，诸生宁能斗乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221007_comment'></div>故先言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1221007", 1221007, "Clauses/26/Comments/1")'>斩将搴旗</span>之士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221007_comment'></div>若通可谓知时务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221007_comment'></div>今金、伪凭陵，中原板荡，此诚陛下驭雄材虎将以制天下之时，臣之所荐，不敢复言文士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221007_comment'></div>臣累任守臣，窃见诸路武士多流落失所，其间人材少壮、弓马趫捷、武艺绝伦者甚众，朝廷既未尝录用，往往散在诸军，无以自拔，或委身盗贼，不能自新，甚可惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221007_comment'></div>臣愚不敢指名论荐，欲望圣慈特降睿旨，令诸路州军广行招收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221007_comment'></div>其间虽无武艺，而通晓兵机，能料敌制胜，或造作攻守之具，各为一科，令监司帅守按试保明，发赴枢密院，量材擢用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221007_comment'></div>庶几韩、彭之徒，或为时而出，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221007_comment'></div>伏候敕旨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221007_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1221007'>可谓：原脱，据《建炎以来系年要录》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1221007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221007'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_1221007_0'>⑴ 《庄简集》卷一二。又见《建炎以来系年要录》卷九一，《历代名臣奏议》卷一六九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1221007_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　知湖州期间，有诗和贺允中韵。作品：宫使少卿作喜雨诗，予辄续貂，然连日烝郁，雨意殊未解。霅川地濒太湖，畏雨而喜旱，亦有足忧者，辄再和贺子忱韵并呈少卿公一笑。<div id='poem_527743' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527743' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527743?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宫使少卿作喜雨诗予辄续貂然连日烝郁雨意殊未解霅川地濒太湖畏雨而喜旱亦有足忧者辄再和贺子忱韵并呈少卿公一笑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527743")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527743'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527743'>老钝安能济中兴，知君此意每推诚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527743'>邦人虽喜天心格，农夫预忧禾耳生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527743'>秋后竹阴侵簟冷，梦回蛩响杂阶声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527743'>雨溪自昔传佳咏，云水相依夜自明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527743'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　知湖州期间，有诗次韵贺允中喜雨诗。作品：次韵贺子忱喜雨。<div id='poem_527646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵贺子忱喜雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527646")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527646'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527646'>天眷周王德，功归傅说霖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527646'>少宽边饷急，聊慰老农心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527646'>雷隐沧江转，阶喧玉漏沈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527646'>西山多爽气，拄笏助清吟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527646'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月3日</a>　除显谟阁直学士，知平江府，上谢表。作品：除显谟阁直学士谢表。<div id='poem_1221064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除显谟阁直学士谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221064")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221064'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221064'>锡宠芝函，猥窃干方之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221064_comment'></div>升华延阁，叨陪扈从之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221064_comment'></div>虽沥恳以固辞，终冒恩而虚受<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221064_comment'></div>伏念臣才疏寡与，学浅无闻，周旋节义之大闲，唯知许国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221064_comment'></div>佩服《诗》、《书》之明训，资以事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221064_comment'></div>出际休明，浸膺膴仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221064_comment'></div>自获尘于器使，尝备历于险夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221064_comment'></div>外执铨衡，罔著公方之誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221064_comment'></div>入陪经幄，蔑闻献替之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221064_comment'></div>顷叨秘殿之崇资，俾冒名都之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221064_comment'></div>怀印未几，谤书已闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221064_comment'></div>怅孤根之易摇，如拉朽尔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221064_comment'></div>嗟谮言之已甚，更下石焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221064_comment'></div>赖圣度之灼知，排群言而复用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221064_comment'></div>起从田野，付以麾符，仅阅两时，稍还旧列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221064_comment'></div>特下十行之札，使兼三组之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221064_comment'></div>曾是罔功，实为非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221064_comment'></div>眷私若此，图报谓何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221064_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下道大兼容，智明旁烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221064_comment'></div>怜臣久侍于从橐，弗忍遐遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221064_comment'></div>知臣粗谨于吏方，特加奖用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221064_comment'></div>臣敢不益坚素履，勉继前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221064_comment'></div>雨露之泽自天，何酬造化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221064_comment'></div>葵藿之心向日，本自精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221064_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1221064_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月3日</a>　除显谟阁直学士，知平江府，上谢宰相表。作品：知平江府谢宰执启。<div id='poem_1221153' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221153' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221153?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知平江府谢宰执启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221153")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221153_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221153'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221153'>霅水分符，方安疏拙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221153_comment'></div>吴门易守，遽被升迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221153_comment'></div>释湖山清旷之居，当舟车凑集之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221153_comment'></div>虽恩荣之过分，顾谫薄以难胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221153_comment'></div>伏念某智不足以趋时，用非长于涉世，徒缘遭遇，浸冒使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221153_comment'></div>每怀报主之心，敢作容身之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221153_comment'></div>群嚣横议，众毁交攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221153_comment'></div>一去修门，再历岁时之久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221153_comment'></div>三纡郡绂，不离江浙之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221153_comment'></div>讫无善状之可称，苐惭救过之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221153_comment'></div>敢冀曲加奖与，力借吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221153_comment'></div>宠骤至以若惊，命已行而莫避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221153_comment'></div>诸惟侥冒，实有夤缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221153_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇仆射都督相公盛德格天，元勋盖世，内隆宽而博爱，外公听而并观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221153_comment'></div>舟楫济川，坐弭风波之险；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221153_comment'></div>盐梅调鼎，曲成品物之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221153_comment'></div>致此孤踪，屡叨殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221153_comment'></div>某敢不虔修职业，勉策疲驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221153_comment'></div>傥蒲柳之馀年，未填沟壑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221153_comment'></div>庶涓尘之薄效，粗报生成。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1221153_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a41cc205fa8b49ea8a1dc14cb59f776c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a41cc205fa8b49ea8a1dc14cb59f776c");'><span id='a41cc205fa8b49ea8a1dc14cb59f776c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>，58岁</div><div id='a41cc205fa8b49ea8a1dc14cb59f776c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月14日</a>　到平江府任，上到任谢表。作品：谢知平江府到任表。<div id='poem_1221065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知平江府到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221065")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221065'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221065'>臣某言：准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除臣显谟阁直学士、知平江府，臣已具辞免职名外，先于七月十四日到任交割职事讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221065_comment'></div>分符霅水，曾无善最之可书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221065_comment'></div>易地吴门，复玷蕃宣之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221065_comment'></div>瞻宸居而甚迩，纡郡绂以知荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221065_comment'></div>伏念臣守道不通，师心自信，误蒙简记，浸冒使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221065_comment'></div>谓忠义可以立身，而专于事上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221065_comment'></div>谓廉勤可以为吏，而果于奉公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221065_comment'></div>丛众毁之所归，坚一心而独往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221065_comment'></div>久困江湖之流落，频更牧守之往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221065_comment'></div>粤自小邦，遽移名郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221065_comment'></div>虽禽鱼之本性，乐此自安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221065_comment'></div>顾犬马之微诚，终于恋主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221065_comment'></div>使筋骸而可强，岂繁剧之敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221065_comment'></div>况此全吴，今为会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221065_comment'></div>顷尝游宦，备悉土风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221065_comment'></div>荐罹兵火之馀，无复豪强之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221065_comment'></div>朱轓入境，觉豺虎之俱空；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221065_comment'></div>竹马相迎，怅儿童之非昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221065_comment'></div>夫何羁蹇，有此遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221065_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下，如日烛幽，体乾行健，御群材而并用，无一物之或遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221065_comment'></div>怜臣志在当官，乐于循理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221065_comment'></div>察臣老不生事，或可庇民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221065_comment'></div>遂使贱微，数叨奖用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221065_comment'></div>臣敢不勉图报效，益励操修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221065_comment'></div>职在近严，敢怠忠嘉之告；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221065_comment'></div>身为屏蔽，力求控御之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221065_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1221065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月</a>　在平江府任，上奏荐举武臣。作品：应诏荐举武臣状。<div id='poem_1221072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应诏荐举武臣状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221072")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221072'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221072'>显谟阁直学士、左朝奉郎、知平江府李某申：准刑部符：「准绍兴五年七月十一日枢密院劄子：尚书省关臣僚上言节文：『窃见诸路武士多流落失所，其间人才少壮、弓马趫捷、武艺绝伦者甚众，乞令监司、帅守按试保明，发赴枢密院，量材擢用』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221072_comment'></div>七月十六日，三省枢密院同奉圣旨：『依奏，令诸路监司、帅守按试保明，具职位姓名申枢密院』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221072_comment'></div>今依应上项指挥，其间有已尝按试、曾经使唤，委有材武、通晓兵机及能造作攻守之具之人，具列职位、姓名如后：保义郎李翼，见任建康府兵马监押，今年十月当满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221072_comment'></div>忠翊郎方良，见在平江府，未有差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221072_comment'></div>承节郎贺伸，见在建康府，未有差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221072_comment'></div>成忠郎翼庆，见在江州，未有差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221072_comment'></div>成忠郎孙懋，见在建康府，未有差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221072_comment'></div>保义郎韩益、效用已借补人朱弁、阎肇，二人并在湖州，未有差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221072_comment'></div>已上？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221072_comment'></div>系守宣城并建康府日已经按试使唤，非徒武艺出伦，兼忠实可任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221072_comment'></div>成忠郎韩恭，保义郎李文，保义郎李兴，效用于青、卢尧弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221072_comment'></div>已上并系知婺州日在将领李进下使唤，武艺人材，超绝伦辈，未知所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221072_comment'></div>伏乞照会施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1221072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年8月</a>　在平江府任，得通公律师仙逝之讯，为其作塔铭，并请友人邹德久书之。作品：舍黄蘖裴公真像并偈。<div id='poem_1221178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舍黄蘖裴公真像<span class='inlineComment2'>（并偈）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221178")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221178'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221178'>宣州广教禅寺，实唐裴公故宅、黄蘖道场，二公像设存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221178_comment'></div>气韵森严，笔法简古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221178_comment'></div>予守郡日，命工摹得之，顾私家不能严净，适通公律师访予五松山，一见若有宿契，因请留寘铁磬堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221178_comment'></div>或曰：「静凝学徒皆宗律教，以南山为祖师，得无异议乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221178_comment'></div>予曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221178_comment'></div>禅、律二宗，本相因依，后学末师，妄自分别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221178_comment'></div>昔宽禅师谓白乐天曰：『无上菩提者，被于身为律，说于口为法，得于心为禅，应用者三，其致一也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221178_comment'></div>故如来所说大乘诸经，以文殊为问答之首者，皆明法身妙慧之门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221178_comment'></div>以普贤为问荅之首者，皆明妙智之万行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221178_comment'></div>诸佛菩萨皆依此二尊者以为师范，然后成菩萨之极果，处如来之上乘，岂有二哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221178_comment'></div>通公志行苦卓，识趣超然，禅、律并行，不相留碍，其必有得于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221178_comment'></div>恐诸衲子尚有疑情，对大众前复说偈曰：君看铁磬堂前像，恰似文殊对普贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221178_comment'></div>更着白须裴老子，夜深同听祖师禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221178_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1221178'>予作此文，通公盖尝刻之石矣，字画既不工，又镌刻失真，师意每怅然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221178_comment'></div>予以绍兴乙卯仲春赴官霅川，师追饯至上虞，临别犹眷眷要予书，且砻石以俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221178_comment'></div>仲秋几望，其徒仲珣法嗣遣净人持书至平江，言师以七月五日示寂坐逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221178_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221178_comment'></div>师虽学律，而于少林宗风尤所通解，盖已超然神游八极之外矣，无足深悲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221178_comment'></div>适予友人邹德久相过，因道师行业之美，相与感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221178_comment'></div>德久书实当今第一，篆、真、行各臻其妙，庶几师之名，托此以不朽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221178_comment'></div>五松居士李某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1221178_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年11月16日</a>　在平江，除礼部尚书。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
台州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='03f90ccb692f4eb88a755aecc8d32d59_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("03f90ccb692f4eb88a755aecc8d32d59");'><span id='03f90ccb692f4eb88a755aecc8d32d59_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>，59岁</div><div id='03f90ccb692f4eb88a755aecc8d32d59' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年6月12日</a>　罢为端明殿学士，知台州，上辞免状。作品：辞免知台州状。<div id='poem_1221011' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221011' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221011?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免知台州状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年6月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221011")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221011_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221011'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221011'>臣闻命震恐，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221011_comment'></div>伏念臣愚憃无知，久尘从列，出入内外，累试罔功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221011_comment'></div>揣分自量，合置閒散，敢谓圣恩宽大，未即弃捐，优礼臣邻，不忘菅蒯，知其老钝，尚使牧民，岂臣殒首碎胸所能报称！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221011_comment'></div>缘臣初以衰疾力祈宫祠，峻职便邦，岂敢轻受？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221011_comment'></div>况端殿秘严，臣虽尝冒处，本非侍从可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221011_comment'></div>伏望圣慈哀悯孤踪，保全危迹，特回涣号，庶免烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221011_comment'></div>所有职名并知台州指挥，伏望特赐寝罢，仍乞检会臣前奏，除一在外宫祠差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221011_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1221011_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='570d85239b934d518287492d9a525cfd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("570d85239b934d518287492d9a525cfd");'><span id='570d85239b934d518287492d9a525cfd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1137')">1136-1137年</a>，59-60岁</div><div id='570d85239b934d518287492d9a525cfd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　冬，知温州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　赴温州途中，过雁荡山，有文祭江子我。作品：祭江郎中子我文。<div id='poem_1221206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭江郎中子我文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221206")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221206'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221206'>士有隐居求志而志不获就，行义达道而道卒不伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221206_comment'></div>嗟嗟子我，实惟其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221206_comment'></div>文章气节，迈往绝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221206_comment'></div>傲睨公侯，心慕隐沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221206_comment'></div>跌宕文史，若将终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221206_comment'></div>我初识公，严濑之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221206_comment'></div>白鬓红颊，藜杖幅巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221206_comment'></div>抵掌笑谈，豪气如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221206_comment'></div>愤世嫉邪，群嚣狺狺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221206_comment'></div>立言虽多，意终在民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221206_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221206_comment'></div>公之志操，凛不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221206_comment'></div>救护众生，甚于饥渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221206_comment'></div>不知公者，见谓强聒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221206_comment'></div>数对便朝，词直意豁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221206_comment'></div>人谓才疏，公岂迂阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221206_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221206_comment'></div>公在奉祠，我处田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221206_comment'></div>诗文往来，曾不我鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221206_comment'></div>期公对床，放浪山水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221206_comment'></div>岂谓奄忽，赍志永已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221206_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221206_comment'></div>人之处世，不过百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221206_comment'></div>生死轮回，情感爱缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221206_comment'></div>孰如子我，去住萧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221206_comment'></div>神游八极，心遍大千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221206_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221206_comment'></div>我守永嘉，携孥南奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221206_comment'></div>道过雁山，岿然孤坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221206_comment'></div>怀想清标，精爽如存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221206_comment'></div>我欲有言，叫号莫闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221206_comment'></div>𢠳恍徘徊，寓哀一尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221206_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221206_comment'></div>四海之内，孰非弟昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221206_comment'></div>过者必酹，奚必子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221206_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1221206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年10月</a>　在温州，有跋文题阎立本列帝图。作品：跋阎立本列帝图。<div id='poem_1221164' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221164' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221164?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋阎立本列帝图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221164")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221164'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221164'>右阎立本《列帝图》，王贽家物，后归吴珏仪仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221164_comment'></div>予守永嘉日，其子祖忠出以相示，偶建安僧灵机善画人物，尤工传神，因使摹得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221164_comment'></div>后有富公序跋，距今才七十八年，而缣素断烂，乃甚于前画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221164_comment'></div>或疑其非真，然富公亲笔眷眷如此，斯人岂欺世者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221164_comment'></div>绍兴丁巳前十月，会稽李某谨题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1221164_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　在温州，有跋文题李纲所作颜真卿真赞。作品：跋李纲所作颜真卿真赞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　守温州期间，与诸贤奠谒许景衡，有诗记之。作品：同永嘉诸贤奠谒右丞许公少伊。<div id='poem_527642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同永嘉诸贤奠谒右丞许公少伊</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527642")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527642'>葱郁佳城秘，回环宅兆深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527642'>悬崖森翠柏，踊地布黄金。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527642'>天下方云扰，斯人竟陆沈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527642'>尘侵徐孺榻，弦断伯牙琴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527642_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　在温州，奏对抗金人之策。作品：论守御大计状。<div id='poem_1221012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论守御大计状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221012")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221012'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221012'>臣以孤蹇无能之身，蒙陛下起之流落放弃之中，更历内外，浸冒器使，十稔于兹，布衣衡茅之士遭遇如臣者，果几人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221012_comment'></div>顾惟天地父母之恩，虽碎首屠肝，岂能称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221012_comment'></div>臣到任未几，恭闻大驾移跸平江府，将亲御戎辂，誓师两淮，此臣捐躯效命之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221012_comment'></div>念方拘縻郡绶，留滞海滨，上之不能吐奇策以佐军谋，下之不能执干戈以卫宗社，乞扈从则贻干进之讥，献谋议则兴空言之诮，夙夜忧愤，莫知计之所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221012_comment'></div>臣闻忠臣不以出处二其心，正士不以险夷易所守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221012_comment'></div>臣岂敢预忧小人不根之言，遽有所畏避哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221012_comment'></div>况臣陛辞之日，陛下尝许臣以言，傥有所见，其忍缄默？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221012_comment'></div>臣伏睹关报，刘光世、张俊捍御大敌，三捷继闻，海县流传，孰不庆幸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221012_comment'></div>然臣闻强敌拥兵淮、扬、宿、亳之间，坐观胜败，此其志不浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221012_comment'></div>赵充国之击羌，以残灭为期，孙权每戒江上诸将不贪小利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221012_comment'></div>臣是以未敢以诸将奏捷为喜，而方以金人大队深入为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221012_comment'></div>昔杨珉问朱伺曰：「将军前后击贼，何以每胜」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221012_comment'></div>伺曰：「两敌共对，惟当忍之，彼不能忍，我能忍，以是胜耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221012_comment'></div>汉祖与项羽对垒，晋宣与诸葛亮相持，方形势未便，孤军远来，未尝与之争锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221012_comment'></div>周亚夫深壁以却吴军，光武坚营以降铜马，此皆已事之验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221012_comment'></div>臣观今日敌人布置，必有主谋，愿陛下勿轻此战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221012_comment'></div>今朝廷所恃独一韩世忠，彼必以精锐当之，而刘麟辈出没光、黄、庐、寿间，以牵制诸将而分吾力，金人必自淮、阳以入楚、泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221012_comment'></div>若社稷之灵，世忠足以御之，则无复事矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221012_comment'></div>万一众寡不敌，便有瓦解之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221012_comment'></div>昔楚屈完谓齐桓公曰：「楚国以方城为城，汉水为池，虽君之众，无所用之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221012_comment'></div>魏文帝至广陵，见波涛汹涌，叹曰：「此天所以限南北也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221012_comment'></div>兵法谓善守者敌不知所攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221012_comment'></div>今陛下已据东南形胜之势，敌人万里远来，投兵死地，利于速战而不利于迟久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221012_comment'></div>今不务持重而誇一时之功，决一旦之命，臣恐正堕敌计，非策之得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221012_comment'></div>臣狂瞽之言，曩备数从列，方燕閒进退造膝之语，所谓万全之策者，尝为陛下陈之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221012_comment'></div>金人往年入境无所得，去冬又无所得而去，士马折伤固已大半，异时虽欲复驱众攻我，孰肯为用者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221012_comment'></div>此乃坐制强敌之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221012_comment'></div>臣愚伏望陛下戒敕诸将，各务持重，不过隐忍三两月间，彼师老食尽，然后广设方略，出兵遣击，或邀其归途，我得胜算矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221012_comment'></div>伪齐恃金为强，金人既退，则刘豫父子岂能立国乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221012_comment'></div>复祖宗之故疆，还二圣于沙漠，当在此举，惟陛下特加圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221012_comment'></div>臣狂愚冒昧，无任惶惧激切待罪之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221012_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1221012_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年11月9日</a>　任江南西路安抚大使、兼知洪州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在洪州任江南西路安抚大使。春，李光与徐俯游洪州南楼，有诗唱和。作品：次韵师川见赠。<div id='poem_527643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵师川见赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527643")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527643'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527643'>钧枢归雅望，邪志寝奸雄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527643'>雕鹗清秋急，豺狼当路空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527643'>经纶思妙手，谈辩想英风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527643'>未厌东山卧，沈机一局中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年4月27日</a>　在洪州任江南西路安抚大使，有文祭张觷。作品：祭张龙图柔直文。<div id='poem_1221207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221207?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭张龙图柔直文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年4月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221207")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221207'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221207'>维绍兴八年戊午，四月丁巳朔，二十七日癸未，具位李某谨以清酌庶羞之奠，昭告于亡友虔州府君龙图张公柔直之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221207_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221207_comment'></div>天之生材，夫岂偶然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221207_comment'></div>或负其器业可为世用而卒于不试，或已试不尽而中道夭阏者，古人皆归之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221207_comment'></div>嗟嗟柔直，忠信孝友，虽武夫悍卒，皆知其贤，曷丰其德，而啬以年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221207_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221207_comment'></div>我初识子，倾盖握手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221207_comment'></div>惟其纯诚，持以悠久，故虽蛮貊可行，虎豹可驯，麋鹿可友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221207_comment'></div>其临民驭众，虽教条不设，而民之爱之，如父如母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221207_comment'></div>嗟嗟世人，厌常好奇，任数设诈，谓人莫知，谓民可罔，谓君可欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221207_comment'></div>孰如柔直，胸怀坦夷，貌如其心，燥湿莫移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221207_comment'></div>呜呼柔直，早厕英躔，中遭放逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221207_comment'></div>既跌复振，晚剖符竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221207_comment'></div>蔼时休声，如汉龚遂，化被犷俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221207_comment'></div>弄兵潢池，卖刀买犊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221207_comment'></div>子之云亡，邦失良牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221207_comment'></div>如晋羊祜，郡民巷哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221207_comment'></div>行者望碑，堕泪濡目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221207_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221207_comment'></div>我来江西，实总甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221207_comment'></div>入境之初，书来欢迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221207_comment'></div>孰谓奄忽，遂隔幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221207_comment'></div>双亲在堂，二孤茕茕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221207_comment'></div>我亦老矣，朋旧凋零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221207_comment'></div>寓词千里，有泪如倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221207_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1221207_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年5月13日</a>　升江南西路安抚制置大使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在洪州任江南西路安抚制置大使。江西久旱后雨，夏，送徐林赴行朝，有诗。作品：稚山运使作斋名藏晖且觅诗，久不能成。今兹以大农召行有日，因成鄙句，并以送行。<div id='poem_527573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>稚山运使作斋名藏晖且觅诗久不能成今兹以大农召行有日因成鄙句并以送行<span class='inlineComment2'>（院本作别）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527573")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527573'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527573'>美玉当韫椟，明珠产<span class='inlineComment2'>（院本作藏）</span>深渊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527573'>达士贵混俗，大隐常居廛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527573'>皓皓终易污，峣峣难自全。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527573'>和光同其尘，老聃有成言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527573'>徐侯如水鉴，胸中定媸妍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527573'>疾恶若仇雠，论事敢直前。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527573'>朅来大江西，独揽刺举权。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527573'>奸赃尽屏迹，豺狼敢垂涎。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527573'>顾欲藏其晖，名室以自镌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527573'>老火正淫恣，旱气方接连。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527573'>怅别南浦亭，去去朝日边。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527573'>中原正涂炭，生民思息肩。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527573'>公归明光奏，输忠倾肺肝。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527573'>功成不自居，名与日月悬。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527573'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_527573_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在洪州任江南西路安抚制置大使，江西久旱后雨，夏，送徐林赴行朝，有诗。作品：江西久旱，遍祷莫应，稚山少卿将赴行朝，一夕大雨。遐迩沾足，因成喜雨诗送行。<div id='poem_527574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527574?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江西久旱遍祷莫应稚山少卿将赴行朝一夕大雨遐迩沾足因成喜雨诗送行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527574")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527574_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527574'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527574'>老火擅炎夏，枯旱气欲然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527574'>伤心早晚禾，注目高下田。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527574'>民穷舍耒耜，群起操戈鋋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527574'>小偷何足道，所忧在四边。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527574'>夜来沧江雨，朝望水接天。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527574'>欢声达四境，渥泽遍大千。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527574'>清风亦徐来，扇簟皆可捐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527574'>有怀林壑幽，僧窗思昼眠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527574'>流浪生死海，一往六十年。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527574'>何以报主恩，粗了江西缘。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527574'>羡子朝上国，扬帆若登仙。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527574'>江山亦世情，雨后清且妍。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527574'>怅别南浦亭，杯行莫流连。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527574'>去去闻好音，一岁定九迁。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527574'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_527574_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年7月26日</a>　在洪州任江南西路安抚制置大使，有祭胡公文。<div id='poem_1221208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221208?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭胡公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年7月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221208")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221208'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221208'>维绍兴八年岁次戊午，七月庚申朔，二十六日乙酉，具位李某谨以清酌庶羞之奠，敢昭告于故徽猷阁直学士给事胡公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221208_comment'></div>惟昔仲尼，生于衰周，志不得伸，褒善贬恶，困于获麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221208_comment'></div>中遭禁锢，微词久堙，晚学末师，莫睹其真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221208_comment'></div>天生硕儒，迈往绝伦，强壮潜心，白首知津，发明纲领，芟夷荆榛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221208_comment'></div>我为诸生，识公成均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221208_comment'></div>道与世违，众说日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221208_comment'></div>衡山之阳，寂寞之滨，鼓吹六籍，若将终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221208_comment'></div>晚遇圣主，尧舜是陈，入侍经筵，献替咨询，排斥异端，诛击乱臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221208_comment'></div>据经守正，群嚣狺狺，一斥不复，竟至沈沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221208_comment'></div>泰山其颓，无复斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221208_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221208_comment'></div>嗟我与公，迹疏心亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221208_comment'></div>我出公入，有如参辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221208_comment'></div>琅然书词，诲言谆谆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221208_comment'></div>公既有子，付以斯文，死生旦暮，曾何足云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221208_comment'></div>缄词千里，寓哀一尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221208_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年9月9日</a>　在洪州任江南西路安抚制置大使，在南楼与贺允中等宴集，有诗。作品：九日会南楼，坐客十有二人，以“人世难逢开口笑，菊花须插满头归”分韵，得归字。次韵子忱郎中九日南楼宴集。<div id='poem_527739' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527739' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527739?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日会南楼坐客十有二人以人世难逢开口笑菊花须插满头归分韵得归字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527739")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527739_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527739'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527739'>不用携壶上翠微，南楼风景古云稀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527739'>宁辞坐上吹乌帽，应笑篱边候白衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527739'>举目佳山伤客意，满园丛菊待人归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527739'>分题未尽宾僚数，更看纹楸小合围<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527739'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527739'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_527739_0'>⑴ 自注：馀须、满两字，子忱、彦约输棋得之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527739_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵子忱郎中九日南楼宴集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527740")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527740'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527740'>登楼把酒面孱颜，富贵功名了不关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527740'>千古池台悲帝子，一时宾幕陋龙山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527740'>影沈寒水雁声断，香抱秋花蝶意闲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527740'>八郡往来聊自哂，孤云出岫尚知还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527740'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527740_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年10月22日</a>　在洪州，试吏部尚书。作品：辞免除吏部尚书状。<div id='poem_1221021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除吏部尚书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年10月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221021")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221021'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221021'>臣今月八日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，除臣吏部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221021_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221021_comment'></div>伏念臣顷以衰残力祈补外，往来江浙，首尾二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221021_comment'></div>既罔著于事功，久合从于罢斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221021_comment'></div>兼臣年龄迟暮，疾疢交攻，筋骸疲于将迎之劳，智虑耗于簿书之冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221021_comment'></div>念方防秋之际，未敢丐閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221021_comment'></div>岂谓陛下廓临照之明，开公正之路，矜怜旧物，收拾陈人，不遗菅蒯之微，复寘鹓鸿之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221021_comment'></div>况天官高选，铨部剧曹，岂臣憃愚所敢冒处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221021_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣诚悃，特赐除臣一宫祠差遣，庶安愚分，以息烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221021_comment'></div>臣已交割职事，见起发至衢、信间，听候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221021_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1221021_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
清江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='413775746ef74ce08a538e4075212215_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("413775746ef74ce08a538e4075212215");'><span id='413775746ef74ce08a538e4075212215_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>，64岁</div><div id='413775746ef74ce08a538e4075212215' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>李光赴藤州，途经清江，有诗寄向子諲。作品：过清江寄向伯恭。再寄向伯恭。<div id='poem_527914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527914?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过清江寄向伯恭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527914")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527914'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527914'>清江已在烟城外，碧瓦珠帘隔断桥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527914'>不见芗林真面目，霜花风叶暮萧萧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527914'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527914_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再寄向伯恭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527915")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527915'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527915'>南行万里敢辞遥，过尽江西独木桥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527915'>已见芗林真面目，依然华发两萧萧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527915'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527915_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在清江，为胡浚明作墓志铭。作品：胡府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1221203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221203?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胡府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221203")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221203'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221203'>吾友胡浚明，讳宗汲，世为越之馀姚人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221203_comment'></div>自其叔祖父穆始以进士起家，仕至屯田员外郎，子孙遂以儒为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221203_comment'></div>曾祖谅，赠大理寺丞，祖俨，父尚能，皆隐居不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221203_comment'></div>君自为儿时有成人之操，其父目为老子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221203_comment'></div>比长，刻意问学，手未尝释卷，夜引睡则以首叩柱，其自强如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221203_comment'></div>为文清古，不蹈袭前人一语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221203_comment'></div>少年预乡荐，益自信不疑，翱翔两学几十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221203_comment'></div>会朝廷以舍选取士，移其籍以归，久之，复不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221203_comment'></div>即所居筑室买书以教子，聚宗族乡党子弟，不问疏昵，讲说经史，责课程，皆耸然知化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221203_comment'></div>君性至孝，虽饮食起居，未尝忘亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221203_comment'></div>治居第，首严祖庙，不以便燕私之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221203_comment'></div>堂室奥址，规模与世俗异，登其门者皆恍然自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221203_comment'></div>奉养至俭薄，田庐所入，仅足糊口，而遇人急难，极力拯救，虽焦首濡足，不悔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221203_comment'></div>乡邻仰以丧葬婚嫁与病而医药者甚众，以是生理益落，君为之不少变，盖急义乐施，出于天资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221203_comment'></div>或以为过，君行之愈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221203_comment'></div>尝曰：「吾损己以益人，虽过，于义庸何伤」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221203_comment'></div>己酉冬，敌犯明、越，恶少相煽而起，几遍山谷，君挺身谕止之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221203_comment'></div>士族避地窜逃颠沛，君与之周旋调护，恩若骨肉，真可以托死生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221203_comment'></div>乡人争讼，多就评曲直，君每折以理法，皆洒然而返，不以干有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221203_comment'></div>闻人一善，若己有之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221203_comment'></div>或少有过差，必正色诘诮，虽其尊属，惮若严父师，惟恐君之闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221203_comment'></div>方士有以奇药爊黄金术授君，忽梦若有告者曰：「君欲为盗乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221203_comment'></div>既寤，亟取焚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221203_comment'></div>每小疾，必梦僧伽处方，服之辄愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221203_comment'></div>所居湖山并海，百井皆盐，梦人指其处，凿之得甘泉，皆君诚意所格也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221203_comment'></div>建炎改元，今上皇帝登宝位，凡五上礼部，例皆推恩，宗人强起之，授房州文学，调潭州浏阳县丞，改迪功郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221203_comment'></div>有知君者荐诸朝，监严州比较务，讥察出入，吏不能欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221203_comment'></div>郡遣官季点，君辄囚服待罪，众亦察其廉介，不复问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221203_comment'></div>务既清整，课亦增羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221203_comment'></div>寻转右修职郎、监潭州南岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221203_comment'></div>考满，转右从政郎，既而授饶之德兴丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221203_comment'></div>其在严也，郡将尤加礼，尝啖以厚利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221203_comment'></div>君曰：「此非所当得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221203_comment'></div>拒不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221203_comment'></div>未几，为郡者以贿闻，至下诏狱，坐贬，独君无一毫之污，众皆叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221203_comment'></div>某与君虽同里闬，崇宁初始识君京师，一见气合，其后契阔，离合不常，每见必欢然道故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221203_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221203_comment'></div>君虽穷老，而浩然之气不少衰，议论益刚决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221203_comment'></div>谓富贵功名可以立致，不在吾身，则在子孙，日夜励其子为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221203_comment'></div>而沂复嶷然有立，能成君之志，魁多士，取甲科，声名籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221203_comment'></div>君喜曰：「是必大吾门，吾志得矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221203_comment'></div>因复丐岳祠，从其子宦游，奉养甚适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221203_comment'></div>往来江湖间，幅巾萧散，怡然自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221203_comment'></div>享年七十，以绍兴十年八月癸未卒于其子秀州军事判官沂之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221203_comment'></div>即日护其柩以归，士友皆为流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221203_comment'></div>明年十二月壬申，葬本邑翁家湖之原，从新卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221203_comment'></div>君平生未尝阅佛书，死之日，沐浴盥栉，神识不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221203_comment'></div>娶莫氏，有贤行，能通书史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221203_comment'></div>凡君所为固有不近人情者，夫人能顺适之，人尤以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221203_comment'></div>子男二人：长即沂，次汾，举进士，亦有志操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221203_comment'></div>葬有期，沂衰绖踵门，出其友左迪功郎、温州州学教授虞仲琳之状，求铭于某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221203_comment'></div>某知君能详，追惟雅好，不敢以鄙拙为解，因掇拾其大略如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221203_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1221203'>凛志节以希古之人兮，既锐而坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221203_comment'></div>谓功名可立致兮，耻没世而无传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221203_comment'></div>强学疾驱兮人十己千，见义必为兮人后己先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221203_comment'></div>心亨志遂兮乐只丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221203_comment'></div>虽屈于一时兮白首迍邅，其存而不朽兮嗣子之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221203_comment'></div>盖造物者不报其人，而报其人之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221203_comment'></div>翁湖之滨，卜此新阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221203_comment'></div>馀庆流芳，子孙绵绵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1221203_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
藤县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0f7a466d0ab7491fbf4c68e8e0f7f46f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0f7a466d0ab7491fbf4c68e8e0f7f46f");'><span id='0f7a466d0ab7491fbf4c68e8e0f7f46f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1145')">1142-1145年</a>，65-68岁</div><div id='0f7a466d0ab7491fbf4c68e8e0f7f46f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年1月</a>　抵达藤州。有诗送枢密使臣。作品：予得罪南迁，朝廷枢密院准备差遣张君送伴，凡八十日。予嘉其勤。于其行也，作诗送之。<div id='poem_527747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527747' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527747?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予得罪南迁朝廷枢密院准备差遣张君送伴凡八十日予嘉其勤于其行也作诗送之<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527747")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527747'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527747'>日日孤村对落晖，瘴<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作蛮）</span>烟深处忍分离。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527747'>追攀重见蔡明远，赎罪难逢郭子仪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527747'>南渡可<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作每）</span>忧鸢共堕，北辕应喜<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作许）</span>雁相随。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527747'>马蹄惯踏关山路，他日重来更<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作又）</span>送谁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527747'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527747_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527748?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527748'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527748'>瘦筇羸马一貂裘，江浙湖湘得纵游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527748'>万里远劳君伴送，隔年应笑我淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527748'>默祈衡岳云开岭，夜入浯溪月满舟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527748'>北阙旧交如问讯，为言白尽老人头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527748'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在藤州，得吕本中书传授气功功法，作食粥诗。作品：谪居古藤，病起，禁鸡猪不食。儿子攻苦，食淡久之，颇觉安健。吕居仁书来，传道家胎息之术，因作食粥诗示孟博，并寄德应侍郎。<div id='poem_527578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谪居古藤病起禁鸡猪不食与儿子攻苦食淡久之颇觉安健吕居仁书来传道家胎息之术因作食粥诗示孟博并寄德应侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527578")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527578'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527578'>晨起一瓯粥，香粳粲如玉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527578'>稀稠要得所，进火宁过熟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527578'>空肠<span class='inlineComment2'>（院本作腹）</span>得软暖，和气自渗漉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527578'>过午一瓯粥，瓶罍有馀粟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527578'>淡薄资姜盐，腥秽谢鱼肉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527578'>岭南气候恶，永日值三伏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527578'>外强几中乾，那受外物触。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527578'>两餐莫过饱，二粥可接续。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527578'>故人尺书至，教我御瘴毒。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527578'>燕坐朝黄庭，妙理端可瞩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527578'>神车御气马，昼夜更往复。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527578'>久久当自佳，根深柯叶绿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527578'>寄语陈太丘，人生真易足。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年4月</a>　李光在藤州。陈时举罢，坐议朝廷罪李光为非。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年5月9日</a>　李光在藤州。朱倬罢，坐谄附李光。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年10月21日</a>　李光在藤州，何铸责授左朝奉郎秘书少监，徽州居住。坐以李光等之论为是。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　长子孟博自藤州归乡，l李光有诗送之。作品：送孟博二首。<div id='poem_527579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_11_527580'>嚬送与笑迎，但可付一噱。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527580'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_527580_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在藤州。李光与黄元功唱和。作品：签判黄元功公廨枕江，有小亭。落成之初，予偶假居之，明洁深稳，因得游息其上，榜曰寓亭，并留鄙句以见意。签判黄元功顷摄守蔚平枕江有小亭，予假居。久之，稍加葺治，且作诗其上名之曰横江，今既还职，辄用写呈。<div id='poem_527582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>签判黄元功公廨枕江有小亭落成之初予偶假居之明洁深稳因得游息其上榜曰寓亭并留鄙句以见意</a><span id='poem_sentence_3_527582'>新亭枕江皋，杳渺可飞步。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527582'>风涛振几席，云月随杖屦。<div
