id='poem_sentence_4_527750'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527750_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在藤州。迁居，有诗。作品：迁城南新居。次前韵。迁城南新居。<div id='poem_527753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迁城南新居</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527753")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527753'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527753'>背郭通幽面翠微，病躯野性最相宜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527753'>旋栽花竹频开径，恐碍云山短著篱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527753'>晓日临窗时读易，晚凉隔屋听评棋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527753'>三年瘴岭无归日，聊向深林占一枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527753'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527753_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次前韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527754")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527754'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527754'>瓮牖茅檐白版扉，地偏犹与病相宜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527754'>雨添山涧苔侵径，竹近阳陂笋过篱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527754'>三爵沉酣陶令酒，一奁成败谢公棋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527754'>车尘不到门前路，渐觉蒿莱长旧枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527754'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527754_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年2月</a>　在藤州。题跋。作品：跋再刋初虞世必用方。<div id='poem_1221167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221167?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋再刊初虞世必用方</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221167")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221167'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221167'>予观《千金》、《外台秘要》诸方书，皆前古圣贤有意拯救生灵，其功甚大，不可轻议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221167_comment'></div>但去古既远，分剂率用升斗，有今人不能晓者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221167_comment'></div>初公和甫，本朝儒医，博学能文，精通医术，所著《必用方》最为有用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221167_comment'></div>五十年来，中原士大夫家藏此书，其间所居僻远，一旦老少疾恙，难致良医，按方治疗，无不愈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221167_comment'></div>虽门类不多，而包括殆尽，信奇书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221167_comment'></div>自兵兴以来，北人多流寓二广，风俗渐变，有病稍知服药，不专巫祝之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221167_comment'></div>予谪居于琼，偶与郡守论近世方术之妙，无出此书者，遂欲刊行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221167_comment'></div>因以所藏本授之，庶遐方异域，知医药之可恃，稍加崇信，则禨祥祷解之风，不攻而自破矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221167_comment'></div>绍兴癸亥二月初吉，上虞李某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1221167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年9月23日</a>　在藤州。潘良能通判江州，坐与李光同党。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年4月</a>　在藤州。为仲兄李德充作记。作品：养生堂记。<div id='poem_1221175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221175' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221175?labeling=true' target='_blank'>养生堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221175")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221175'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221175'>予兄德充寓居越之馀姚，实在龙泉之北，江山映带，最为胜壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221175_comment'></div>尝于南偏作堂，爽垲而深隐，外不假台池苑囿之玩，内不列琴书图画之观，萧然一榻，而日游息其中，吐纳导引，以求长年，因榜之曰「养生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221175_comment'></div>客有过而问曰：「子于治生则信有术矣，何自而知养生乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221175_comment'></div>德充曰：「嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221175_comment'></div>子乌知治生？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221175_comment'></div>使子而知治生，则可与论养生之妙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221175_comment'></div>予今燕坐一室，心超三际，方以形为舍宅，神为主人，灌漱乎玉池之清泉，以溉丹田；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221175_comment'></div>呼吸乎玄牝之冲气，以营尺宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221175_comment'></div>锄胸中之荆棘而梨枣生，薅害稼之稂莠而嘉谷植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221175_comment'></div>子视予之养生，果异于治生乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221175_comment'></div>客无以应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221175_comment'></div>某方谪处南荒，书来告曰：「予辟养生堂，世俗之人或以为疑，予虽告以大略，意有未尽，汝其为我记之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221175_comment'></div>某自少年喜阅道书，游走四方，延见方士多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221175_comment'></div>神仙之说，虽传记备载，然皆虚荒幻怪，不足考信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221175_comment'></div>自陶隐居以正一之道授王知远、潘师正、司马子微，皆蝉蜕而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221175_comment'></div>然其法后世罕传，惟抱朴子论最简而易行者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221175_comment'></div>其说以住息为妙，盖息息之中，神气相合，如婴儿之处乎胞胎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221175_comment'></div>及其至也，如释氏之入定，六根皆废，心想都灭，胎从复气中结，气自有胎中息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221175_comment'></div>然非真积力久、功行俱圆者，未易到也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221175_comment'></div>世人不能捐弃外事，澄心观照，而日奔趋乎是非利害之境，遂使气自出入乎内，神自驰乎外，神气各行，子母不相守，至于夭死者，非不幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221175_comment'></div>古之善养生者，莫如广成子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221175_comment'></div>庄周之书载黄帝问答之语最详，摘其要言曰：「无视无听，抱神以静，形将自正」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221175_comment'></div>又曰：「汝神将守形，形乃长生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221175_comment'></div>老氏五千言，虽泛论道德之旨，其要言则曰：「谷神不死，是谓玄牝，玄牝之门，是谓天地根，绵绵若存，用之不勤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221175_comment'></div>此二者皆胎息之门户也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221175_comment'></div>德充学道垂三十年，平生寡欲，无所嗜好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221175_comment'></div>悟厚禄高位之伤德，故每安于卑官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221175_comment'></div>知珍脆肥浓之害性，故自甘于藜藿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221175_comment'></div>以慈俭为可宝，故无侈汰之过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221175_comment'></div>以朴素为可尚，故绝声色之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221175_comment'></div>今以从心之年，白须红颊，浮沉里巷，无一不如志者，虽使不知吐纳咽漱之理，固可与数子争年而比寿矣，尚何慕于彼哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221175_comment'></div>虽然，广成子修身千二百岁，而形未尝衰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221175_comment'></div>老氏则跨历商周至秦，莫知所终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221175_comment'></div>又有深于此者，西域圣人已成等正觉，视身犹浮云，斯须变灭，惟圆明一点，历劫而常存，今大乘诸经备载斯事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221175_comment'></div>德充倘兼修此道，暇时访寻禅宿，参透西来的的意，则飞行自在，出没去来，真游戏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221175_comment'></div>古所谓神形俱妙，殆谓是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221175_comment'></div>某去乡四年，忧伤困悴，有他人不能堪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221175_comment'></div>德充万里致书，必以此道过相勉策，且有白首相从之语，览之悽然，因书其末以见区区之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221175_comment'></div>异时倘遂生还，将筑室泥湾之上，风雨对床，其必有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221175_comment'></div>绍兴甲子孟夏几望，藤州寓亭北窗，某谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1221175_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年8月15日</a>　在藤州。甲子中秋微雨，闻施君家宴，戏赠。作品：临江仙（画栋朱楼凌缥缈）<div id='poem_117774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_117774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/117774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙 甲子中秋微雨，闻施君家宴，戏赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_117774")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_117774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_117774'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_117774'>画栋朱楼凌缥缈，全家住在层城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_117774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_117774'>中秋风露助凄清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_117774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_117774'>香凝燕寝，遮莫下帘旌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_117774_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_117774'>佳节喜逢今夕月，后房重按新声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_117774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_117774'>姮娥端解妒娉婷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_117774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_117774'>微云点缀，不放十分明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_117774_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年10月</a>　在藤州。赵鼎知吉阳军道过藤州，李光与之相从累日，有诗。作品：赵丞相过藤州，相从累日。因言在朝与诸史官会话，论修史事恐它时不免南行，坐有一士云：“若有此，某当从行。”今日到此，音问也不通，退作小诗。次韵赵丞相海鸣。<div id='poem_527925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赵丞相过藤州相从累日因言在朝与诸史官会话论修史事恐它时不免南行坐有一士云若有此某当从行今日到此音问也不通退作小诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527925")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527925'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527925'>平时尽道相随去，度岭何曾见一人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527925'>赖是随身有孤影，灯前月下却相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527925'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527925_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵赵丞相海鸣<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527960")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527960'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527960'>幽人一枕梦魂清，风鼓寒潮夜有声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527960_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527960'>海色天容本澄静，年来应为不平鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527960_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527960'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527960_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527961?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527961'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527961'>身如一叶任风飘，闭眼观心路匪遥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527961'>惯听海鸣还熟寝，未妨归梦趁回潮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527961'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年11月26日</a>　移琼州安置。<br /><a href="javascript: <div class='label1' id='252daa1af46f4f68b348b034eb198365_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("252daa1af46f4f68b348b034eb198365");'><span id='252daa1af46f4f68b348b034eb198365_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>，68岁</div><div id='252daa1af46f4f68b348b034eb198365' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过陆川，有诗赠别。作品：乙丑二月，予赴贬琼山，苏令办自蔚平追路至陆川访别，临行作两小诗。<div id='poem_527929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乙丑二月予赴贬琼山苏令办自蔚平追路至陆川访别临行作两小诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527929")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527929'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527929'>墟落相逢一笑迎，旋沽浊酒得深倾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527929'>明朝转首俱千里，君到藤江我到琼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527929'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527929_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527930' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527930?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527930'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527930'>淹留客馆雨冥冥，烽火仍连近贼营。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527930'>已悟去来生死梦，年来愈觉一身轻<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《庄简集》卷六）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527930'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527930_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过陆川，有诗呈陆川邑官。作品：离容南百里间，多古松僵仆道上，不免斧斤之患。感之，作小诗呈陆川邑官，使稍禁戢之。<div id='poem_527928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>离容南百里间多古松僵仆道上不免斧斤之患感之作小诗呈陆川邑官使稍禁戢之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527928")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527928'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527928'>百年斤斧避龙鳞，尚被樵夫斫作薪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527928'>三伏修涂多暍死，清阴留取庇行人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527928'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527928_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
雷州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='35cc12b33fce405b8bd0ed60882aed40_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("35cc12b33fce405b8bd0ed60882aed40");'><span id='35cc12b33fce405b8bd0ed60882aed40_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>，68岁</div><div id='35cc12b33fce405b8bd0ed60882aed40' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　道过雷州，渡海南行，途中有诗抒怀。<div id='poem_527931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>渡海三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527931")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527931'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527931'>三载藤江守药炉，身轻那复羡飞凫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527931'>琼山万里乘风便，始觉惊涛异坦途。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527931'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527931_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527932' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527932' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527932?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527932_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527932'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527932'>出处从今莫问天，南来跨海岂徒然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527932_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527932'>须知鲁叟乘桴兴，未似商岩济巨川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527932_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527932'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527932_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527933?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527933'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527933'>潮回齐唱发船歌，杳渺风帆去若梭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527933'>可是胸中未豪壮，更来沧海看鲸波。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527933'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527933_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
琼山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='27b1f5d5a0dc47e7be3e98fcb164b32c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("27b1f5d5a0dc47e7be3e98fcb164b32c");'><span id='27b1f5d5a0dc47e7be3e98fcb164b32c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1150')">1145-1150年</a>，68-73岁</div><div id='27b1f5d5a0dc47e7be3e98fcb164b32c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年3月15日</a>　抵琼州贬所。作品：琼州安置谢表。<div id='poem_1221069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>琼州安置谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年3月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221069")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221069'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221069'>臣某言：今年二月十六日，准藤州公文送到尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，移臣琼州安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221069_comment'></div>臣寻于当月二十日起离藤州，至三月十五日已至琼州贬所讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221069_comment'></div>投寘峤南，采公言而未厌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221069_comment'></div>窜流海外，据罪戾以犹轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221069_comment'></div>怅来日之无多，岂生还之敢望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221069_comment'></div>徒怀结恋，莫报恩私<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221069_comment'></div>伏念臣寒苦立身，间关出仕，躬受圣神之眷，屡更要剧之除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221069_comment'></div>越自从班，超预机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221069_comment'></div>而臣刚褊自任，戆愚不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221069_comment'></div>器小疾颠，亟投閒而置散；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221069_comment'></div>根孤易拔，卒负衅以招尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221069_comment'></div>顾九死以犹甘，虽三黜而无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221069_comment'></div>扪心自讼，没齿何言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221069_comment'></div>空贻岁月之多，难逭简书之畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221069_comment'></div>尚全视息，未即诛锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221069_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下舜孝格天，尧仁覆物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221069_comment'></div>干戈载戢，故得百姓之欢心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221069_comment'></div>温凊不违，以尽一人之荣养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221069_comment'></div>有如草芥，咸被矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221069_comment'></div>而臣年仅七旬，主拘囚于瘴地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221069_comment'></div>行踰万里，更冒涉于鲸波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221069_comment'></div>伏望怜臣奉事之有年，悯臣废黜之已久，稍回眷遇，曲赐保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221069_comment'></div>大明中天，庶容光之必照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221069_comment'></div>时雨及物，幸枯蘖之再生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221069_comment'></div>永依樵牧之群，以毕桑榆之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221069_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1221069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年4月</a>　在琼州。寒食节，有诗。作品：雷化多旷野，道傍常闻鹧鸪声。<div id='poem_527934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雷化多旷野道傍常闻鹧鸪声</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527934")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527934'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527934'>已过梅岭更南征，渺渺琼山四百程<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：自雷渡海南四百里。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527934'>日暖风和寒食路，行人休听鹧鸪声<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：俗讹其声曰行不得。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527934'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年4月7日</a>　在琼州。葺居于双泉。撰记赋诗。作品：琼州双泉记。次韵徐念道琼台泂酌亭两绝。<div id='poem_1221176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>琼州双泉记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年4月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221176")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221176'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221176'>《洪范》论五行，一曰水，曰「润下作咸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221176_comment'></div>山者水所出，海者水所钟，莫崇于山，莫卑于海，故海中之水无不咸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221176_comment'></div>自雷渡海而南曰琼，琼本海中山耳，而双泉之井，独冠于二广，岂其源渊所禀，得天地粹灵之气，而不资于海邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221176_comment'></div>陆羽《茶经》论水云：「山水上，江水次，井水下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221176_comment'></div>又云：「山水乳泉漫流者上，江水取去人远者，井取汲多者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221176_comment'></div>双泉在郡之东北隅，冈峦回抱，泉谽窦间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221176_comment'></div>其发源甚微，初为小池，泓澄清澈，莹若冰鉴，不见其流动之形，盖所谓乳泉漫流者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221176_comment'></div>郡人初不知贵，苏公端明南迁过琼，酌水而异之，往告其人，而郡守求亭名与诗，遂名其亭曰「泂酌」，且留诗其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221176_comment'></div>绍兴乙丑，予自藤江再贬海外，以三月望至琼，众指双泉之胜，乃葺居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221176_comment'></div>一日尽出积水，因得详究二泉所从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221176_comment'></div>盖一井而有两脉，其一自西南，其一自正北，皆濆涌而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221176_comment'></div>水既渴，泉益湍驶，因各盛以器皿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221176_comment'></div>色味初若不可辨，久之，众皆谓西南来者尤清甘，然后知只尺而异味者，非虚语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221176_comment'></div>泉自小沟南走十馀步，溢为方池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221176_comment'></div>又自两龙口入下池，则泉之觱发者益众，水益深广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221176_comment'></div>每当暴雨涨溢，众流散漫，灌注于外，四方之民无男女少长，挈瓶罂就浣濯者无昼夜，常满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221176_comment'></div>双泉之名闻于远近，实自苏公发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221176_comment'></div>旧传有白龙尝露脊尾，气浮水面，询之故老，以为信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221176_comment'></div>苏公既不载，然亦莫有见者，独惠洪记注间一诗，其略云：「异哉寸波中，露此横海脊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221176_comment'></div>举首玉箸插，忽去银丁掷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221176_comment'></div>大身何时见，夭矫翔霹雳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221176_comment'></div>谁言鹏背大，更觉宇宙窄」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221176_comment'></div>语虽不凡，然决非苏公诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221176_comment'></div>龙之有无，固不系水之美恶，今所在潭洞池井以龙得名者，其神灵或能兴云雨，而未必皆甘泉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221176_comment'></div>盖水之有源，其畜必深，畜之深，则其发必远，其为龙神所宅焉，无有疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221176_comment'></div>《易》言：「山下出泉，蒙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221176_comment'></div>《禹贡》载禹之治水之迹，亦详其所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221176_comment'></div>盖水之发源，不过杯勺间，及为江沱潜汉，为渭为洛，则贯穿中华，横绝吴楚，非有本者能如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221176_comment'></div>世所称甘泉多出于深山乱石中，好奇之士至穷探远讨，不惮岩壑之险，攀缘上下，然后得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221176_comment'></div>今乃不出户庭几席之上，清流滉漾，影摇窗扉，潺湲之声，夜到枕上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221176_comment'></div>风月之下，每与客把酒徘徊，酌泉而歌之曰：「泉之泠泠兮以濯予缨，泉之湛湛<span class='inlineComment2'>（音沈）</span>兮以洗予心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221176_comment'></div>朝资予之食饮兮，暮伴予之孤吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221176_comment'></div>或泛流杯，或横素琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221176_comment'></div>予既寓居之久矣，日涉浅而汲深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221176_comment'></div>咽漱元和，涤除烦襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221176_comment'></div>玉池生肥兮沙砾变金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221176_comment'></div>凛冰雪之绕齿兮，何瘴烟毒雾之能侵邪」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221176_comment'></div>歌罢，辄欣然自得，忘其身之在万里外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221176_comment'></div>独恨海外险远，不得与惠山、虎丘、南零诸水同列于图经，非苏公一顾之重，则斯泉也委于荒榛蔓草间，饮牛羊而产蛙鲋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221176_comment'></div>流俗所传，既多怪妄，因志其本末，使后来者有考焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221176_comment'></div>四月七日，上虞李某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1221176_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵徐念道琼台泂酌亭两绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年4月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527936")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527936'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527936'>笙箫杳渺鹤徘徊，嬴女时应下玉台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527936'>莫问三山在何许，更寻方丈与蓬莱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527936'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527936_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527937?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年4月7日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527937'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527937'>苏公陈迹半成空，杖策经行绍圣中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527937'>便与佳名还泂酌，晔然光景照无穷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527937'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527937'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527937_0'>⑴ 自注：泂酌亭、琼台，在海南孤绝之处，限以鲸波，而风物萧然若在尘外，疑即三山之一也。东坡先生绍圣间往来琼山，独饮双泉，因作亭其上，名曰泂酌亭，且留诗云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527937_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年8月15日</a>　在琼州。中秋，李光有诗谢雷州太守王趯惠酒。作品：中秋谢彦恭惠酒。<div id='poem_527589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527589?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中秋谢彦恭惠酒</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_527589'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527589'>中秋有佳月，名酝来海康。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527589'>海康太守贤，怜我持空觞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527589'>远分十具至，呼儿唤邻墙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527589'>坐客尽饮流，一举空罍缸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527589'>酒酣对明月，不藉灯烛光。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527589'>移席俯清流，照我两鬓霜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527589'>海北与海南，各在天一方。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527589'>我老归无期，两地遥相望。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527589'>宴坐桄榔庵，守此岁月长。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527589'>愿子一咄嗟，跨空结飞梁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527589'>度此往来人，鱼盐变耕桑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527589'>篱边白衣来，莫待菊蕊黄<span id='poem_sentence_12_527589_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年9月2日</a>　在琼州。自公馆迁居双泉，有诗。作品：九月二日自公馆迁居双泉，风物幽胜，作双泉诗二十韵。泂酌亭。<div id='poem_527585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九月二日自公馆迁居双泉风物幽胜作双泉诗二十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年9月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527585")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527585'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527585'>山腰秘灵源，初出才一线。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527585'>方池湛空碧，奔驰忽萦转。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527585'>皎皎涵青蘋，累累涌珠串。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527585'>夜深耿落月，澄澈静如练。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527585'>呀然旧穴深，神物或时现。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527585'>邦人傥知敬，早岁起雷电。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527585'>凛然居其间，正味独不变。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527585'>我来卜幽居，萧洒得奇观。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527585'>惠泉入权门，疲人走邮传。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527585'>贪泉亦强名，闻者自鄙贱。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527585'>瓶罂日夜汲，闾里悉周遍。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527585'>数椽如可老，一壑吾欲擅。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_527585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年9月3日</a>　在琼州。徐自然、李申之携酒来访，李光有诗。作品：九月二日徙居双泉，翌日，徐自然使君、李申之监郡携酒见过，退成古调百三十言，戏简二公一笑。<div id='poem_527586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九月二日徙居双泉翌日徐自然使君李申之监郡携酒见过退成古调百三十言戏简二公一笑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年9月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527586")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527586'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527586'>南行踰万里，公馆烦造请。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527586'>主人怜老病，为卜林庐静。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527586'>郊居偶然遂，俗虑尽可屏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527586'>双泉信奇绝，岁久浑泥泞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527586'>稍觉藻荇繁，渐已产蛙黾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527588'>明朝汲新泉，旧箧馀赐茗。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年9月9日</a>　在琼州。重九日宴琼台，有词。作品：南歌子（佳节多离恨）<div id='poem_117776' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_117776' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/117776?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南歌子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>重九日宴琼台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_117776")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_117776_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_117776'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_117776'>佳节多离恨，难逢笑口开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_117776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_117776'>使君携客上层台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_117776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_117776'>不用篱边凝望、白衣来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_117776_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_117776'>且看花经眼，休辞酒满杯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_117776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_117776'>玉人低唱管弦催。<div id='poem_sentence_4_117776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_117776'>归去琐窗无梦、月徘徊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_117776_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年11月13日</a>　在琼州。生日，有诗。作品：乙丑生朝。<div id='poem_527935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乙丑生朝</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年11月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_527935'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527935'>今朝生日岂须论，老去难酬父母恩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527935'>惟有海南香一瓣，直教薰炙遍乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527935'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年1月</a>　在琼州。有诗多首抒怀。作品：丙寅元日偶出，见桃李已离披，海南风土之异，不无感叹。独追维三伏中荔支之胜，又江浙所不及也。因并见于诗。新年杂兴十首。<div id='poem_527761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙寅元日偶出见桃李已离披海南风土之异不无感叹独追维三伏中荔支之胜又江浙所不及也因并见于诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527761")'>李光</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_1_527761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527761'>庭院秋深时有燕，园林春半已无花。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527989_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年1月15日</a>　在琼州。魏安石邀观看灯火，李光因病未赴，有诗。作品：元夕阴雨，孤城愁坐。适魏十二介然书来，言琼台将然万炬，因以寄之。<div id='poem_527591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527591?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元夕阴雨孤城愁坐适魏十二介然书来言琼台将然万炬因以寄之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527591")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527591_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527591'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527591'>海滨遇元夕，况值愁阴天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527591'>重云<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>障佳月，微雨杂瘴烟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527591'>孤城欲黄昏，里巷已萧然。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527591'>荒祠鼓坎坎，老巫舞蹁跹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527591'>挥杖眩村氓，捩齿传神言。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527591'>异域俗尚鬼，殊形耳垂肩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527591'>邦人素敬畏，香灯竞骈阗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527591'>使君招我饮，老病不得前。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527591'>有如伏枥马，硉兀难加鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527591'>遥知琼台上，万炬照绮筵。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527591'>幽人正愁绝，跏趺坐深禅。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527591'>雾霭埋群山，不碍孤月圆。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527591'>茅庵一灯留，照我独不眠。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527591'>夜阑香篆销，息息火自传。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527591'>何当访羽客，同上罗浮巅<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527591'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_527591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527591'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527591_0'>⑴ 原作阴，据《永乐大典》卷二○三五四、院本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_527591_0'>⑵ 自注：罗浮山不甚穹，而夜见日，东坡有诗云：罗浮见日鸡一鸣。又小说，中秋大雷雨，坐有道人引客上罗浮顶，月色皎然，云雷皆在山脚下。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527591_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年1月15日</a>　在琼州。琼台元夕次太守韵。作品：汉宫春（危阁临流）<div id='poem_117771' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_117771' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/117771?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉宫春 琼台元夕次太守韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_117771")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_117771_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_117771'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_117771'>危阁临流，渺沧波万顷，涌出冰轮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_117771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_117771'>星河澹澹，天衢迥绝纤尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_117771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_117771'>琼楼玉馆，遍人间、水月精神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_117771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_117771'>□□□，清江瘴海，乘流处处分身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_117771_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_117771'>邦侯盛集佳宾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_117771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_117771'>有香风缥缈，和气氤氲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_117771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_117771'>华灯耀添绮席，笑语烘春。<div id='poem_sentence_6_117771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_117771'>窥帘映牖，看素娥、偏顾幽人。<div id='poem_sentence_7_117771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_117771'>空怅望，通明观阙，遥瞻一朵红云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_117771_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在琼州。春，为徐自然作辞赋。作品：感春辞一篇为自然使君作。<div id='poem_1220922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感春辞一篇为自然使君作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1220922")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220922'>有美人兮天一方，秀外而慧中兮，体便娟而生香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220922_comment'></div>腰支婀娜兮，曳六铢之仙裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220922_comment'></div>表倾城之巨丽兮，施粉太白，增之则长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220922_comment'></div>瞬明眸而流盼兮，莹秋水之清扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220922_comment'></div>良辰胜日，宾客满堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220922_comment'></div>忽歌喉之宛转兮，声遏云而绕梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220922_comment'></div>异巫山之朝云兮，徒见梦于楚襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220922_comment'></div>怅尤物之不可久兮，抚衾枕于空床。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220922_comment'></div>耿青灯之闪闪兮，怨秋夕之未央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220922_comment'></div>记音容于彷佛兮，掩涕泪之浪浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220922_comment'></div>于时烦暑既退，微露宵零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220922_comment'></div>风萧萧而入牖，虫唧唧而悲鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220922_comment'></div>徂清夜于兰房，收乱志于短檠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220922_comment'></div>虽冥冥而罔觌，犹依依而奉承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220922_comment'></div>嗟予生之耿介兮，视死生于虚诳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220922_comment'></div>慕壮夫之猛烈兮，悟释氏之真妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220922_comment'></div>浩歌径醉，饮醇啜醨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220922_comment'></div>我兮为客，彼得所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220922_comment'></div>焚香清坐，神气相随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220922_comment'></div>有来唁者，一笑而挥之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1220922_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年4月</a>　在琼州。寒食节，有诗。作品：居岭外遇寒食。<div id='poem_527600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>居岭外遇寒食</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527600")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527600'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527600'>春日自明霁，我心何郁伤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527600'>草木竞芳菲，飞鸣自颉颃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527600'>悄悄坐书幌，幽幽宴空床。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527600'>既无功名念，反思白昼长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527600'>愁来不自持，零落鸿雁行。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527600'>三过解泽流，六见槐柳黄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527600'>最怜小儿女，路远不得将。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527600'>生还一笑喜，死去埋他乡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527600'>生死如循环，我师佛老庄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527600'>感此寒食节，新烟过邻墙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527600'>松楸渺云海，目极摧肝肠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527600'>书成附鳞翼，不如永相忘。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527600'>何以慰目前，作诗示阿张。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527600'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_527600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年8月7日</a>　在琼州。月夜与魏安石对饮，有诗。作品：八月七日夜对月。<div id='poem_527602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八月七日夜对月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年8月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_527602'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527602'>仲秋气已爽，林壑雨新过。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527602'>忽惊浮霭空，乍觉天宇大。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527602'>夜凉风露清，佳月才半破。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527602'>清辉渐可爱，入户惊照坐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527602'>团圞绕中庭，有似蚁循磨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527602'>西山耸冈峦，轮侧愁易堕。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527602'>魏子不解饮，诗语颇顿挫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527602'>呼儿聊与盏，我唱渠辄和。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527602'>停杯看月落，客去未能卧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527602'>海月夜夜好，新诗幸频课。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527602'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_527602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年9月8日</a>　在琼州。有文祭孙昌。作品：祭孙昌文。<div id='poem_1221209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221209?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭孙昌文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年9月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221209")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221209'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221209'>维绍兴十六年岁次丙寅，九月戊辰朔，初八日乙亥，具位李某今遣虞候陈武以酒食之奠，致祭于故吏进义尉副孙昌之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221209_comment'></div>惟丁未之初，汝方事予，实二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221209_comment'></div>武林之变，犬狼豺虎，戈矛满前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221209_comment'></div>奔逃窜伏，昼夜拥护，脱予馋涎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221209_comment'></div>予之得罪，台舆皂隶，散如云烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221209_comment'></div>汝独万里，梯山航海，从予南迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221209_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，岂谓汝之一病，药石非效，竟至沉绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221209_comment'></div>汝之生也，能自刻励，抄经坐禅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221209_comment'></div>今其死也，必不泯默，沦堕九泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221209_comment'></div>死生出没，败坏相续，理之常然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221209_comment'></div>予所恨者，日冀勿药，从予北遄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221209_comment'></div>今其永诀，不可柰何，必归之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221209_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221209_comment'></div>荼毗归骨，予敢忘汝，属纩之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221209_comment'></div>聊致薄奠，魂其有知，享吾意焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1221209_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年9月</a>　在琼州。徐自然任满北返，李光有诗送之。作品：自然解印北还作古风送行。<div id='poem_527595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自然解印北还作古风送行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527595")'>李光</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_527595'>徐侯古循吏，作牧海南边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527595'>三载抚民夷<span id='poem_sentence_2_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527595'>父老有好词，不见吏索钱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527595'>忽闻解印绶，蛮歌惨离筵。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527595'>远控横海鲸，追蹑凌波仙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527595'>寄语广利神，无令飓风颠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527595'>临行一麾手，万事尽弃捐。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527595'>勿作儿女恋，咿嚘涕潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527595'>火云赤峥嵘，修途愿加鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527595'>爱君气猛厉，心似铁石坚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527595'>迥悟出世法，痛扫习气缠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527595'>明窗净棐几，华藏了大千。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年9月9日</a>　在琼州。与李申之等宴饮，有诗。作品：丙寅重九，权郡李申之置严氏野趣亭，爱其幽深，因作此诗。<div id='poem_527592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙寅重九权郡李申之置酒严氏野趣亭爱其幽深<span class='inlineComment2'>（院本作胜）</span>因作此诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527592")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527592'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527592'>迁流南海滨，两见菊蕊黄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527592'>今晨有嘉招，驾言陟崇冈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527592'>寒花卧短篱，疏松间修篁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527592'>西风起萧瑟，吹我两鬓霜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527592'>旋驾岂无期，良燕讵易忘。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在琼州。李申之植竹数十棵于李光后圃，李光有诗记之。作品：申之移竹数十竿，植之后圃，增贲幽人之居，作诗为谢。<div id='poem_527755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申之移竹数十竿植之后圃增贲幽人之居作诗为谢</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527755")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527755_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527755'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527755'>节概平生慕此君，晚年流落偶相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527755'>装添小圃林泉胜，隔尽权门车马尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527755'>雨浥寒梢香掩冉，月归疏影夜精神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527755'>他年亭下清阴满，谁记当时种莳人。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在琼州。久旱得雨，李光与李申之唱和。作品：久旱得雨奉呈申之权郡学士。<div id='poem_527762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527762?labeling=true' target='_blank'>久旱得雨奉呈申之权郡学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527762")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527762'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527762'>不用椎牛渎帝乡，精诚端可格穹苍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527762'>举头忽见千山雨，默祷惟凭一瓣香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527762'>已度南天三伏旱，未妨北牖午风凉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527762'>老蛟欲睡重鞭起，莫遣晴鸠唤夕阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527762'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527762_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在琼州。与徐自然唱和。作品：再蒙自然使君宠和竹诗率尔为谢、自然使君连赋竹诗辄复次韵。<div id='poem_527756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再蒙自然使君宠和竹诗率尔为谢</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527756")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527756_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527756'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527756'>画手休誇最逼真，东墙月影画难亲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527756'>常陪翠柏凌寒景，几见夭桃委路尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527756'>鸣凤引雏来应瑞，箨龙得雨便能神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527756'>双泉异日增幽胜，开盏时时中圣人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527756'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527756'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_527756_0'>⑴ 自注：曹希蕴作《墨竹诗》云：最爱小轩岑寂夜，月移清影上东墙。苏公每叹赏此句，《次韵吴传正枯木歌》云：天公水墨自奇绝，瘦竹枯松写残月。梦回疏影在东壁，惊怪霜枝连夜发。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527756_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527757' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527757' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527757?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_527757'>闲客携觞日对君，岁寒相与独心亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527757'>栽培野外千竿碧，抖擞胸中万斛尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527757'>月影临窗如见画，风轮长笋不无神<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527757'>使君好事频吟赏，萧洒襟怀似晋人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527757'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527757'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_527757_0'>⑴ 自注：世言草木之长，常在昧明间，蚤作而伺之，乃见拔起数寸，竹笋尤甚。东坡《和子由拔白发诗》云：风轮晓长春笋节。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527757_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年9月11日</a>　在琼州。李光会客严氏野趣亭，有诗。作品：重阳后二日，会严氏野趣亭，坐客吴德永、裴尧文、杜志林、林元宪、李彦实、严君锡、魏介然及予八人，因成拙诗，以纪一时之集云。<div id='poem_527766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_3_527766'>始知风景中原隔，对泣何须效楚囚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527766'></div><div id='poem_title_527654_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527654'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527654'>窜流今六载，无复望天朝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527654'>象魏阙云远，宝陀山匪遥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在琼州。有信与萧振。作品：与萧德起书。<div id='poem_1221101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与萧德起书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221101")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221101'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221101'>人生享全乐，孰如德起者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221101_comment'></div>六十之年，有此具美，无愧老莱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221101_comment'></div>不知前世作何大因缘，有此无量善报耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221101_comment'></div>某度岭海，首尾六年，惟书史可以自娱，此心不敢它用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221101_comment'></div>绍伊居相近，必时会合城中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221101_comment'></div>见诸友，望一一致意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221101_comment'></div>许厚之夫妇并亡，横伤之后，愈觉寂寥，天之报施，果何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221101_comment'></div>厚之贪嗜酒色，乃有取死之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221101_comment'></div>古宿云：「出世间法，乃大丈夫事，非将相所能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221101_comment'></div>惟公勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221101_comment'></div>某中间缘丧第三子，远乡无与开释，悲恼过当，遂至大病，几入鬼录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221101_comment'></div>踰年得安，始翻然感悟，今幸顽健如旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221101_comment'></div>某自离乡，朋友丧亡，如胡已茂、张全真，无虑数十人，多缘不能节省世缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221101_comment'></div>全真在会稽搜求妙丽，丹砂茸附，如啖鱼肉，徒资嗜欲耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221101_comment'></div>自谓享荣贵，得便宜，今为一丛枯骨，有甚便宜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221101_comment'></div>到这里，便世尊诸大菩萨出来，也救不得，岂不哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1221101_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年2月27日</a>　在琼州。与客至陈师正居所，退而赋诗。作品：丁卯二月二十七日，与客纵步至判官陈师正所居，前有花竹，后有港浦。爱其幽胜，退作此诗。师正历官九任，今年六十有一，母年九十二岁。杜门养亲，不复仕宦，盖琼士之安贫守道者也。<div id='poem_527769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527769?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁卯二月二十七日与客纵步至判官陈师正所居前有花竹后有港浦爱其幽胜退作此诗师正历官九任今年六十有一母年九十二岁杜门养亲不复仕宦盖琼士之安贫守道者也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年2月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527769")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527769'>幽居非是避危机，涩勒遮藏客到稀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527769'>白发不传毛义檄，青衫常戏老莱衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527769'>舟行别浦随潮去，燕认低檐带雨归。<div id='poem_527962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三月三日陪郡守宴严亭<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527962")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527962'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527962'>旌旆悠悠照暮春，兰亭修禊在斯晨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527962'>不须县尹前驱去，自有随车雨洗尘<span id='poem_sentence_2_527962_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527963?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年3月3日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527963'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527963'>寻花问柳到村扉，叶暗槟榔昼影移。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527963'>从此山翁频倒载，严池今胜习家池。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527963'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527963_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　在琼州。康元寿在郡圃植竹数百竿，中有小亭，曰通幽，李光成诗。作品：唐常建作破山寺诗，云‘竹径通幽处，禅房花木深。’欧阳永叔毎叹赏此句，以为不可及。温陵康元寿守琼，踰年乐其地僻而事简，以清静治之，于郡圃植竹数百竿，中有小亭，因榜曰通幽。偶成拙句。<div id='poem_527767' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527767' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527767?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐常建作破山寺诗云竹径通幽处禅房花木深欧阳永叔每叹赏此句以为不可及温陵康元寿守琼踰年乐其地僻而事简以清静治之于郡圃植竹数百竿中有小亭因榜曰通幽偶成拙句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527767")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527767_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527767'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527767'>萧洒襟怀慕子猷，剩栽修竹径通幽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527767'>三间远比渊明宅，百尺徒誇庾亮楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527767'>风送鸟声春寂寂，日筛帘影梦悠悠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527767'>破山绝景亲曾到，谁遣移来海外州<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527767'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527767'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_527767_0'>⑴ 原校：一云花露泣残春寂寂，鸟声惊断梦悠悠</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_527767_0'>⑵ ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年3月</a>　在琼州。暮春，与客宴野趣亭，有诗。作品：予自暮春与客燕野趣亭，俛仰三时，始复再至，则花木益茂，亭亦稍葺矣。因思去岁重九之集，览物增慨，题三小诗。<div id='poem_527956' class='_poem'><div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与潘子贱书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221100")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221100'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221100'>某顿首：孟坚行日，附状必已浼达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221100_comment'></div>元宵后有专介自婺女过，乃不令往请书，踰年不得公书，殊跂仰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221100_comment'></div>即日溽暑，伏惟台候起居佳胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221100_comment'></div>某自乙丑春渡海，今踰二年矣，幸且顽健。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221100_comment'></div>但老无超然之见，日复一日，年已从心，如舶船已离港汊入大洋，两军已交锋，生死劈面来，如何避得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221100_comment'></div>潘居士虽在酒色林中，十二时中亦要著便宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221100_comment'></div>其次夜半或五更睡，觉来燕坐定息，吐故纳新，舒眉引手，令稍倦再睡，此活计大不负人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221100_comment'></div>得正月十五日一报，圣主有宽大之意，囚锢之人皆起生还之望，此亦妄想耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527598'>二子俱可人，皎皎莹冰玉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527598'>初弹醉翁操，再鼓南风曲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527598'>琅然山水音，一洗瘴雾毒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527598'>陈园俯江郊，茅茨拥修竹。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527598'>造门慕子猷，缓步效颜斶。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527598'>汲泉瀹佳茗，萧散谢羁束。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527598'>清华临水岸，下有万荷绿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527598'>披榛访萧子，清净独无欲。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527598'>黎沈爇瓦鼎，溪荪养石斛<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：石昌蒲非九节者皆溪荪。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527598'>良辰不易遇，此会岂难续。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年2月3日</a>　在琼州。李光步至林氏园，又至了然道人小亭，逢魏安石，有诗。作品：己巳二月三日晚食罢，步至林氏园，了然道人新筑小亭，爱其閴寂，独坐久之，白上人来出门，又逢魏子，归而写之，以诗偶翻旧稿见之，恍然因书以示庭植。<div id='poem_528003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己巳二月三日晚食罢步至林氏园了然道人新筑小亭爱其阒寂独坐久之白上人来出门又逢魏子归而写之以诗偶翻旧藁见之恍然因书以示庭植二首<span class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528004?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年2月3日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_528004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528004'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528004'>夕照穿林暮霭收，出门忽见月如钩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528004'>幽人曳杖来寻伴，一笑能令万虑休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528004'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_528004_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　在琼州，与林庭植交游唱和有诗。作品：庭植家琼山水北小园，颇幽胜。予顷寓双泉，每食罢招邻士杖策访之，园有小亭，常与客对奕，因名坐隐。今岁亭侧辄生双竹，庭植二子皆卓然有立，岂造物者产此以瑞其家庭乎？作长句赠之。次林庭植喜雨韵。庭植惠雪菊严冬盛开。戏题林庭植茅亭。十月二十二日纵步至教谕谢君所居，爱其幽胜，而庭植、道源诸友见寻，烹茗奕棋小酌而归，因成二绝句。<div id='poem_527759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庭植家琼山水北小园颇幽胜予顷寓双泉每食罢招邻士杖策访之园有小亭常与客对奕因名坐隐今岁亭侧辄生双竹庭植二子皆卓然有立岂造物者产此以瑞其家庭乎作长句赠之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527759")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527759'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527759'>桃笙涩勒漫成林，并立林亭一径深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527759'>月下竞看双凤影，风来时听二龙吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527759'>冰霜不改夷齐操，富贵无忘鲁卫心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527759'>寄语园人频爱护，等闲莫遣斧斤侵<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527759'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年1月</a>　在琼州。究治李光撰私史事，送大理寺勘实。乃陆升之告发。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年3月19日</a>　在琼州。贬昌化军，永不检举。连坐者胡寅、程瑀、潘良贵、张焘、贺允中、吴元美、李孟坚八人皆降官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在琼州，上谢表。作品：上谢昌化军安置表。<div id='poem_1221070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>移昌化军安置谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221070")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221070'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221070'>十年远徙，犹冀生还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221070_comment'></div>三黜愈严，未知死所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221070_comment'></div>惊魂失据，危涕自零<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221070_comment'></div>伏念臣性实戆愚，老益顽鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221070_comment'></div>遭时遇主，妄有意于功名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221070_comment'></div>抱椠怀铅，本无称于翰墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221070_comment'></div>年齿衰晚，志气凋零，久杂处于黎蛮，唯归依于佛祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221070_comment'></div>每师蘧瑗，深悟己非；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221070_comment'></div>敢效郑人，妄议朝政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221070_comment'></div>而臣子孟坚，平居里巷，不择交游，怨咎横生，语言妄发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221070_comment'></div>纳官赎罪，罕逢国士之知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221070_comment'></div>下石反挤，近出乡人之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221070_comment'></div>仰恃神圣之眷，未加斧钺之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221070_comment'></div>恩重命轻，咎深责重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221070_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下体天地之大德，扩日月之盛明，怜臣尝冒近班，念臣频更繁使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221070_comment'></div>年同绛老，宜久辱于泥涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221070_comment'></div>罪比虞翻，盍永拘于海岛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221070_comment'></div>捐躯无路，没齿何言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221070_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1221070_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在琼州，游双泉。作品：双泉亭。<div id='poem_528006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>双泉亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_528006")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_528006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528006'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528006'>甃石流沟汲愈新，秋无落叶旱无尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528006'>他年莫忘痴顽老，曾是双泉旧主人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528006'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_528006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在琼州，有诗咏啄木鸟。作品：世以啄木为珍禽，其声至入乐府。而海南一种形小而声滛，每四五月间，飞鸣如蛙蝈，至八九月乃已，亦名啄木。繁声可恶，然琼人讹其声为骂，秃禽殆得其实，因为赋诗。<div id='poem_527599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>世以啄木为珍禽其声至入乐府而海南一种形小而声淫每四五月间飞鸣如蛙蝈至八九月乃已亦名啄木繁声可恶然琼人讹其声为骂秃禽殆得其实因为赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527599")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527599'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527599'>枝间时瞥见，黑啄羽毛绿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527599'>雌雄相应和，生哺依老谷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527599'>或疑在家僧，受施不看读。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527599'>为禽不知名，但自骂秃秃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527599'>小兵特轻趫，修竿每驰逐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527599'>今晨耳目清，桑下闻布谷。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在琼州，有诗吟琼连日阴雨。作品：予始到琼，众谓海南自来无大寒。今岁腊月，连日风雨，殆不异北地，因成小诗记之。<div id='poem_527651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予始到琼众谓海南自来无大寒今岁腊月连日风雨殆不异北地因成小诗记之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在琼州，赋吟琼台。<div id='poem_527758' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527758' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_note_527758_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在琼州，有诗题将领战胜亭。作品：题将领占胜亭，亭据双泉之上，尽见城东南风物之胜，落成之初，屡来乞诗，为赋长句云。<div id='poem_527764' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527764' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527764?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题将领占胜亭亭据双泉之上尽见城东南风物之胜落成之初屡来乞诗为赋长句云</a><span id='poem_sentence_1_527937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527937'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote'
