class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1156')">1150-1156年</a>，73-79岁</div><div id='eb17ddd4a1fb4a728d1d2be3f9cc93fa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。李光贬昌化军，魏安石等远送至儋耳，李光有诗。作品：庚午春，予得罪再贬昌化，琼士饯送者皆怅然，有不忍别之意。严君锡、魏介然追路至儋耳，兹事当求之古人，感叹成古风二首送行。<div id='poem_527603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚午春予得罪再贬昌化琼士饯送者皆怅然有不忍别之意严君锡魏介然追路至儋耳兹事当求之古人感叹成古风二百言<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>送行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527603")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527603_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_527603_0'>① 二字原作首，据院本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527603'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527603'>绍兴庚午春，李子复南徙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527603'>仓皇就长途，夜担不敢弛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527603'>饯我无杂宾，亦有方外士。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527603'>裴杜二耆哲，矍铄浑童稚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527603'>老禅不忍别，握手挥涕泪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527603'>行行至澄迈，名姓难尽纪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527603'>酒酣通湖阁，颇获一笑喜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527603'>缅怀双泉居，风土信清美。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527603'>床头挂海月，枕上听流水。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527603'>夜棋招隐沦，浊酒会邻里。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527603'>桑下不三宿，怅恋吾过矣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527603'>人生随遇乐，已过犹脱屣。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527603'>最怜严与魏，触热到儋耳。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527603'>世情逐炎凉，万古同一轨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527603'>对境心数役，何以敌生死。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527603'>南窗可寄傲，散帙忽盈几。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527603'>松林十里间，移植颇易致。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527603'>赫日资繁阴，且复宥老楮。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527603'>夜凉得深禅，日永常晚起。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_527603'>恨君不少留，伴我读书史<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_527603'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_527603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527603'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_527603_0'>⑴ 自注：寓多老谷，方暑，藉其繁阴，不忍伐去。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527603_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。李光贬昌化军，魏安石等远送至儋耳，李光有诗言及杜介之。作品：琼惟水东，林木幽茂，予爱此三士所居，虽无亭馆之胜，而气象清远，连日水涨隔绝，悠然遐想，各成一诗，目为“城东三咏”<div id='poem_527593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>琼惟水东林木幽茂予爱此三士所居虽无亭馆之胜而气象清远连日水涨隔绝悠然遐想各成一诗目为城东三咏<span class='inlineComment2'>（原按：今存二首。）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>杜公司法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527593")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527593'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527593'>南极多老人，及见九代孙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527593'>君生古崖州，气质清且温。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527593'>今年八十二，颇觉行步奔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527593'>白发映红颊，疑是羲皇人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527593'>城东有幽居，潇洒真隐沦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527593'>渊明寓栗里，子美还羌村。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527593'>迁流到双泉，得与君子邻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527593'>仁里圣所择，德齿古所尊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527593'>佳节近重阳，黄花已纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527593'>家家社酒香，处处烹鸡豚。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527593'>今朝风日好，水落依旧痕。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527593'>一散腰脚顽，杖策时叩门。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527593'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_527593_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527594?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>林曾城</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527594'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527594'>我爱曾城居，负郭颇幽雅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527594'>田畴绕屋庐，门径绝车马。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527594'>但虞水侵门，敢怨风飘瓦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527594'>渊明非避俗，自觉往来寡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527594'>嗟予屏斥久，兹地犹里社。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527594'>相望十里间，舟楫幸可假。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527594'>风休水亦落，晴日照郊野。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527594'>愿言驾柴车，始觉我忧写。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527594'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。寻访苏东坡旧游之地，得东坡载酒堂诗真本，有诗赋咏。作品：绍圣中，苏公内翰谪居儋耳，尝与军使张中游黎氏园。爱其水木之胜，劝坐客醵钱作堂，黎氏名子云，因用扬雄故事名其堂曰载酒。予始至儋，与琼士魏安石杖策访之，退作二诗。<div id='poem_527605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绍圣中苏公内翰谪居儋耳尝与军使张中游黎氏园爱其水木之胜劝坐客醵钱作堂黎氏名子云因用扬雄故事名其堂曰载酒予始至儋与琼士魏安石杖策访之退作二诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：实存一首）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527605")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527605'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527605'>何年老扬雄，寄此十亩园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527605'>年深草木荒，杖策谁叩门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527605'>缅怀东坡老，陈迹记旧痕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527605'>空馀载酒堂，往事孰与论。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527605'>黄柑与丹荔，不受瘴雾昏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527605'>邦人时馈奠，一笑空罍尊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527605'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_527605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。寻访苏东坡旧游之地，得东坡载酒堂诗真本，有诗追和东坡。作品：东坡载酒堂二诗，盖用渊明《始春怀古田舍》韵，遂不见于后集，予至儋始得真本，因追和其韵。<div id='poem_527606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东坡载酒堂二诗盖用渊明始春怀古田舍韵遂不见于后集予至儋始得真本因追和其韵<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527606")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527606'>平泉与金谷，视此颜有腼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527607'>藷芋饷昼耕，松明照夜勤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527607'>当年两黎老，能邀玉堂人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527607'>一往五十年，遗迹宛若新。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527607'>邦君时举酒，父老举欣欣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_note_527607_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。寻访苏东坡旧游之地，有诗赋咏载酒堂。<div id='poem_527630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>载酒堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527630")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527630'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527630'>东坡文章喧宇宙，粲如日星垂不朽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527630'>六一老人犹避路，作者纷纷皆束手<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527630'>俊逸精神追李杜，华妙雄豪配韩柳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527630'>晚年流落海南村，黎唱蛮讴随蜑叟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527630'>先生已去五十年，遗墨残篇尚多有。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527630'>败垣坏壁秘蜗涎，夭矫龙蛇已惊走<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527630'>杖藜乘兴访遗像，遐想英风伫立久。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527630'>曾吹葱叶送迎翁，当日儿童今白首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527630'>莫嗟寂寂路荒芜，亦有幽人时载酒<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《庄简集》卷二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527630'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_527630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527630'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527630_0'>⑴ 自注：欧公见东坡文叹曰：老夫当避路，放他出一头地也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_527630_0'>⑵ 自注：东坡真迹多为有力者取去，所存但摹本耳。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_527630_0'>⑶ 自注：子云之子今六十馀矣，东坡所谓小童，即此人也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527630_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。春，有诗感于叛乱实缘于赃吏。作品：海外谣。<div id='poem_527604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海外谣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527604")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527604'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527604'>嗟尔海南民，遭此赃吏阨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527604'>衔冤无所诉，相炽起为贼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527604'>为贼计诚拙，尚可活朝夕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527604'>摄官陈建中，贪猥最狼藉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527604'>有女攀势要，不料非偶匹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527604'>但务<span class='inlineComment2'>（院本作矜）</span>房奁多，苞苴又络绎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527604'>挟此恣贪惏，如虎傅以翼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527604'>贰车号按察，往诉遭箠击。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527604'>其次经界官，太守乃姻戚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527604'>郡县遭唾骂，图册成覆易<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527604'>三豪因众怒，从者如苇棘。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527604'>去年从说谕，闾里已帖息。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527604'>狂谋起赇吏，从此复反侧。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527604'>愚民本无知，胁诱冒锋镝。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527604'>焚荡玉石俱，老弱转沟洫。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_527604'>遗骸横道路，流血千里赤。<div id='poem_sentence_19_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_527604'>沉香与翠羽，穷搜远弹射。<div id='poem_sentence_22_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_527604'>祖宗有成法，赃吏盍杖脊。<div id='poem_sentence_25_527604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年8月1日</a>　李光在昌化军。王趯停官，坐与李光、赵鼎交往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年8月15日</a>　在昌化。“昌化郡城之北，长桥跨江，风月之夕，气象甚胜。庚午八月望夜，士友悉赴郡会。杖策独游，颇怀平生故人，作《水调》歌以自释。予自长年，粗闻养生之术。放逐以来，又得司马子微叙王屋山清虚洞所刻《坐忘论》一编，因得专意宴坐，心息相依。虽不敢仰希乔松之寿，度未即死，庶有会合之期“作品：水调歌头（独步长桥上）<div id='poem_117767' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_117767' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/117767?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>昌化郡长桥词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_117767")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_117767_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_117767'>昌化郡城之北，长桥跨江，风月之夕，气象甚胜。庚午八月望夜，士友悉赴郡会。杖策独游，颇怀平生故人，作水调歌以自释。予自长年，粗闻养生之术。放逐以来，又得司马子微叙王屋山清虚洞所刻坐忘论一编，因得专意宴坐，心息相依。虽不敢仰希乔松之寿，度未即死，庶有会合之期。</div><div id='poem_preface_117767_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_117767'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_117767'>独步长桥上，今夕是中秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_117767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_117767'>群黎怪我何事，流转古儋州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_117767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_117767'>风定潮平如练，云散月明如昼，孤兴在扁舟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_117767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_117767'>笑尽一杯酒，水调杂蛮讴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_117767_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_117767'>少年场，金兰契，尽白头。<div id='poem_sentence_4_117767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_117767'>相望万里，悲我已是十年流。<div id='poem_sentence_5_117767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_117767'>晚遇玉霄仙子，授我王屋奇书，归路指蓬丘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_117767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_117767'>不用乘风御，八极可神游。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_117767_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年9月9日</a>　在昌化军。至陈氏水阁，有诗。作品：庚午重九，予以忧患经此节物，亦强举杯，复同坐客。步至陈氏水阁，率尔成韵。<div id='poem_527792' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527792' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527792?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚午重九予以忧患经此节物亦强举杯复同坐客步至陈氏水阁率尔成韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527792")'>李光</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_0_527792'>累岁严亭会众宾，今年九日未全贫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527792'>樽中有酒须招客，篱外无花免笑人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527792'>竹杖芒鞋行自惯，风轩水阁坐来频。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527792'>鬓边强把茱萸插，万里谁嗟老病身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527792'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527792'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527792_0'>⑴ ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。有书与胡铨游。作品：与胡邦衡书两篇。<div id='poem_1221126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与胡邦衡书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_1221126")'>李光</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221126'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221126'>某咨目上启：秋暑异常，伏惟卫生有道，台候起居佳胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221126_comment'></div>某旋得省劄，大理具狱，儿子窜峡州，永不检举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221126_comment'></div>父子蹈此大祸，固无可言，而累及平生知友，如张焘、程瑀二尚书、潘良贵舍人各降三官<span class='inlineComment2'>（坐尝通书。）</span>，胡寅侍郎镌职<span class='inlineComment2'>（坐通书扇摇经略。）</span>，馀人贺、许二郎官凡五六人各降两官，使人不能不怅然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221126_comment'></div>诸友自知无益，各已相忘久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221126_comment'></div>架空造此，不知其因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221126_comment'></div>盖此数人一向投閒，此其罪也，置之勿复道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221126_comment'></div>连日忧愤，无与晤语，领来书，启缄快读，信如执热之濯清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221126_comment'></div>佳篇乃未尝得见苏、李句，此句法则工，而拟非其伦，则不敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221126_comment'></div>三序须俟神閒志定，今未暇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221126_comment'></div>然骫骳之文，岂足发扬妙趣，以传示后来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221126_comment'></div>闻命愧惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221126_comment'></div>令郎气象未易量，仆孙女多，俟公还朝，未免当择一端谨以配君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221126_comment'></div>长儿女子乙卯生，已非偶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221126_comment'></div>亭午汗方浃背，勉作此纸，阅毕则付丙丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221126_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221126_comment'></div>某咨目上启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1221126_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年9月11日</a>　坐与李光交结，吴元美容州编管。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。冬，跋碧虚子纂经。<div id='poem_1221169' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221169' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221169?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋碧虚子纂经</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1221169'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221169'>庚午冬至后四日再阅一过，碧虚子何人，出入儒释道三教，可谓博达之士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221169_comment'></div>自念平生交友未见其人，其方外之士，道家者流乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221169_comment'></div>异时见潘子，当质之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1221169_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在昌化军。有六无诗。作品：食无肉。居无屋。<div id='poem_527609' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27356, "宋", "李光", "poem_title_527609")'>李光</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_0_527609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527609'>十年岭海游，一钵随僧粥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527609'>空肠无滓秽，气转声漉漉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527609'>腥膻减吾寿，厚味有腊毒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527609'>颜回称好学，陋巷一瓢足。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527610'>华榱庇千间，子孙无托足。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527610'>海南吾欲老，是处堪卜筑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527610'>野老日往来，席地有<span class='inlineComment2'>（院本作布）</span>棋局。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221170'>昨所言《维摩经》，字画精妙，仆所宝藏，今以遗荆华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221170_comment'></div>海外不知佛法，公能留意于此，日诵一卷，以岁计之，当得百馀卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221170_comment'></div>异时此邦之人薰染成熟，悟真如之性，造无生之理，当自荆华始，可不勉哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221170_comment'></div>绍兴辛未五月十一日，无碍居士。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1221170_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　旧识吴由道来昌化，索梅花诗，李光次韵三首。作品：戊辰冬，与邻士纵步至吴由道书会所课诸生，作梅花诗，以先字为韵，戏成一绝句。后三年，由道来昌化索前作，复次韵三首，并前诗赠之。<div id='poem_528028' class='_poem'><div
